# Roadmap

Pyde's path from design-complete to mainnet, structured as **five phases (MC-0 through MC-5)** with **three parallel implementation streams** in the core phase (MC-1). Each phase ships when its bar is met ‚Äî no calendar dates.

Coordination details (crate ownership, branching protocol, interface contracts, session handoff prompts for the three streams) live in [`companion/IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md`](companion/IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md). Read that first if you're implementing.

**Legend:**
- `[SEQ]` ‚Äî sequential (must complete before the next phase starts)
- `[PAR]` ‚Äî parallel (can run concurrently with siblings)
- `‚Üí` ‚Äî explicit dependency
- `Œ±` / `Œ≤` / `Œ≥` ‚Äî owning implementation stream (see `IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md` ¬ß4)

---

## Top-level shape

```
MC-0  INTERFACE FOUNDATION              [SEQ ‚Äî main session]
  ‚îÇ   Create engine repo, lock types + interfaces crates, CI baseline.
  ‚îÇ   This is the prerequisite that makes parallelism safe.
  ‚ñº
MC-1  PROTOCOL CORE                     [PAR ‚Äî three streams]
  ‚îÇ   Stream Œ± (Toolchain)   in pyde-net/otigen
  ‚îÇ   Stream Œ≤ (Execution)   in pyde-net/engine on `execution-side` branch
  ‚îÇ   Stream Œ≥ (Consensus)   in pyde-net/engine on `consensus-side` branch
  ‚ñº
MC-2  INTEGRATION                       [SEQ ‚Äî Œ≥ owns]
  ‚îÇ   Merge Œ≤ + Œ≥ branches; bring up local devnet end-to-end.
  ‚ñº
MC-3  STATE SYNC + PARACHAIN ACTIVATION [SEQ ‚Äî Œ≤ + Œ≥ joint]
  ‚îÇ   Snapshot machinery, weak-subjectivity, parachain framework live.
  ‚ñº
MC-4  PERFORMANCE + FAILURE HANDLING    [PAR within]
  ‚îÇ   Performance harness, chaos drills, soak.
  ‚ñº
MC-5  VALIDATION + MAINNET LAUNCH       [SEQ]
      External audits, incentivized testnet, mainnet.
```

Old MC-1 through MC-7 numbering (pre-2026-05-23) collapses into this shape: old MC-1 + MC-2 ‚Üí MC-0 + MC-1; old MC-3 ‚Üí folded into Stream Œ±; old MC-4 ‚Üí folded into MC-3; old MC-5 ‚Üí MC-3; old MC-6 ‚Üí MC-4; old MC-7 ‚Üí MC-5.

---

## MC-0 ‚Äî INTERFACE FOUNDATION `[SEQ]` ‚Äî main session ‚úÖ shipped

The sequential prerequisite to parallelism. Without MC-0 complete, streams Œ≤ and Œ≥ clash on shared types and interface drift. ~1 day of focused work; the main session owns it.

Tagged `phase-0-foundation` on `main` at `pyde-net/engine`. 92 unit/integration tests pass; `cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -- -D warnings` clean; `cargo fmt --all -- --check` clean.

### 0.1 Engine repo creation

- [x] Create `pyde-net/engine` repo on GitHub (fresh; post-pivot)
- [x] Clone locally at `/pyde-net/engine/`
- [x] Initial commit: README + LICENSE (Apache-2.0) + `.gitignore` + `SECURITY.md` + `rust-toolchain.toml`

### 0.2 Workspace skeleton

- [x] `Cargo.toml` workspace with every crate stubbed:
  - `types`, `interfaces`
  - `account`, `state`, `tx`, `wasm-exec`, `mempool` (Œ≤-owned)
  - `consensus`, `net`, `dkg`, `slashing`, `node` (Œ≥-owned)
- [x] Each crate stub: `Cargo.toml` + `src/lib.rs` with a placeholder function so the workspace compiles (node also has `src/main.rs` for the `pyde` binary)

### 0.3 `types` crate (frozen at end of MC-0)

- [x] `Address` ([u8; 32]) ‚Äî full Poseidon2, no truncation
- [x] `SlotHash`, `Value` (state primitives)
- [x] `Balance` (u128), `Nonce` (u64), `NonceWindow` (16-slot bitmap)
- [x] `Tx` flat envelope + `TxType` discriminant (Ch 11 ¬ß11.6 wire format; tag 2 reserved-as-vacant)
- [x] `TxHash`, `Receipt`, `ReceiptStatus`, `FeePayer`, `AccessEntry`, `AccessType`
- [x] `StateRoot` (dual: Blake3 + Poseidon2)
- [x] `EventRecord` (with `wave_id` / `tx_index` / `event_index` primary key + `Vec<Topic>` for multi-topic v1) + `EventCursor` for `pyde_getLogs` pagination
- [x] `WaveId` (u64), `Round` (u64), `CommitId` (= WaveId)
- [x] `VertexHash`, `BatchHash`, `BatchRef`, `Vertex` (with `member_id` + `batch_refs` + `decryption_shares` per Ch 6 ¬ß3) + `Batch` (network gossip type)
- [x] `WaveCommitRecord` (with `anchor_round` / `prior_anchor_round` / `events_root` / `events_bloom` / `events_count` / `tx_count` / `gas_used: u128`)
- [x] `HardFinalityCert` with 85-of-128 quorum check
- [x] `FalconPubkey` (897 B fixed), `FalconSignature` (variable, ‚â§690 B cap)
- [x] `EventsBloom` ‚Äî spec-aligned algorithm: 256 B / 3 hashes / `blake3(item)[..8/8..16/16..24]` mod 2048 (consumer-side blake3 ‚Äî leaf-dep invariant preserved)
- [x] `ContractAbi` per HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß3.7: `pyde_abi_version: u32`, `contract_type`, `state_schema_hash`, `constructor_index` / `fallback_index` / `receive_index` + `EventAbi` extension for ¬ß14.1 event signatures
- [x] `FunctionAttrs` (u32 bitfield: VIEW / PAYABLE / REENTRANT / SPONSORED / CONSTRUCTOR / FALLBACK / RECEIVE / ENTRY)
- [x] Error codes from `HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß4` ‚Äî `ERR_*` consts + typed `ErrorCode` enum (i32 wire format; round-trips via `as_i32` / `from_i32`)
- [x] `AuthKeys` (None / Single / MultiSig / Programmable-reserved at tag `0x03`) with `MAX_MULTISIG_SIGNERS = 16` and structural validation
- [x] 81 unit + property tests including wire-tag verification and field-order pin tests

### 0.4 `interfaces` crate (frozen at end of MC-0)

- [x] `trait StateView` ‚Äî async; balance / nonce_window / slot / code_hash / code / account_type / auth_keys / state_root
- [x] `trait StateMutator: StateView` ‚Äî async; `commit_wave(wave_id, txs)` ‚Üí `WaveCommitRecord`, `rollback_wave`, `snapshot` ‚Üí `SnapshotHandle`
- [x] `trait Executor` ‚Äî async; `execute_tx(state, tx, gas_limit)` + `view_call(state, target, data)`
- [x] `trait MempoolView` ‚Äî async; insert / drain_for_batch / contains / fetch_by_hash / pending_count
- [x] `trait NetworkView` ‚Äî async; publish_vertex / publish_batch / fetch_vertex / fetch_batch (libp2p gossip surface)
- [x] `trait ConsensusEngine` ‚Äî async; current_round / current_wave / get_finality_cert (read-only observation surface)
- [x] `InterfaceError` ‚Äî boundary error enum with retryability classification
- [x] `mod mock` ‚Äî `MockState` / `MockExecutor` / `MockMempool` / `MockNetwork` / `MockConsensus`, 11 tests each exercising at least one trait method per impl

### 0.5 CI + branching

- [x] `.github/workflows/ci.yml` running fmt + clippy (-D warnings) + test + doc on every PR with target/registry caching
- [x] Long-lived branches created: `execution-side` (Œ≤), `consensus-side` (Œ≥)
- [x] Tag `phase-0-foundation` on `main`

### 0.6 IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN cross-link

- [x] `pyde-book/src/companion/IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md` already current
- [x] Cross-linked from this roadmap

**MC-0 BAR:** ‚úÖ engine repo exists with all 12 crate stubs compiling; `types` + `interfaces` crates fully written and tested (92 tests, all green); CI green; branching protocol established; `IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md` committed.

---

## MC-1 ‚Äî PROTOCOL CORE `[PAR ‚Äî three streams] ‚Üí MC-0`

The core protocol implementation. Three streams run in parallel: Œ± (toolchain), Œ≤ (execution), Œ≥ (consensus). Each owns disjoint crates per the ownership map in [`IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md ¬ß4`](companion/IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md). The session-handoff prompts for each stream are in [`IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md ¬ß7`](companion/IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md).

### MC-1 Stream Œ± ‚Äî Toolchain `[SEQ within Œ±] ‚Üí MC-0` ‚Äî repo `pyde-net/otigen`

Implements [`OTIGEN_BINARY_SPEC.md`](companion/OTIGEN_BINARY_SPEC.md).

#### Œ±.feat ‚Äî Feature surface (spec ¬ß3 + ¬ß9 + supporting crates)

- [x] `pyde-net/otigen` repo + Rust workspace
- [x] `otigen-toml`: config parser + schema validation (spec ¬ß4)
- [x] `otigen-abi`: `ContractAbi` construction + Borsh encoding + custom-section injection via `wasm-encoder` (spec ¬ß6)
- [x] `otigen-cli`: subcommand framework via `clap` (spec ¬ß3)
- [x] `otigen build`: full validation pipeline (spec ¬ß3.2 step-by-step)
- [x] `otigen-wallet`: keystore (Argon2id + AES-256-GCM, single-file multi-account per spec ¬ß7.1), FALCON-512 signing, secret-key zeroisation on drop ‚Äî ported from archived `wright` repo
- [x] `otigen wallet new` / `import` / `list` / `show` / `delete` / `password` ‚Äî single-file `~/.pyde/keystore.json` (override via `--keystore`), confirmation prompt before destructive ops, NDJSON event stream under `--json`
- [x] `otigen-rpc`: JSON-RPC client per Ch 17.4 ‚Äî sync `reqwest::blocking` `Client` + 15 typed method wrappers (account / call / send / receipt / gas / wave / logs / snapshot), typed error envelope, wiremock-driven e2e tests. WebSocket subscriptions deferred to v2.
- [x] `otigen deploy` ‚Äî full ¬ß3.3 pipeline (bundle ‚Üí re-validate ‚Üí resolve network + wallet ‚Üí fetch nonce ‚Üí build canonical tx ‚Üí FALCON-sign ‚Üí `pyde_sendRawTransaction` ‚Üí poll receipt). `--dry-run` for offline inspection, `--no-wait` for fire-and-forget scripts. Wire format (`Tx` envelope + `TxType` / `FeePayer` / `AccessType` discriminant tags + canonical Poseidon2 hash) pinned to Ch 11 ¬ß11.6 / ¬ß11.8 / ¬ß"Transaction hash" on the toolchain side until Stream Œ≤'s `tx` crate lifts beyond its current scaffold.
- [x] `otigen upgrade` / `pause` / `unpause` / `kill` ‚Äî shared lifecycle pipeline via `TxType::Standard` with `data = borsh(LifecyclePayload)`. Name-or-address targeting (auto-resolves via `pyde_resolveName`). `kill --yes` skips the retype-the-target confirmation. `LifecyclePayload` discriminants (0x00..=0x03) pinned to spec ¬ß8.3 until Stream Œ≤'s `tx` crate formalises.
- [x] `otigen inspect` ‚Äî read-only metadata + state via the rpc client (`pyde_getAccount` + `pyde_getContractCode`). `--field <name>` queries `Poseidon2(name)`-derived storage slots; `--at-wave <id>` forwarded for archive nodes (v1 RPC catalog surfaces current state with a notice).
- [x] `otigen verify` ‚Äî reproducible-build check (spec ¬ß3.9). Compares local bundle's `contract.wasm` against chain-stored bytes via `pyde_getContractCode`, surfaces blake3 hashes + size delta + first-diff offset on mismatch. Fail-fast: local checks before RPC.
- [x] Canonical example contracts: Rust ‚úÖ, AssemblyScript ‚úÖ, Go (TinyGo) ‚úÖ, C/C++ ‚úÖ ‚Äî all four `otigen init --lang X` templates render valid hello-world projects with a `ping` entry point + commented host-fn import example. Rust end-to-end (init ‚Üí build ‚Üí bundle) exercised by `tests/hello_rust_e2e.rs`; AS/Go/C source‚Üíwasm compilation deferred to per-language external toolchains (`asc` / `tinygo` / `clang --target=wasm32`). Init's "next:" message picks the right build command per language.
- [x] **simple-multisig example + FALCON-512 `falcon_verify` runner mock + `bytes` typed-arg** ‚Äî canonical 3-signer multisig demonstrating in-contract post-quantum signature verification. Runner gains: `falcon_verify` mock via `pyde_crypto::falcon` (real PQ verification at test time; sigs round-trip to chain); Phase 4 `bytes` typed-arg (variable-length blobs; each `bytes` expands to 2 wasm i32 params: ptr + len); `[accounts].keypair = "falcon512"` + three DSL prefixes (`@pubkey:NAME`, `@sig:NAME:args.IDX`, `@pubkey_hash:NAME`) so test authors never hand-paste kilobyte FALCON blobs. Adjacent fixes: `host_transfer` mock now debits `env.contract_address` (matches `HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß7.2`), event matcher handles `bytes32` indexed fields. `make verify-examples`: 6/6 builds, 31/31 test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#54](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/54) + docs [pyde-book#124](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/124)
- [x] **upgradeable-proxy example + delegate_call runner mock** ‚Äî canonical Pyde upgradeable-proxy pattern: admin-controlled implementation pointer + pyde::delegate_call to swap behaviour without touching storage. Runner gains delegate_call mock that re-enters the same Instance at a named export with (calldata_ptr, calldata_len) shape, preserving the caller storage context per HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß7.8. v1 limitation: target must equal self_address (single-wasm); multi-contract delegate is on the roadmap. TestEnv.instance cached at setup so host fns that re-enter wasm can look up named exports. make verify-examples: 7/7 builds, 38/38 test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#55](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/55) + docs landed alongside on pyde-book/main
- [x] **counter-token ports to TinyGo / AssemblyScript / C** ‚Äî three new examples (counter-token-go, counter-token-as, counter-token-c) porting the canonical Rust counter-token to the remaining wasm32 target languages otigen supports. Same 5 entry points, same Blake3 event topic-0 constants, same u128 BE-in-upper-16-bytes encoding, identical TOML test suite copied verbatim into each ports tests/. The contract pyde.abi custom section hashes byte-identical across all four ports (blake3 0617b1d55b725b5d) ‚Äî proving the test framework is language-agnostic by design. Sizes: Rust 1.5 KB, AS 3.1 KB, C 3.3 KB, TinyGo 65 KB. make verify-examples: 10/10 builds, 59/59 test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#56](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/56)
- [x] **Examples catalog page in pyde-book** (otigen/examples.md) ‚Äî single-table index of all 11 canonical examples (counter-{rust,go,as,c}, counter-token-{rust,go,as,c}, erc20-token, simple-multisig, upgradeable-proxy) with language, test count, host fns exercised, GitHub link. Backfills the two previously-unreferenced examples (erc20-token in WASM_AUTHOR_GUIDE ¬ß7.6; counter-token Go/AS/C ports in ¬ß14) so every example is reachable from at least one named book section. Closes discoverability gap pre-Alliance-DAO. ‚Äî PR [pyde-book#136](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/136)
- [x] **Runner multi-contract support + cross_call mock + counter-pair canonical example** ‚Äî [[contracts]] block in test TOML lets a test deploy multiple contracts at distinct canonical addresses in the same Store. host_cross_call mock: target lookup, snapshot/rollback, value transfer (debits caller + credits target), context switch (caller / contract_address / instance / scratch_base / tx_value), copies calldata across separate linear memories, invokes named export with (calldata_ptr, calldata_len) -> i32, restores. Sub-call trap rolls back state + returns ERR_CROSS_CALL_FAILED (-8) ‚Äî parent doesnt trap. counter-pair-a + counter-pair-b example exercises all four ¬ß7.8 invariants (storage isolation, caller() shift, value transfer, revert rollback) in a 6-test suite. Docs: WASM_AUTHOR_GUIDE ¬ß8.5, OTIGEN_TEST_SPEC ¬ß4.7 / ¬ß6.3, examples catalog. make verify-examples: 11/11 builds, 71/71 test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#57](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/57) (runner) + PR [otigen#58](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/58) (example) + docs [pyde-book#143](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/143)
- [x] **Parachain host fn mocks + profile-registry example** ‚Äî runner now mocks 6 of 9 ¬ß8 parachain host fns (parachain_storage_{read,write,delete}, parachain_id, parachain_version, parachain_emit_event). TestEnv gains parachain_storage BTreeMap (variable-length-keyed, namespaced by parachain address) + parachain_version u32. profile-registry canonical parachain example (type=parachain in otigen.toml, 1.5 KB wasm) exercises all 6 fns through 7 behaviour tests covering: variable-length blob round-trip, distinct-user isolation, overwrite (not append), delete+event, parachain_id matches Poseidon2 derivation, large-blob round-trip. Spec-conformance fix bundled: ERR_SIGNATURE_INVALID = -17 + ERR_CROSS_CALL_FAILED = -10 (were both -8 ‚Äî drift from PRs 11/15b). Deferred to later: send_xparachain_message (multi-parachain harness), threshold_{encrypt,decrypt} (DKG state). make verify-examples: 12/12 builds, all test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#59](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/59) (constants fix) + PR [otigen#60](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/60) (mocks) + PR [otigen#61](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/61) (example) + docs [pyde-book#147](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/147) + [pyde-book#150](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/150)
- [x] **erc721-token canonical NFT example** ‚Äî closes the obvious gap (we had ERC20 but no non-fungible counterpart). Per-token ownership (one slot per token, uint64-keyed), balance_of secondary index, single-spender per-token approval cleared atomically on transfer_from. Demonstrates three-topic indexed events (Transfer/Approval each carry from + to + token_id as indexed ‚Äî bumps into ¬ß7.5 4-topic max). 10 behaviour tests covering mint, distinct-IDs, transfer + balances, non-owner revert, approve + transfer_from + atomic approval clear, no-approval revert, wrong-from-arg revert, non-owner approve revert, nonexistent-token revert, owner-as-self-spender. make verify-examples: 13/13 builds, all test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#62](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/62) + docs [pyde-book#154](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/154)
- [x] **merkle-claim-airdrop canonical example** ‚Äî closes the hash-host-fn use-case gap (we had `hash_blake3` wired in the runner from the PR 11 batch but no example demonstrating it). Off-chain commitment + on-chain inclusion verification: commits a (claimant, amount) allocation set as a single 32-byte merkle root, claimants present a path that hashes back via per-step `hash_blake3` calls. Domain-separated leaf vs node hashing (RFC-9162 style), 33-byte/step proof encoding (1 position byte + 32 sibling), one-shot init pattern with separate root_set flag. 10 behaviour tests covering happy path + all-four-claim + double-claim revert + unset-root revert + second-set-root revert + non-eligible revert + wrong-amount revert + garbage-proof revert + malformed-length revert + unclaimed-default-zero. Also demonstrates variable-length `bytes` typed-arg marshalling (proof = ptr+len pair). make verify-examples: 14/14 builds, all test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#63](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/63) + docs [pyde-book#158](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/158)
- [x] **vesting canonical example** ‚Äî surfaces the `block_timestamp` host fn we hadn't demoed yet. Linear-vesting-with-cliff contract: configure(beneficiary, total, start, cliff, duration) once at deploy, permissionless `release()` pays `vested - released` to the beneficiary over time. Linear-from-start with cliff delay (matches OpenZeppelin VestingWallet semantics). Time-travel in tests via per-test `[tests.cheats].now` overrides. u128-promotion math is overflow-safe up to total √ó 2^64 ‚Äî far past realistic vesting setups. 10 behaviour tests covering configure-readback, pre-cliff revert, at-cliff proportional, mid-vesting half, after-duration full + double-release revert, double-configure revert, release-before-configure revert, non-beneficiary-poke (anyone-can-call), zero-duration degenerate, released+releasable invariants. make verify-examples: 15/15 builds, all test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#64](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/64) + docs [pyde-book#161](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/161) ‚Äî **Note (2026-05-28):** the `block_timestamp` host fn was renamed to `wave_timestamp` in [otigen#69](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/69) + [engine#151](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/151); the live example now imports `wave_timestamp` (semantically identical, name aligned with the rest of the consensus surface).
- [x] **WASM_AUTHOR_GUIDE ¬ß11 ‚Äî Hash-based commitments and Merkle proofs** ‚Äî new 200-line author-guide chapter closing the docs gap noted in PR 18b (the merkle-claim-airdrop example landed with a catalog entry but no surrounding pattern guide). Subsections: ¬ß11.1 the three hash host fns + when to use each (blake3 performance / poseidon2 ZK-friendly / keccak256 cross-chain-only), ¬ß11.2 domain separation (why prepend a tag, second-preimage attack mechanics, RFC 9162 reference), ¬ß11.3 off-chain tree construction with diagram + ordering / odd-level rules, ¬ß11.4 proof encoding (33-byte/step rationale, alternatives evaluated), ¬ß11.5 full on-chain verification loop with caller-binding safety, ¬ß11.6 five concrete pitfalls (sibling ordering, address-as-ASCII, length checks, caller vs arg, cross-protocol reuse), ¬ß11.7 pointer to live example. Renumbers former ¬ß11-14 ‚Üí ¬ß12-15 (verified clean of external section refs). References gain merkle-claim-airdrop + RFC 9162. ‚Äî PR [pyde-book#164](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/164)
- [x] **dao-governance composed canonical example** ‚Äî the marquee example for v1: composition of FALCON-signed votes + time-phased state machine + composite-key per-proposal storage + hash_blake3 calldata commitment + self_address-domain-separated canonical message. Demonstrates how the v1 primitives stack into a production-shape governance pattern. Lifecycle: init (one-shot 3-signer setup) ‚Üí propose (anyone, returns monotonic id) ‚Üí cast_signed_vote (off-chain FALCON sig, on-chain verify, anyone can submit ‚Äî gasless voting via relayer) ‚Üí execute (post-deadline, requires quorum + majority + calldata-hash match). 15 behaviour tests covering init flow, propose flow, alice happy-path yes-vote, quorum met, tampered-message revert, unknown-signer + invalid-pubkey-length + double-vote + after-deadline + zero-duration + below-quorum + unknown-proposal + vote-on-unknown reverts. Out of scope: cross_call dispatch (pattern in counter-pair-a), vote weighting (= 1 per signer), cancel/queue/time-lock. make verify-examples: 16/16 builds, all test cases green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#65](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/65) + docs [pyde-book#168](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/168)
- [x] **Per-call cheat overrides** (`now` / `wave_id` / `chain_id`) with **sticky semantics** in otigen-test ‚Äî closes the time-travel-within-a-test limitation surfaced by dao-governance (PR 21). Each `[[tests.calls]]` entry can now set its own clock; once set, the value persists into subsequent calls until another override fires (matches a real chain's monotonically-advancing clock). Implementation: add fields to `TestCall` + `ResolvedCall`, apply to `TestEnv` before dispatch ‚Äî ~30 lines runner + 6 test fixtures updated, no behaviour change for tests that don't use the new fields. Unlocks: dao-governance gains `full_lifecycle_propose_vote_execute` (propose@T0 ‚Üí vote@T0+500 ‚Üí execute@T0+2000 in one test) + previously-unreachable `execute_wrong_calldata_reverts` + `no_majority_defeats_proposal` paths. dao-governance test count: 15 ‚Üí 16, with stronger coverage on the existing 15. OTIGEN_TEST_SPEC ¬ß4.2 + ¬ß4.5 documents the new fields + adds Foundry ‚Üí otigen translation table (`vm.prank` ‚Üí `from`, `vm.deal` ‚Üí `[tests.setup].balances`, etc.) to close the discoverability gap for Solidity-coming devs. ‚Äî PR [otigen#66](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/66) + docs [pyde-book#172](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/172)
- [x] **`debug_log` host fn ‚Äî `console.log`-style printf debugging** ‚Äî closes the biggest dev-ergonomics gap from Foundry parity. Runner registers `pyde::debug_log(msg_ptr, len)` unconditionally; contracts get to sprinkle `debug_log(b"value=...")` calls during development, and the runner writes `[debug] <fn_name>: <msg>` to stderr (+ captures into `TestEnv.debug_logs` for trace renderers). Test-only by design: HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß9.1 lists it as a hard-rejected import on chain; ¬ß9.3 (new) documents the runner-side semantics; WASM_AUTHOR_GUIDE ¬ß14.8 (new) carries the copy-paste `dump(label, value)` pattern + stripping rules. Devs previously fell back to `revert(b"value=42")` to dump intermediates ‚Äî that crutch is now obsolete. 4 KB payload cap on each call bounds runaway-loop stderr blow-up. Tests: 2 unit tests on the runner (happy-path captures into `debug_logs` + oversized payload traps with the expected error message). ‚Äî PR [otigen#67](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/67) + docs [pyde-book#175](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/175)
- [x] **`otigen devnet` wrapper with `--fork` pass-through** ‚Äî closes the last otigen toolchain feature item from MC-1 Stream Œ±. Authors drive devnet bootstrapping from one toolchain entry point instead of remembering the engine binary path (`../engine/target/release/pyde`). Thin wrapper around `pyde devnet`; every flag is pass-through ‚Äî the headliner is **`--fork <FILE_OR_URL>`** which matches the engine's existing scope: local borsh snapshot file (`./snapshot.bin`, produced by `Snapshotter::build`) OR HTTP(S) URL to a running validator's `pyde_getSnapshot` RPC endpoint (`http://127.0.0.1:9933`, or once they ship: mainnet / testnet validator URLs). Pre-mainnet the URL option is "fork another local devnet"; post-mainnet it's the canonical "snapshot real production state for local debugging" shape Foundry users expect from `anvil --fork-url`. Other pass-through flags: `--rpc-listen`, `--prefund-count`, `--prefund-amount`, `--chain-id`, `--tick-ms`. Binary resolution: `--engine-bin` ‚Üí `PYDE_BIN` env ‚Üí `pyde` on `PATH` (three-tier fallback so devs can run against a locally-built engine, a system-installed one, or a CI-cached binary without re-typing the path). Up-front mutual-exclusion check between `--fork` and the `--prefund-*` flags so authors get a fast clear error instead of mid-startup engine-side rejection. stdin/stdout/stderr inherited from the parent so the engine's startup banner + `RUST_LOG=info` traces flow straight through; Ctrl-C from the terminal hits both processes (same fg pgrp) and the engine handles its own graceful shutdown. 11 unit tests on the argv builder + binary resolution; live smoke verifies the mutual-exclusion error catches before spawn, and `--engine-bin <path> --rpc-listen 127.0.0.1:9933` actually spawns the engine with the RPC responding to `pyde_waveId`. **Out of scope** (follow-ups if demand surfaces): static-file HTTP URL support (otigen-side download into tempfile, would add an HTTP dep), `otigen test --fork` (in-process snapshot loading into the test runner's state store ‚Äî 2-3√ó bigger surface). ‚Äî PR [otigen#140](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/140)
- [x] **Final README cleanup ‚Äî simple-multisig + profile-registry** ‚Äî closes the example-README substrate-alignment sweep. `simple-multisig`: two "Phase 4" coordination-label leaks scrubbed; new "predates the macro substrate" callout up top pointing at the acceptance-suite `multisig-wallet` for the current shape, while noting `simple-multisig` stays useful as the canonical reference for the in-contract FALCON-verify + off-chain-signed-claim pattern that `multisig-wallet` doesn't cover (it uses on-chain approval bookkeeping instead); `SDK_AUTHOR_GUIDE` + cross-link to `multisig-wallet` added to references section. `profile-registry`: already well-positioned by the existing "Status (v1)" section that honestly explains the v2 parachain deferral; only addition is a new "References" section with `HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß8` + `WASM_AUTHOR_GUIDE` + `SDK_AUTHOR_GUIDE` so parachain authors + community SDK porters have the canonical entry points. - [x] **Struct-typed storage values in `declare_storage!()`** ‚Äî closes the biggest authoring footgun the substrate-batch handoff brief flagged: declaring a borsh-codable struct as the value type of a storage field used to require manually borshing into `bytes` and back on every read / write. Now `{ name = "owner_profile", type = "struct(UserProfile)" }` works directly ‚Äî the macro emits typed accessors that delegate to the chain's variable-length `sstore_*` / `sload_*` host fns with a borsh round-trip (`::borsh::to_vec(&value)` on write, `<T as ::borsh::BorshDeserialize>::try_from_slice(&buf)` on read). Pure otigen-only work; no engine ask. Chain-side mapping is `ScalarType::Bytes` ‚Äî the engine validates the slot as opaque bytes; the macro layers the typed wrapper on the contract source side. Authors `#[derive(BorshSerialize, BorshDeserialize)]` on their type and write idiomatic Rust against the typed accessor. Both scalar and `map<address, struct(Name)>` shapes supported. `pyde-storage-macros`: new `Scalar::Custom(String)` variant + parser branch with ident validation (rejects invalid Rust idents up front); `rust_ty()` emits `super::<Name>` so types resolve through the emitted `pub mod storage`; `lower_fields` rejects struct-as-map-key (variable-length ‚Äî matches the existing vec-key policy) and `vec(struct(X))` falls through the existing `vec(<variable>)` rejection. `otigen-abi::build::parse_scalar_type` accepts `struct(<Name>)` and maps it to `ScalarType::Bytes`. 8 new unit tests in the macro crate (22/22 total). Canonical acceptance contract `examples/struct-storage/` exercises `UserProfile { display_name, joined_wave, karma, avatar }` as both a scalar and `map<address, UserProfile>` with a 12-assertion Python harness driving real `pyde devnet` over JSON-RPC (set / get / clear / default-on-unset / two-key writes / cross-key delete isolation ‚Äî ALL PASS). Wired into `make e2e` via the existing harness pattern. ‚Äî PR [otigen#135](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/135)
- [x] **Bump `pyde_abi_version` test assertions from V1.1 to V1.2** ‚Äî companion cleanup to the acceptance-suite batch (otigen #116‚Äì#133, engine #228‚Äì#234). - [x] **otigen-rpc accepts hex-string numeric fields on Receipt / WaveInfo / LogEntry** ‚Äî once A23/A24 landed on engine main and the deploy tx started actually flowing through admission ‚Üí apply ‚Üí receipt, the next surface in the way was a wire-shape mismatch: the devnet emits `gas_used`, `wave_id`, `tx_index`, `event_index`, `anchor_round`, `tx_count`, `timestamp_secs`, and `gas` as `0x`-prefixed hex strings per spec ¬ß17.4, but otigen-rpc's typed response bodies deserialised them as raw `u64` / `u32`. `otigen deploy` broke at receipt poll with `DecodeShape: invalid type: string "0x989680", expected u64` (`0x989680` = the 10M gas charge). Added a small `deserialize_u64_hex_or_int` + u32 counterpart that accept BOTH shapes ‚Äî numeric (kept for backward compat with the existing test fixtures) and `0x`-prefixed hex string (what the devnet actually emits) ‚Äî then applied across `Receipt`, `LogEntry`, `LogCursor`, `WaveInfo`, `GasEstimate`. Three deserialise tests: int-only (pre-existing), hex-only (new), mixed-in-one-payload (new). End-to-end verified against live `pyde devnet`: the deploy command now passes receipt poll and surfaces the next downstream issue (engine ask A25 ‚Äî `apply_deploy` reads raw `tx.data` as wasm instead of borsh-decoding `DeployData` first). ‚Äî PR [otigen#115](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/115)
- [x] **`InclusionTimeout` carries the tx hash + actionable hint** ‚Äî the receipt-poll timeout in `deploy` + `lifecycle` (and `call`, which reuses lifecycle's `poll_receipt`) dropped the tx hash on the way out: `tx not included after 60s` left the user with no handle to re-check the receipt later or trace the tx through the chain. - [x] **Default `--bundle` path resolves against `--config` dir, not cwd** ‚Äî surfaced by the first non-trivial deploy attempt against `pyde devnet`: `otigen --config /abs/project/otigen.toml deploy` errored with `BundleNotFound: ./artifacts/<name>.bundle` even though the config pointed at a project tree with one. Root cause: `deploy.rs::resolve_bundle_dir` and `verify.rs::resolve_bundle_dir` used `PathBuf::from("./artifacts")`, which Rust resolves against the caller's cwd ‚Äî directly contradicting the help text that promised `--config`-anchored resolution. Verify's help text now explicitly mentions `--config`-anchored resolution (deploy's already did). - [x] **otigen-cli routed through `otigen-tx-codec` ‚Äî local Tx fork dropped** ‚Äî `otigen-cli/src/tx.rs` had been carrying a parallel Tx envelope + `canonical_hash` implementation since the engine's tx crate was a scaffold. Same drift-trap that bit `otigen-abi` once already (PR #95). This pulls otigen-cli onto the shared shim: `tx.rs` becomes a re-export of `pyde_engine_types::tx::{Tx, TxType, FeePayer, AccessEntry, AccessType}` plus the otigen-specific payload types (`DeployData`, `ContractType`, `LifecyclePayload`) and the `build_deploy_tx` / `build_lifecycle_tx` constructors. `Tx::canonical_hash` and `Tx::to_wire_bytes` gone; deploy + lifecycle commands now call `otigen_tx_codec::tx_canonical_hash` / `otigen_tx_codec::tx_wire_bytes`. Deploy / pause / unpause / kill / upgrade flows now produce signatures the engine's mempool `verify_tx_signature` accepts verbatim ‚Äî no translation layer. ‚Äî PR [otigen#102](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/102)
- [x] **`otigen-tx-codec` crate ‚Äî canonical `tx_hash` signing + cross-repo parity vectors** ‚Äî new crate (second T-10 toolchain-threat-model exemption alongside `otigen-test`) providing `tx_canonical_hash` / `tx_wire_bytes` / `sign_tx` helpers. Delegates the hash computation to `pyde_engine_tx::tx_hash` directly ‚Äî no parallel implementation, no recipe drift. Six committed parity vectors in `fixtures/cross_repo_tx_vectors_v1.json` span every relevant encoding axis (Standard / Deploy / StakeDeposit; Sender / GasTank / Paymaster fee payers; populated + empty data / access_list / deadline; large u128 values). The 32-byte hash bytes are byte-equality asserted on regen; sample sig + wire bytes are committed-but-not-byte-equality-asserted (FALCON-512 in `pyde-crypto` uses randomized signing ‚Äî every call produces a different valid sig). Initial PR #100 modeled the wrong signing protocol (mirrored `devnet/wallet.rs::tx_pre_image` placeholder which signs raw borsh-Tx-minus-sig); #101 course-corrected to the authoritative `pyde_engine_tx::tx_hash` protocol the mempool's `verify_tx_signature` actually verifies against. Devnet wallet's `tx_pre_image` helper is a MockSigner-era placeholder; will converge on `tx_hash` when A16 part 2 lands. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#100](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/100) + [otigen#101](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/101)
- [x] **upgradeable-proxy passes under `--engine` (void-void inner + `pre_register_self_account`)** ‚Äî closed the last cross-contract holdout on the engine path. Two fixes: (1) `_inner_set_value` rewritten to spec-compliant void-void (HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß3.5.2) so engine's void-void dispatcher can invoke it via `delegate_call`. (2) `EngineRunner::pre_register_self_account` writes the primary contract's own `Account.code_hash` into the overlay before tests run ‚Äî engine's `delegate_call(self_addr)` reads the target account from overlay to resolve code; without the record it returned `ERR_INVALID_FUNCTION_NAME` and the proxy reverted with `"DelegateFailed"`. Harmless for tests that don't delegate-call self. Engine-path tally moved 14/18 ‚Üí 15/18. ‚Äî PR [otigen#99](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/99)
- [x] **counter-pair-b spec-compliant void-void rewrite + legacy `cross_call` / `delegate_call` calldata mocks** ‚Äî counter-pair-b was the last spec-non-compliant example; its inner entry points exported `(calldata_ptr, calldata_len) -> i32`, which the engine's void-void dispatcher (HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß3.5.2) cannot invoke. Rewrites `bump_remote` / `revert_remote` / `record_received` to void-void; pulls calldata via `pyde::calldata_size` + `pyde::calldata_copy`. Adds matching mocks to the legacy runner (mirroring the engine's saturating semantics ‚Äî `i32::MAX` / `u32::MAX` rather than trapping); teaches both `host_cross_call` and `host_delegate_call` to accept either shape (0 or 2 params), staging `env.calldata` around the sub-call so void-void callees read the parent-supplied bytes back. Result: counter-pair-a went from holdout to 6/6 on both legacy and engine paths. ‚Äî PR [otigen#98](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/98)
- [x] **`otigen build --strict` + implicit-strict `otigen deploy`** ‚Äî closes the honour-system gap from PR 23 (debug_log). Adds `TEST_ONLY_HOST_FNS = ["debug_log"]` as the third companion list to `CORE_HOST_FNS` / `PARACHAIN_HOST_FNS`; threads a `strict: bool` through `validate_imports` / `validate_all`. Behaviour table: `otigen build` (default) + `otigen check` accept test-only fns so the dev loop stays unobstructed; `otigen build --strict` + `otigen deploy` reject with `TestOnlyHostFn` ‚Äî mirroring the chain-side hard rejection. `otigen deploy` hard-codes strict=true so authors who skip the explicit flag still get the production gate. 2 new unit tests pin both paths. Spec + author-guide updated: HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß9.3 + WASM_AUTHOR_GUIDE ¬ß14.8 now describe the live flag (removed PR-23b's "planned" hedging). ‚Äî PR [otigen#68](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/68) + docs [pyde-book#177](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/177)
- [x] **macro layer: `#[pyde::entry]` + `declare_storage!()` + `declare_events!()` + ergonomic `pyde::*` wrappers** ‚Äî closes the "every contract author hand-writes the calldata-decode + return-wrap boilerplate" footgun the `() -> ()` strict ABI created. Three new proc-macro crates plus a rewritten `pyde-host` ergonomics layer. **`pyde-entry-macros::entry`** ships `#[pyde::entry]` which wraps any `fn foo(a: A, b: B) -> R` into the canonical void-void shape: emits a sibling `extern "C" fn foo()` that fetches calldata via `pyde::raw::calldata_size` + `pyde::raw::calldata_copy(out_ptr, out_len_ptr) -> i32` (3-arg ABI matching the chain ‚Äî the original 2-arg `calldata_copy(offset, len)` extern was a pre-PR drift that didn't surface in `counter-rust` because it takes no args; surfaced in `erc20-token` PR), borsh-decodes into a tuple `(a, b)`, calls the user function, borsh-encodes the return value, hands the bytes back via `pyde::raw::return_with_data(ptr, len)`. `#[pyde::entry(view)]` / `#[pyde::entry(payable)]` / `#[pyde::entry(constructor)]` / `#[pyde::entry(reentrant)]` thread the attribute into the emitted `pyde.abi` custom-section entry so the chain's deploy-time validation + per-call dispatch sees the right flags. **`pyde-storage-macros::declare_storage`** reads the `[state]` schema from `otigen.toml` at compile time + emits typed accessors: `storage::value() -> u64`, `storage::value_set(v: u64)`, `storage::balances_get(addr: Address) -> u128`, `storage::balances_set(addr: Address, v: u128)`, etc. ‚Äî one accessor pair per declared field at every arity. Field-type vocabulary matches chain-side `StorageType` (`U8..U128`, `I8..I128`, `Bool`, `Address`, `Hash32`, `Bytes`, `String`, fixed `Vec(...)`); `vec(<variable>)` rejected at parse time with a clear error pointing at the rule. Slot derivation is host-side via the typed `sstore_map*` / `sload_map*` host fns ‚Äî macro only emits the encode/decode + call-the-right-arity glue. **`pyde-events-macros::declare_events`** ships `declare_events! { Transfer(from: Address indexed, to: Address indexed, amount: u128) }` shapes computing `Blake3(signature_string)` for the event topic0 at expansion time (constant `[u8; 32]`); indexed primitives LE-padded-to-32 for canonical topic encoding; `.emit()` method on each event struct writes `(topics: Vec<Hash32>, data: Vec<u8>)` through `pyde::raw::emit_event` matching the chain's `EventRecord` shape. **`pyde-host` ergonomics**: `pyde::ctx::*` (sender, value, self_address, wave_id, wave_timestamp, chain_id), `pyde::calldata::*` (size, read_at, read_all), `pyde::hash::*` (blake3, poseidon2), `pyde::emit_event`, `pyde::revert(&str)`, `pyde::return_(&[u8])` all wrap the raw externs under `pyde::raw::*` ‚Äî authors who want the raw calls keep them; the wrappers handle the borsh + panic-on-error path for everyone else. **`pyde-host::call::execute<T>` / `execute_with_value` / `execute_static` / `execute_delegate`** introduced as the typed cross-call wrapper returning `Result<T, CallError>` ‚Äî `CallError::{Reverted(Vec<u8>), InvalidFunction, NonPayable, InsufficientBalance, ReentrancyBlocked, DecodeError, ReturnDataTooLarge { actual }}` matches every negative `i32` the chain may return from `pyde::cross_call*` per HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß4. **Migrated `counter-rust`** to the new shape end-to-end as the smoke contract. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#116](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/116), [#117](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/117), [#118](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/118), [#119](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/119), [#120](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/120), [#121](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/121), [#124](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/124)
- [x] **`otigen-toml`: typed-storage `[state]` schema + custom-type `[types.MyStruct]` / `[types.MyEnum]` parsing + ABI v1.2 wire** ‚Äî extends the bundler's `otigen.toml ‚Üí pyde.abi` borsh path to carry the full schema + types section the macros + chain consume. **State schema**: `[state]` table accepts one entry per storage field with `type = "u64"` / `type = "map<address, u128>"` / `type = "map<address, map<u64, bool>>"` / `type = "MyStruct"` / `type = "vec<u8>(fixed=32)"`; parser produces `StateFieldAbi { name, ty: StorageType, key_arity }` filling `ContractAbi.state_schema`. **Custom types**: `[types.MyStruct] fields = { a = "u64", b = "address", balances = "map<address, u128>" }` produces `TypeAbi { name: "MyStruct", kind: TypeKind::Struct { fields } }`; `[types.MyEnum] variants = ["Pending", "Active", "Closed"]` produces unit-only `TypeAbi::Enum`. **ABI version bump**: bundle now emits `pyde_abi_version = V1_2 = 0x0001_0002` once `[types]` or `[state]` is non-empty (V1_0 baseline kept for contracts that don't use either). Validation: undefined type names, cyclic struct refs, variable Vecs as state values rejected at `otigen build` (`pyde.abi` custom section never gets emitted with an invalid shape). `MAX_SUPPORTED_ABI_VERSION` test pin updated to `V1_2` so the bundler + chain advance lockstep. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#122](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/122), [#126](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/126)
- [x] **acceptance suite: 10 contracts √ó 242 on-chain assertions covering every primitive every real DApp shape needs** ‚Äî closes the "we have a strict ABI but does anyone actually build something real on it" question with a full live e2e suite. Each contract exercises a distinct primitive set; each lands with a Python harness that drives the release `pyde` binary + `otigen` CLI over real JSON-RPC + asserts on actual chain state + event logs + balance moves. **Phase 1: `erc20-token`** ‚Äî `Transfer` + `Approval` events, allowance bookkeeping, decimal-aware balance math, deny-overdraw + deny-unauth-spend reverts. **Phase 2: `erc721-token`** ‚Äî token-id ownership, `setApprovalForAll`, `transferFrom` authorization paths, `tokenURI` lookup. **Phase 3: `nft-marketplace`** ‚Äî cross-call from marketplace ‚Üí NFT contract via `pyde::call::execute<()>`; surfaces the per-frame caller_address fix (engine #234); funds escrow + payout on `fill(id)`. **Phase 4: `dao-governance`** ‚Äî proposal lifecycle (`propose` ‚Üí `vote` ‚Üí `execute`), quorum + threshold math, cross-call into a target contract on `execute(id)`. **Phase 5: `escrow`** ‚Äî `#[payable]` `create(beneficiary, release_at)` deposits value; time-gated `claim()` releases after `wave_timestamp >= release_at`; refund path before release. **Phase 6: `upgradeable-proxy` + `proxy-logic-v1` + `proxy-logic-v2`** ‚Äî admin-gated `upgrade_to(new_logic)`, `delegate_call` preserves proxy's `self_address` so writes land in the proxy's slots; state survives v1‚Üív2 upgrade end-to-end; logic contracts' own state confirmed untouched via post-call audit (`logic_v1.get() = 0` + `logic_v2.get() = 0` after the proxy's `value` slot reaches 50). **Phase 7: `payment-channel`** ‚Äî off-chain signed claims with `falcon_verify`; on-chain `close(claim, sig)` settles + transfers via `delegate_call` into a settlement library. **Phase 8: `multisig-wallet`** ‚Äî M-of-N owner approvals; both a no-value cross-call (counter.increment) and a value-forwarding cross-call (escrow.create funded by the multisig's own deposit); replay-blocked by action-hash bookkeeping. Plus **`storage-stress`** (every `StorageType` √ó every arity round-tripped) + **`borsh-coverage`** (custom structs + enums √ó multiple args + return types). All 10 contracts each ship with a `tests/<name>_e2e.py` Python harness driving the live chain. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#123](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/123), [#125](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/125), [#127](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/127), [#129](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/129), [#130](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/130), [#131](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/131), [#132](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/132)
- [x] **e2e infrastructure: `examples/_e2e_lib.sh` shared helpers + per-contract `run_e2e.sh` drivers + `make e2e` orchestrator + GitHub Actions wrapper** ‚Äî closes the "every harness re-implements devnet spin-up + wallet import + deploy" pain. `examples/_e2e_lib.sh` exports `start_devnet` (boots `pyde devnet` into a temp dir, traps EXIT so the devnet dies after each suite), `import_devnet_wallets` (reads the prefund-N keystore lines into `DEVNET_ADDR_<N>` env vars), `export_devnet_addresses`, `build_bundle <toml>`, `deploy_contract <toml> <wallet>` (sets `$DEPLOY_ADDR`), `deploy_contract_with_init_args <toml> <wallet> <hex>`, `borsh_string_hex <s>`. Each `examples/<name>/tests/run_e2e.sh` is ~30 lines and delegates everything else to its `tests/<name>_e2e.py` harness over real JSON-RPC. **`make e2e`** runs all 10 suites in sequence; each spins a fresh devnet via the EXIT trap so the runner stays clean between suites. **CI wrapper** (`.github/workflows/e2e.yml`) sibling-clones `pyde-crypto` + `engine` via `PYDE_REPOS_TOKEN`, builds the release `pyde` binary + the release `otigen` binary once + runs `make e2e`. PR-gated by an explicit `e2e` label so the ~10-15 min job doesn't fire on every PR; push-to-`main` + manual `workflow_dispatch` always run. Devnet stdout/stderr uploaded as `devnet-logs` artifact on failure (7-day retention) for postmortem. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#128](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/128), [#133](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/133)
- [x] **pyde-book: `() -> ()` entry-point ABI chapter + SDK Author Guide for community contributors** ‚Äî closes the "we just made deploy break for every contract author with WASM-level args or results; here's how to fix yours + how to write your own language SDK" doc gap engine #225 left open. **`companion/HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC.md` ¬ß3.0** ‚Äî new section "Entry-point WASM signature" spelling out the void-void rule explicitly: every exported entry is `() -> ()` at the WASM-function-boundary level; args flow through the `pyde.calldata_size` / `pyde.calldata_copy` host fns + return data flows through `pyde.return_with_data`. Cross-references the deploy-time validation error message + the runtime check that catches anything slipping past deploy. **`companion/SDK_AUTHOR_GUIDE.md`** ‚Äî new doc walking a non-Rust SDK author through the calldata-decode + return-encode shim pattern, the `pyde.abi` custom-section emission, the `#[entry]`-equivalent macro shape (where the language supports one), the canonical Borsh wire format Pyde standardized on, the gas-table-aware host-fn registry, and the deploy-time validation paths their bundler must satisfy. Targeted at someone wanting to ship a TinyGo / AssemblyScript / Zig SDK ‚Äî gives them a concrete spec to implement against instead of having to reverse-engineer otigen. **Chapter 17 "Developer Tools"** ‚Äî new "Contract-side SDKs (community)" subsection making it explicit that the otigen Rust path is the reference implementation, that the chain is language-agnostic at the WASM + host-fn boundary, and that contributions for other languages are welcome with the SDK Author Guide as the entry point. ‚Äî PR [pyde-book#269](https://github.com/pyde-net/pyde-book/pull/269)
- [ ] `otigen test` ‚Äî Foundry-grade contract behaviour test framework. Spec: [`OTIGEN_TEST_SPEC.md`](companion/OTIGEN_TEST_SPEC.md). Ships in three sequential PRs:
  - [x] **Phase 1 ‚Äî parser + name resolution + spec validation.** `crates/otigen-test` crate; TOML schema types for `[accounts]` / `[cheats]` / `[[tests]]`; account-name ‚Üí Blake3 address + state-field ‚Üí Poseidon2 slot derivation; `otigen test --dry-run` lists tests + resolved hashes without executing; e2e tests against a hand-written `.test.toml` fixture. ‚Äî PR [otigen#30](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/30) ‚Äî 28 unit + 1 doctest + 9 e2e tests; workspace total 261 ‚Üí 299 passing.
  - [x] **Phase 2 ‚Äî wasmtime runner + read/write/event/revert mocks.** Mock host fns: `sload` / `sstore` / `sdelete` / `caller` / `value` / `emit_event` / `revert` / `now` / `current_wave` / `chain_id`; single-call execution + per-call `expect`; return-value + storage-after + events + revert assertions; sample `tests/contract.test.toml` in `examples/hello-rust`. ‚Äî PR [otigen#31](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/31) ‚Äî 17 new tests (7 runner unit + 9 e2e + 1 doctest); workspace total 299 ‚Üí 316 passing. wasmtime 36 (security-patched).
  - [x] **Phase 3 ‚Äî full Foundry surface.** Multi-call `[[tests.calls]]` chains, native-balance mocks (`balance_of` / `transfer_native`), final-state `[tests.expect]` assertions, per-test cheat overrides, named event matching against `[events.*]`, `--filter` flag + per-test timing, plus --json NDJSON test events (test_suite_start / test_start / test_pass / test_fail / test_suite_done) and --bundle override. ‚Äî PR [otigen#32](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/32) ‚Äî 9 new e2e tests; workspace 316 ‚Üí 325+ passing; `make all` byte-equivalent to GitHub CI now serves as local pre-push gate while Actions billing is blocked.
- [x] **`otigen console` REPL (spec ¬ß3.8)** ‚Äî interactive `pyde>` prompt against a Pyde node for ad-hoc chain queries + tx submission without re-typing `otigen call --network ‚Ä¶ --from ‚Ä¶` every time. Foundry-`cast` shape; line-edited via rustyline with persisted history at `~/.otigen_console_history` and Ctrl-C / Ctrl-D handling that matches every other shell. **MVP surface**: `help` / `?`, `balance <addr>`, `nonce <addr>`, `call <addr> <fn> [hex]` (view, free, no tx), `tx <addr> <fn> [hex] [--value <decimal>]` (sign + submit + receipt poll), `exit` / `quit`. **Session-scoped network + sender** ‚Äî `--network` and `--from` bind once at REPL startup and every per-command call reuses the same `RpcClient`. **Lazy wallet unlock** ‚Äî views never prompt; the first `tx` asks for the password once and the unlocked signer is cached for the rest of the session. **Address inputs accept either a `0x`-prefixed 32-byte hex address OR a registered name resolved via `pyde_resolveName`** ‚Äî same `resolve_target` path the rest of the toolchain uses; unknown names surface `address resolution failed` and the REPL stays alive instead of crashing out. **`tx` reuses the same `lifecycle::poll_receipt` + `otigen_tx_codec::tx_canonical_hash` + FALCON-sign path** the `otigen call` subcommand drives, so chain-side behaviour of `pyde> tx ‚Ä¶` is byte-identical to the corresponding `otigen call ‚Ä¶` invocation. **Coverage**: 12 unit tests on argument parsers (`call` / `tx`), `--value` flag in any position, hex prefix tolerance, double-calldata + value-without-arg rejection, PYDE pretty-printer for round + fractional amounts; **16-assertion Python e2e harness** (`make e2e-console`) drives the real release binary via stdin pipe against a live `pyde devnet` ‚Äî startup banner (network / chain_id), help catalog, `balance` quanta + PYDE pretty-print on prefund accounts, `nonce` = 0 on fresh devnet, error-path on unknown name + unknown command surface diagnostics and the REPL stays alive across both. ALL PASS first real run. Wired into `make e2e` after the existing smoke suites. **Deferred** (each 2-3√ó MVP scope, follow-up PRs): `events <addr> [--topic <hash>] [--from <wave>]` (needs `pyde_getLogs` typing + filter wiring), `state <addr> <field>` (needs ABI-aware decoding from the contract's `pyde.abi` section), `subscribe` (needs websocket / long-poll the devnet doesn't expose yet), ABI-aware calldata typing (Foundry's `cast send --json-abi` flow). ‚Äî PR [otigen#136](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/136)

#### Œ±.qual ‚Äî Quality bar (production-readiness gate)

Every item below clears before Œ± ships. Documented separately from the feature surface so the gate is unambiguous.

**Testing infrastructure**

- [x] Criterion benchmarks for every hot path with baselines committed to `benches/baseline/*.json`:
  - `otigen-toml`: TOML parse + cross-cutting validation ‚úÖ (pyde-net/otigen#6)
  - `otigen-abi`: `ContractAbi` build, Borsh encode/decode round-trip, `pyde.abi` custom-section inject + extract, validators, full pipeline ‚úÖ (pyde-net/otigen#6)
  - `otigen-cli`: full `otigen build` pipeline end-to-end ‚Äî measured via the otigen-abi full_pipeline bench (parse‚Üívalidate‚Üíbuild‚Üíencode‚Üíinject = 14.5 ¬µs on the reference machine); the wall-clock `otigen build` invocation is dominated by file I/O, not validator work
- [x] `cargo-fuzz` targets shipped across the workspace with `make fuzz-soak` driving the 24h+ cumulative run per target (otigen#143):
  - `otigen-toml` parser: `fuzz_toml_parser` (malformed input, deep nesting, huge fields) ‚Äî PR [otigen#39](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/39)
  - `otigen-abi` WASM validator: `fuzz_wasm_validator` (malformed binaries, edge cases in section structure) ‚Äî PR [otigen#39](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/39)
  - `otigen-abi` custom-section injection: `fuzz_section_injection` (extreme WASM module shapes) ‚Äî PR [otigen#39](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/39)
  - `otigen-test` parser + storage paths: `fuzz_test_toml` + `fuzz_storage_path` ‚Äî PR [otigen#39](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/39)
  - **Soak handle** (`make fuzz-soak` all 5 √ó FUZZ_SOAK_SECONDS=86400 default, per-target shortcuts for re-soaking just the target you reduced+fixed after a crash; substrate batch raised the rustc nightly minimum to 1.93+; live validation via `make fuzz-smoke` 60s √ó 5 = 12.8M iterations, 0 crashes) ‚Äî PR [otigen#143](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/143)
- [x] Property-test coverage audit: 21 proptest groups across `otigen-toml` and `otigen-abi` (was ~10, 11 new groups added) ‚Äî PR [otigen#37](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/37)
- [x] Adversarial corpus: 34 hand-rolled `otigen.toml` files under `crates/otigen-toml/tests/corpus/{pass,fail}/` each verified by the corpus harness to pass / fail with the expected diagnostic (20 new fixtures landed in PR [otigen#38](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/38))
- [x] Reproducibility test: two clean builds of the canonical hello-rust example produce byte-identical `contract.wasm` and `abi.json` (modulo `manifest.build_timestamp`) ‚Äî `examples/hello-rust/tests/run_reproducibility.sh` hard-resets `target/` + `artifacts/`, runs `cargo build --release --target wasm32-unknown-unknown` followed by `otigen build` twice, snapshots both bundles, hashes via shasum (macOS) / sha256sum (Linux), strips `build_timestamp` from `manifest.json` (python stdlib, no jq dep) for the manifest comparison, and asserts byte-identical on all three. ALL PASS on first real run against the current shipping toolchain ‚Äî confirms the pipeline is already deterministic; the invariant is locked going forward. Wired as `make reproducibility` Makefile target alongside the existing `e2e-*` family. Slow (two full cargo builds) ‚Äî intended pre-release, not every commit. ‚Äî PR [otigen#141](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/141)

**CI + supply chain**

- [ ] Multi-platform CI matrix: `ubuntu-latest` x86_64 + aarch64, `macos-latest` arm64, `windows-latest` x86_64 ‚Äî build / test / clippy / fmt on every PR
- [ ] `cargo-audit` (RustSec advisories) gate on every PR
- [ ] `cargo-deny` (license policy + version policy + duplicate-version checks) gate on every PR
- [ ] `cargo-machete` (unused dep detection) on every PR
- [ ] MSRV check: workspace `rust-version = "1.87"` enforced in CI on a 1.87 toolchain *(bumped from 1.75 ‚Üí 1.87 in 2026-05 when `wasmtime 28 ‚Üí 36` cleared 7 RUSTSEC advisories and `pyde-crypto`'s Plonky3 transitive started using `unsigned_is_multiple_of` ‚Äî stabilized in 1.87)*
- [ ] cargo-about generated 3rd-party attribution report shipped with every binary release
- [x] Signed binary releases via GitHub Actions: Linux x86_64/aarch64 + macOS arm64 + Windows x86_64 tarballs, sha256sums, sigstore-keyless OIDC signatures, attached to GitHub Releases ‚Äî `.github/workflows/release.yml` shipped via PR [otigen#42](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/42). Workflow triggers on `v*` tag push. v0.1.0-testnet.0 smoke tag exists; first successful run blocked on GitHub Actions billing upgrade (per-org plan needed)
- [x] **Security audit + cargo-deny gate green post-engine-embed** ‚Äî after [otigen#168](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/168) pulled the engine workspace's transitive deps into otigen's build graph, cargo-audit + cargo-deny surfaced three upstream-blocked advisories (`hickory-proto 0.25` NSEC3 unbounded loop + O(n¬≤) DNS name-compression CPU exhaustion, both pinned to 0.25 by `libp2p 0.56`'s `libp2p-dns` + `libp2p-mdns`; `lru 0.12.5` unsound `IterMut`) plus three engine path-deps the existing skip-tree didn't cover (`pyde-engine-mempool` / `pyde-engine-net` / `pyde-engine-node`). All four surfaces addressed: rustsec audit-check action now reads `.cargo/audit.toml` (mirrors `deny.toml`'s ignore list in cargo-audit's separate config); `deny.toml` skip-tree extends with the three new engine crates. Each ignore documents the reachability case for why the path isn't exercised from otigen's code (`otigen devnet` runs single-validator without bootnode DNS lookups; `lru` is consumed via `get`/`put` only). `release.yml` also picked up the engine sibling-clone step the engine path-dep needs (previously cloned only `pyde-crypto`). Plus a clippy `needless_raw_string_hashes` hotfix in `otigen-rpc/src/types.rs` that the rust 1.96 clippy bump caught. CI back to all-jobs green on main. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#169](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/169) + [otigen#171](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/171)

**UX completeness**

- [x] `--json` NDJSON output wired across every subcommand per OTIGEN_BINARY_SPEC ¬ß10.2 ‚Äî `InspectStart`, `VerifyStart`, `DeployFailed`, `LifecycleFailed` plus the existing build / wallet / test event streams, all emitted to stdout as one event per line ‚Äî PR [otigen#34](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/34)
- [x] `--verbose` / `-vv` actually emits the documented log levels ‚Äî tiny `log::info` / `log::debug` wrapper on `eprintln!`; `-v` enables info, `-vv` enables info + debug; threaded through `Cli` ‚Üí `Args` ‚Üí commands ‚Äî PR [otigen#35](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/35)
- [x] Signal handling: `Ctrl-C` mid-build cleans up partial bundle artifacts ‚Äî `otigen build` installs a `ctrlc` SIGINT handler the first time it runs in the process. The handler reads a shared `OnceLock<Mutex<Option<PathBuf>>>` slot containing the currently-active partial dir (set by `PartialBundleGuard::new`, cleared by `.commit()` or Drop), best-effort `fs::remove_dir_all`s the path, then `process::exit(130)` to terminate (matching bash's "process terminated by signal" convention). Three cleanup layers now stacked: (1) Drop on early return / panic / `?` propagation, (2) SIGINT handler on Ctrl-C, (3) `sweep_stale_partials` at the next build (SIGKILL / power loss fallback where neither Drop nor the handler runs). 4 unit tests in `commands::build::sigint_tests` cover slot management (new registers / commit clears + skips removal / drop sweeps + clears / concurrent-build safety). Reproducibility test (`make reproducibility`) ALL PASS unchanged. New dep: `ctrlc = "3"` on otigen-cli ‚Äî small, cross-platform, exactly the right API. ‚Äî PR [otigen#142](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/142)
- [x] `otigen --version` includes git-sha + build profile ‚Äî `build.rs` captures git sha + dirty marker + cargo `PROFILE` at compile time; re-runs on `.git/HEAD` change ‚Äî PR [otigen#33](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/33)
- [x] **`otigen console state <addr> <field>` ‚Äî substrate-typed scalar storage read in the REPL** ‚Äî closes the "values?" half of the deferred surface flagged in otigen#136. Same `Blake3(self_address ‚Äñ field_name)` slot derivation the chain's `sstore_scalar` host fn writes, then decodes the bytes per the type token declared under `[state].schema` in `otigen.toml`. Full primitive vocabulary the macro substrate emits today: `u8..u128`, `i8..i128`, `bool`, `address`, `hash32`, `bytes`, `string`; `vec(...)` / `struct(...)` / `map` are explicitly reserved with a clear "REPL MVP scope ‚Äî follow-up" message instead of silently truncating. Wrapper bugfix that fell out: `otigen_rpc::Client::get_storage_slot` now sends the engine's actual `[{"slot": hex}]` param shape (the old `[address, slot]` array was a dead two-param call the devnet rejected) and returns `Option<HexBytes>` so the engine's `null` for an unwritten slot lands as `None` rather than a serde-decode failure. `inspect --field` updated for the same return-type change. **Tests**: 13 new unit tests in `commands::console::tests` cover every primitive decoder branch + wrong-width hint + the deferred-type messages; console-smoke e2e adds 4 assertions (success path ‚Üí `<unset>` for empty slot, unknown-field error, map-field MVP-scope error, help-catalog line). Smoke seeds a `[state]` schema with one scalar + one map so both branches exercise. 21 / 21 smoke assertions green; `make e2e` 11 contracts stays green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#145](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/145)
- [x] **`otigen inspect --state-field` ‚Äî scriptable substrate-typed scalar read** ‚Äî closes the fragmentation where `inspect --field` was the legacy raw-storage path (`Poseidon2(name)`) and only the REPL `state` cmd handled substrate (`Blake3(self_address ‚Äñ field_name)` + typed decode). Same derivation + decoder as console `state` (extracted to a shared `state_decode` module so the vocabulary stays in lockstep), exposed as a `--json`-able one-shot for CI / deploy scripts. Focused mode: `--state-field` short-circuits the full account-snapshot path so it works against chains that don't yet expose `pyde_getAccount` / `pyde_getContractCode` (was the devnet's state at the time; closed in engine #247 shortly after). Output is contract addr / field declaration / slot key / raw bytes / decoded value. Mutually exclusive with the legacy `--field` (clap `conflicts_with`) ‚Äî they use different derivations for different contract conventions; mixing them in one call would be ambiguous. Help text on `--field` calls out that substrate authors want `--state-field` instead. **Tests**: 15 unit tests in the shared `state_decode` module (every primitive branch + Blake3 derivation invariants); console-smoke gains 6 inspect assertions (`<unset>` success path, unknown-field error, map-field error, `--field`/`--state-field` mutual-exclusion clap rejection); 31 / 31 smoke assertions green; `make e2e` stays fully green; no regression in the legacy `--field` consumers (the field-name ‚Üí Poseidon2 ‚Üí raw-hex path unchanged). ‚Äî PR [otigen#146](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/146)
- [x] **`pyde::call::execute_delegate_raw` ‚Äî type-erased proxy forwarders** ‚Äî closes the proxy-author footgun where the typed `execute_delegate::<T>` wrapper was unusable for `forward(function, calldata) -> Vec<u8>` dispatchers (the proxy doesn't know each logic function's return shape at compile time, can't pick a concrete `T`) and authors fell back to hand-rolling 25 lines of `pyde::raw::delegate_call` boilerplate ‚Äî buffer sizing, status check, revert-payload extraction, UTF-8 fallback, truncate. New `pyde::call::execute_delegate_raw(target, function, calldata) -> Result<Vec<u8>, CallError>` shares all of that path with `execute_delegate<T>` (refactor: shared `execute_inner_raw` returning `Vec<u8>`; all four typed wrappers ‚Äî `execute`, `execute_with_value`, `execute_static`, `execute_delegate` ‚Äî call it then borsh-decode), public API surface unchanged. Migrated the `upgradeable-proxy` example's `forward()`: ~25 lines of manual FFI ‚Üí 4-arm match on `CallError`. `CallError::Reverted` passes the logic's revert string straight through (so the proxy's caller sees exactly what the logic said, not a generic "proxy failed"); `CallError::InvalidFunction` surfaces "logic has no such function"; anything else generic-reverts. **Tests**: upgradeable-proxy e2e (20+ assertions including the bogus-function path that exercises `CallError::InvalidFunction`) stays green; `make e2e` across all 11 contracts stays green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#147](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/147)
- [x] **`otigen inspect <addr>` against a fresh devnet EOA ‚Äî first live coverage** ‚Äî engine #247 landed `pyde_getAccount` + `pyde_getContractCode` on the devnet RPC catalog matching the exact wire shape the otigen-rpc wrappers were already typed against. Wires the default-mode `inspect` path into console-smoke: 6 new assertions on a prefund EOA cover address echo, `Account type: eoa`, fresh nonce 0, hex-encoded prefund balance (`0x2540be400` = 10¬π‚Å∞ quanta), code size = 0. Smoke up to 37 / 37 assertions; `make e2e` stays fully green. The contract-account path remains pending ‚Äî `pyde_getContractCode` returns empty bytes for deployed contracts even though `pyde_getAccount` reports a valid `code_hash` for the same address; addendum ask filed (`/tmp/ENGINE_ASK_devnet_rpc_batch.md`) covering the bug plus two new methods (`pyde_getLogs`, `pyde_resolveName`). ‚Äî PR [otigen#148](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/148)
- [x] **`make e2e-soak` ‚Äî single-node devnet sustained-load regression-floor** ‚Äî captures hard numbers we can cite for the end-to-end submit ‚Üí admit ‚Üí drain ‚Üí execute ‚Üí receipt loop holding together under sustained load, without the usual hand-wavy "X TPS" claim. Boots a fresh devnet, deploys counter-rust, spawns N concurrent worker threads each driving K sequential `increment()` txs from a distinct prefunded wallet (per-sender receipt-wait between submissions so nonces advance cleanly), then asserts the counter slot equals N √ó K with zero reverts. **Headline (10 √ó 100 = 1000 txs, M2 / 16GB, 2026-06-06)**: cold deploy 3.2s; 1000 txs total wall-clock 318.43s; aggregate 3.1 tx/s end-to-end; per-tx p50 / p95 / p99 / max = 3120 / 3140 / 4133 / 4168 ms; success rate 1000 / 1000. **NOT a Pyde TPS claim** ‚Äî bounded by wave-commit cadence √ó per-sender receipt-wait, not by chain capacity (real chain throughput from engine PRs #142 + #144 microbenches: admit 31.6K/s, execute 17.8K tx/s, combined ~11.4K tps single-threaded, aligning with [[honest_throughput_reset]]'s 10-30K plaintext target). Originally landed as `make perf-baseline`; renamed in the same arc to `make e2e-soak` so the directory + Makefile target match the actual scope (`fuzz-soak` family naming, regression-floor framing). README opens with a prominent ‚öÝÔ∏è banner pointing readers at the engine microbench numbers as the citable chain-throughput figures. Two presets: `make e2e-soak` (full 10√ó100, ~6 min) and `make e2e-soak-smoke` (10√ó30, ~2 min); both intentionally outside `make e2e` because too slow for per-merge. ‚Äî PRs [otigen#149](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/149) (harness) + [otigen#150](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/150) (rename + strengthen anti-misuse framing)
- [x] **`otigen inspect <contract-addr>` + `<name>` ‚Äî live coverage of the engine #250 batch** ‚Äî closes the otigen-side consumption gap for the three RPCs landed in engine PR #250 (`pyde_getContractCode` bugfix + `pyde_getLogs` + `pyde_resolveName`). Three new console-smoke assertion groups: (a) **contract-account inspect** deploys counter-rust via devnet-9 (chosen so devnet-0 / devnet-1 ‚Äî the addresses the console assertions hard-code ‚Äî keep their fresh balance + nonce-0 shape), then `otigen inspect <contract-addr>` asserts exit 0, `Account type: contract`, `Code size: 5076 bytes` (pinned exactly so future bundle-shape drift surfaces here), `Code hash: 0xf2e1c7b2‚Ä¶` ‚Äî proves `pyde_getContractCode` returns the actual wasm bytes (was empty pre-engine#250); (b) **inspect by name** resolves `counter-rust` through `pyde_resolveName` to the same contract address, asserts address + account type match the by-address inspect; (c) **negative name path** ‚Äî unregistered name exits non-zero with `NameNotFound` diagnostic. Shell wrapper grows a build + deploy step before invoking the Python; the address is forwarded as a third `argv`. 47 / 47 console-smoke green (was 37, +10 new); `make e2e` across all 12 contract suites stays fully green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#151](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/151)
- [x] **`otigen console events <addr> [--from N] [--to N] [--limit N]` ‚Äî Phase 3 #8** ‚Äî wraps engine #250's `pyde_getLogs` in the REPL so authors can pull a contract's event log without dropping out to curl or scripting around the typed `Client::get_logs` wrapper. Address argument resolves through the shared `resolve_target` (hex or registered name). Renders each entry as a `(wave_id, tx_index, event_index)` coordinate plus contract / topics table / data; if the response is paginated (server clipped at `limit`), prints the cursor + a hint to re-query with `--from <next_wave>`. Empty pages render as `(no events matching filter)` so authors aren't left wondering whether the call silently failed. Flag parser is order-independent and rejects missing values, duplicate flags, unknown flags (topic filtering is a v2 ask), and non-numeric values. **Tests**: 7 unit tests on `parse_events_flags` covering every rejection branch; console-smoke gains 4 new assertions (help catalog lists `events <addr>`; success path against counter-rust renders `(no events matching filter)`; unknown-name surfaces `address resolution failed`; bad-flag surfaces `unknown flag`; REPL stays alive across all error paths). 51 / 51 console-smoke green (was 47); 19 / 19 console unit tests (was 12); `make e2e` stays green. Closes the "Deferred" line in the earlier otigen#136 console roadmap entry. ‚Äî PR [otigen#152](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/152)
- [x] **`examples/amm-uniswap-v2` ‚Äî constant-product AMM, Uniswap V2 math** ‚Äî canonical DEX reference example demonstrating the substrate idiom an actual on-chain market maker needs: two-token reserves bound once at init, an LP-share balance map derived from `sqrt(reserve_a * reserve_b)` on the first deposit and pro-rata thereafter, cross-contract calls into ERC20s for the underlying transfers (`transfer_from` on the pull side, `transfer` on the payout side), and a constant-product swap with the 30 bps Uniswap V2 fee. Surface: `reserve_a` / `reserve_b` / `lp_total_supply` / `lp_balance_of` views; `quote_swap(amt_in, a_to_b)` for pinning `min_out` before signing; `add_liquidity(amt_a, amt_b)`; `remove_liquidity(lp_amt)` (amounts paid out surfaced via the `LiquidityRemoved` event, since the v1 ABI caps function outputs at one); `swap_exact_in(amt_in, min_out, a_to_b)` with explicit slippage protection. **e2e harness** (`make e2e-amm`): 27 assertions green against a fresh devnet covering happy-path liquidity / swap / remove plus the negative paths (missing approve reverts; `min_out` > live quote reverts cleanly with reserves untouched). The two erc20 sides reuse the canonical `erc20-token` wasm via two thin name-only manifests under `tests/` ‚Äî same blake3 bytes, distinct chain-side names so a second deploy lands cleanly alongside the first. `make e2e` across all 13 contract suites stays fully green. ‚Äî PR [otigen#167](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/167)
- [x] **`otigen devnet` ‚Äî embed the chain runtime, drop the second binary** ‚Äî collapses the "download two binaries" friction that was the single biggest UX cost in the toolchain story. The chain runtime is now linked into `otigen-cli` via a path-dep on `pyde-engine-node`; the `devnet` subcommand builds a `DevnetRunConfig`, stands up a tokio runtime, and blocks on `pyde_engine_node::devnet::run_devnet_until_ctrl_c`. The pre-existing `--engine-bin` / `PYDE_BIN` resolution is dropped ‚Äî there's no external process to resolve. Validator and full-node roles still ship via the engine's own `pyde` binary (operator concerns, not author concerns). **Binary cost**: 28 MB ‚Üí 40 MB release-stripped; build graph absorbs the engine workspace's transitive deps (consensus, dkg, mempool, net, slashing, state, tx, wasm-exec, plus rocksdb / wasmtime / libp2p / axum); cold check 2m38s, incremental rebuild ~7s on the reference machine. **Tests**: 4 new unit tests in `commands::devnet::tests` cover the `--fork` / `--prefund-*` mutual-exclusion + `--rpc-listen` parser; 132/132 otigen-cli unit tests pass; `cargo fmt -p otigen-cli --check` + `cargo clippy -p otigen-cli -- -D warnings` clean; live smoke against the embedded chain ‚Äî `otigen devnet --rpc-listen 127.0.0.1:9934` boots, `pyde_chainId` returns `0x7a69`, Ctrl-C cleans up; erc20-token + amm-uniswap-v2 e2e ALL PASS unchanged through the new in-process devnet. `examples/_e2e_lib.sh` swapped from spawning `$ENGINE_BIN devnet ...` to `${OTIGEN[@]} devnet ...`. ‚Äî PR [otigen#168](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/168)

#### Œ±.live ‚Äî Live tests (blocked on MC-2 devnet)

- [ ] `otigen deploy` against a running devnet ‚Äî end-to-end transaction submission + receipt fetch
- [x] `otigen inspect` against a deployed contract on the devnet ‚Äî closed by otigen#151 (console-smoke deploys counter-rust via devnet-9, asserts `Account type: contract` + `Code size: 5076 bytes` + `Code hash: 0xf2e1c7b2‚Ä¶` against the real chain-side `pyde_getAccount` + `pyde_getContractCode` outputs)

- [x] Multi-validator stress: deploy + call from 7 distinct keystore identities concurrently ‚Äî `examples/multi-sender-stress/tests/run_e2e.sh` boots `pyde devnet`, deploys `counter-rust` via `devnet-0`, then drives `devnet-1`..`devnet-7` through `otigen call <addr> increment --from devnet-N` concurrently via Python `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor`. Three assertions all-pass on first real run: all 7 receipts `status="success"` (queried via `pyde_getTransactionReceipt` to bypass any drift in otigen's stdout banner), counter slot final value = 7 via `pyde_call(get)` (no dropped txs / no double-counted increments), all 7 senders' nonces advanced 0 ‚Üí 1 via `pyde_getTransactionCount` (per-sender nonce-window state holds under concurrent load). Catches concurrent mempool admission, wave-commit ordering across distinct senders, per-sender nonce advancement, and counter-slot finality ‚Äî none of which the single-sender acceptance suites exercise. Wired into `make e2e` as `e2e-multi-sender-stress` after the console smoke; ~12 contracts √ó ~290+ assertions in the full suite now. ‚Äî PR [otigen#144](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/144)

**Œ± BAR (production-ready):** every checkbox in `Œ±.feat`, `Œ±.qual`, and `Œ±.live` ticked; CI green on every platform; fuzz targets have run ‚â•24h cumulative with no surviving crashes; two independent builds of the canonical hello-rust produce byte-identical artifacts; performance baselines committed and tracked on every PR.

**Œ± BAR (pre-devnet, demonstrable today as of pyde-net/otigen#5):** ‚úÖ ‚Äî the `init ‚Üí cargo build ‚Üí otigen build ‚Üí bundle` flow is exercised end-to-end by `tests/hello_rust_e2e.rs` against the real Rust toolchain. The full BAR adds the `Œ±.qual` quality gate plus the `Œ±.live` devnet items.

### MC-1 Stream Œ≤ ‚Äî Engine Execution `[PAR within] ‚Üí MC-0` ‚Äî `pyde-net/engine` branch `execution-side`

Implements [`HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC.md`](companion/HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC.md) (chain side), Chapter 4, PIPs 2/3/4.

**Crates owned:** `account`, `state`, `tx`, `wasm-exec`, `mempool`.

#### Œ≤.1 `state` crate `[SEQ within Œ≤]` ‚Äî foundational
- [x] RocksDB scaffold + seven column families declared (`state_cf`, `jmt_cf`, `events_cf`, `events_by_topic_cf`, `events_by_contract_cf`, `wave_commits_cf`, `code_cf` ‚Äî last added in Œ≤.4 PR-19 for persistent WASM bytecode); `StateStore` + `StateConfig` + open/close lifecycle. Foundation for the items below. ‚Äî PR [#34](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/34) + PR [#115](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/115)
- [x] Dual-hash JMT (Blake3 for internal nodes via `jmt::SimpleHasher`; Poseidon2 reserved on `HybridJmtHasher` for the state-root + address-derivation surfaces per Chapter 4 ¬ß4.1). `PersistentJmt` exposes `update / get / root_hash_option / leaf_count` over `jmt_cf`. ‚Äî PR [#35](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/35)
- [x] Two-table architecture: `state_cf` (flat `slot_hash ‚Üí value`) + `jmt_cf` (versioned tree). `StateCommitter::commit` writes both CFs in one RocksDB `WriteBatch` (atomic across families); live reads via `StateStore::read_slot` (single `state_cf` get, JMT not consulted). ‚Äî PR [#38](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/38)
- [x] PIP-2 clustered slot keys (contract-prefix layout). `slot_key.rs` ships `account_meta_key`, `storage_slot_key`, `map_entry_key`, `nested_map_entry_key`, `system_key` over `address[..16] || Poseidon2(...)[..16]`. PIP graduated Draft ‚Üí Accepted in [pyde-net/pips#1](https://github.com/pyde-net/pips/pull/1); validation bench at `crates/state/benches/clustered_keys.rs`. ‚Äî PR [#38](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/38)
- [x] PIP-3 wave-level state prefetch (state-side). `prefetch_slots(store, &[SlotHash])` issues one `multi_get_cf` against `state_cf`; dedup + 10K-slot budget cap; per-key errors warn-logged and swallowed. Validation bench at `crates/state/benches/prefetch.rs`. PIP graduated Draft ‚Üí Accepted in [pyde-net/pips#2](https://github.com/pyde-net/pips/pull/2). The tx-pipeline wire-up that calls this primitive before wave dispatch is deferred to Œ≤.3. ‚Äî PR [#41](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/41)
- [x] PIP-4 write-back cache (DashMap + warm window + lazy flush). PIP graduated Draft ‚Üí Accepted in [pyde-net/pips#3](https://github.com/pyde-net/pips/pull/3) with the "JMT writes are lazy too" resolution baked in (cache spans `state_cf` + `jmt_cf` via parallel `JmtPendingQueue`). Shipped across 5 PRs.
  - [x] **PR-5a** primitives ‚Äî `CacheStore`, `CacheEntry`, `EntryState` machine, `JmtPendingQueue` ‚Äî landed in PR [#44](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/44)
  - [x] **PR-5b** read-path integration ‚Äî `StateStore::read_slot` now does cache ‚Üí `state_cf` ‚Üí None with cache-fill on disk hit (no fill on miss); gains `wave_id: WaveId` parameter for `last_read_at_wave` tracking. Landed in PR [#46](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/46)
  - [x] **PR-5c** write-path integration ‚Äî `StateCommitter::commit` now writes slot values to `CacheStore` (Dirty / tombstone) + enqueues the wave's `TreeUpdateBatch` on `JmtPendingQueue`. No RocksDB writes per wave. New `CacheAwareJmtReader` lets `put_value_set` see preceding unflushed waves' tree state. `CacheEntry.value` becomes `Option<SmallVec>` to distinguish tombstones from empty values. Landed in PR [#48](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/48)
  - [x] **PR-5d** background flush task ‚Äî `flush_once` is the atomic cross-CF drain primitive (snapshots dirty cache + drains JMT pending queue ‚Üí single RocksDB `WriteBatch` ‚Üí Pending ‚Üí Clean on ack). `FlushPolicy` + `should_flush` hold the three-signal trigger logic (100K dirty / 5s wall clock / 16 waves). `FlushTaskHandle::spawn` runs a tokio loop polling on a 100 ms tick; `shutdown().await` runs a final flush and returns cumulative `FlushStats`. Auto-tune is a no-op stub for v1; fixed-threshold defaults match PIP-4. Landed in PR [#54](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/54)
