  - [x] **PR-5e** crash recovery ‚Äî `last_flushed_wave` checkpoint persisted in `jmt_cf` under a new `TAG_META = 0x03` (written in the same atomic `WriteBatch` as the flush data, so partial-flush is structurally impossible). `StateStore::last_flushed_wave()` exposes it; `recovery::replay_wave` re-runs a historical wave through the cache + JMT layer. `kill_9` integration test exercises the full PIP-4 ¬ß"Crash recovery" flow against a synthetic chain log. Chain-log walking itself (extracting per-wave updates from the consensus log) lives at higher layers ‚Äî Œ≤.3/Œ≤.4/Œ≥. Landed in PR [#55](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/55)
- [x] events_cf + events_by_topic_cf + events_by_contract_cf (per `HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß15.3`). New `EventsBuffer` on `StateStore`; `StateCommitter::commit_with_events` enqueues per-wave events; `flush_once` drains the buffer alongside cache + JMT into the same atomic `WriteBatch` (5 CFs land together or none does). Query helpers in `events.rs`: `events_for_wave`, `events_for_topic` (prefix scan + primary fetch with `from..=to` + limit), `events_for_contract` (same shape). An event with N topics writes N rows to the topic index per ¬ß15.3. Landed in PR [#57](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/57)
- [x] **Atomic wave-commit ‚Äî cross-DB log-then-flush ordering + bounded flush primitive + wave-committer wire-up** ‚Äî the original framing ("WriteBatch across state + events + wave commit record in one transaction") assumed a single RocksDB instance; the architecture split into two ‚Äî `state_store` (state_cf + jmt_cf + events CFs + last-flushed checkpoint) and `consensus_store` (waves_cf + receipts_cf + txs_cf + slasher/escrow/finality CFs) ‚Äî so a literal cross-DB `WriteBatch` is impossible. The correctness property the line wanted ("a crash mid-commit leaves the chain at either wave N or wave N+1, never torn") IS achievable via cross-DB log-then-flush sequencing; this is the ticket that closes that out. **The invariant**: state never advances past the chain log. For every wave `w` durable in `state_store.last_flushed_wave`, `consensus_store.waves_cf` MUST contain a `WaveCommitRecord` at key `w`. Crash recovery walks `waves_cf` forward and replays from `state_store.last_flushed_wave() + 1`. **State crate**: `CacheStore::mark_dirty_as_pending_up_to(max_wave)` filters dirty entries by `written_at_wave`; `flush_once_up_to(store, max_wave)` is the bounded variant of `flush_once` (which is now `flush_once_up_to(WaveId::MAX)`). **Node crate**: new `wave_commit_atomic.rs` ships `commit_wave_atomically(state, consensus, wave_id, updates, events, build_record)` orchestrating phase 1 (in-memory state apply via `StateCommitter`) ‚Üí phase 2 (durable `consensus_store.put_wave` to waves_cf) ‚Üí phase 3 (bounded `flush_once_up_to`). `AtomicCommitError` documents per-phase failure semantics; `flush_state_up_to_committed(state, consensus)` is the convenience for the background flush task. **Production wire-up**: `WaveCommitter::commit_wave` now calls `pyde_engine_state::flush_once_up_to(state_store, wave_id)` immediately after a successful `consensus_store.put_wave` when the `DevnetState` carries a real `StateStore` (via `with_contract_support`). Bounded by the just-logged wave so the cross-DB invariant holds even if a background flush is racing. Errors are logged at error level ‚Äî the wave's record is durable; cache holds the writes; recovery replays on next boot if the flush never completes. `DevnetState::state_store()` accessor + `WaveCommitter::for_test_with_state` constructor expose enough surface for tests to exercise the wired path against a real RocksDB. **Tests**: 4 unit tests in `wave_commit_atomic` cover happy path, simulated put_wave failure, flush-up-to-committed picking up the chain log's high-water mark, and the killer scenario (an out-of-order unbounded flush with uncommitted writes stays behind the log via the cap); 1 integration test in `wave_committer` pinning the wire-up (`tick_with_wired_state_store_advances_last_flushed_wave_after_put_wave`). Workspace 1861 passed, 0 failed. Clippy clean. ‚Äî PR [#235](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/235)
- [x] events_root (Blake3 binary Merkle) + events_bloom (256-byte, 3-hash) computation. `compute_events_root` and `compute_events_bloom` in `events.rs`; both pure functions over `&[EventRecord]`, deterministic, reproduced exactly on crash-recovery replay. `StateCommitter::commit_with_events` now returns `WaveCommitment { state_root, events_root, events_bloom }` ‚Äî the trio consensus signs in the `HardFinalityCert`. `events_bloom` wraps `EventsBloom::insert_digest` from the types crate (state crate brings blake3; types crate preserves its leaf-dep invariant). Landed in PR [#59](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/59)
- [x] Implement `StateView` + `StateMutator` traits (from `interfaces`) ‚Äî partial impl on `StateStore`. Wired through: `StateView::get_slot` ‚Üí `StateStore::read_slot` at `last_flushed_wave`, `StateView::state_root` ‚Üí `PersistentJmt::root_hash_option` (Blake3 only; Poseidon2 surface stays zero until the `HybridJmtHasher` Poseidon2 output is exposed), and `StateMutator::snapshot` ‚Üí opaque `SnapshotHandle` keyed by `last_flushed_wave` (chunks reached via `Snapshotter::build` directly). Account-shaped reads (`get_balance` / `get_nonce_window` / `get_auth_keys` / `get_code` / `get_code_hash` / `get_account_type`) return `InterfaceError::NotImplemented` until Œ≤.2 ships the account encoding; `commit_wave` / `rollback_wave` return `NotImplemented` until Œ≤.4 (wasm-exec) wires through `StateCommitter::commit_with_events` at MC-2. Landed in PR [#62](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/62)
- [x] Snapshot generation (chunks + manifest). `Snapshotter::build` walks `state_cf` under a pinned `rocksdb::Snapshot` at `last_flushed_wave`, partitions entries into `SnapshotChunk`s of configurable size (default 1024), and produces a `SnapshotManifest` with `wave_id`, `state_root`, per-chunk Blake3 hashes, and `total_keys`. State-sync consumers fetch the manifest first, stream chunks in order (hashes verify chunk integrity), rebuild a fresh JMT, and confirm the recomputed root matches the manifest's `state_root` (which the committee signed in the wave's `HardFinalityCert`). Per-chunk JMT inclusion proofs deferred to v2 (rebuild-and-compare is correct and simpler for v1). Landed in PR [#61](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/61)
- [x] `code_cf` persistent WASM bytecode storage ‚Äî `Cf::Code` + `CODE_CF = "code_cf"` keyed by `Blake3Hash` (32 BE bytes), value = raw WASM bytes (10-200 KB typical, ‚â§16 MB cap per spec). Written by the Deploy tx handler at contract-creation time so cold-restart nodes can re-compile every contract's WASM into the wasm-exec `ModuleCache`. `StateStore::store_code(hash, bytes)` synchronous write (small + rare; per unique contract). `StateStore::get_code(hash) -> Option<Vec<u8>>` used by cold-restart + the StateView trait's get_code (previously `NotImplemented` stub, now wired through). `StateStore::has_code(hash)` cheap existence check. wasm-exec gained `WasmExecutor::compile_and_persist(state, bytes)` one-shot (compile + cache + state.store_code) and `WasmExecutor::load_from_persistent(state, code_hash)` cold-restart loader (cache lookup; on miss fetch from code_cf + compile with debug_assert that recomputed hash matches lookup key). Append-only in v1 (contracts can't be undeployed); the byte-pun gap with `Account.code_hash` (Poseidon2 ‚Üí currently treated as Blake3 bytes at host fn boundary) is documented in `cross_call.rs` module docs as the next unification step. 11 tests (6 state + 5 wasm-exec). Unblocks Œ≤.4 PR-17 Deploy `NotImplemented` placeholder. Landed in PR [#115](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/115)

#### Œ≤.2 `account` crate `[PAR within Œ≤]`
- [x] On-disk `Account` record per Ch 11 ¬ß11.1 ‚Äî `address`, `nonce_window`, `balance`, `code_hash` (Poseidon2), `storage_root` (Blake3, kept zero in v1 per ¬ß11.11's single-global-JMT resolution), `account_type`, `auth_keys`, `gas_tank`, `key_nonce`. Constructors for EOA / Contract / System; `is_eoa` / `is_contract` / `is_system` / `has_code` accessors. Borsh layout pinned by a 144-byte all-zero-EOA test plus a bitmap-offset pin. The actual encoding adds 2 bytes vs the ¬ß11.1 summary text (which elides `NonceWindow.bitmap` but ¬ß11.4 requires it for replay protection) ‚Äî flagged in the module docs for a spec-text touch-up. Landed in PR [#64](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/64)
- [x] `AccountStore` ‚Äî PIP-2 bridge from account record to state slot storage. Allocates discriminator `0x10` (`ACCOUNT_RECORD`) under the account-crate's owned `0x10..=0x1F` namespace; `account_slot(addr) = addr[..16] || Poseidon2(0x10)[..16]` clusters every account's record by address prefix in RocksDB's lex order. `AccountStore::get` / `write` / `delete` thread borsh encode/decode through `StateStore`; field-level helpers (`balance`, `nonce_window`, `auth_keys`, `code_hash`, `storage_root`, `account_type`) match the state-crate `StateView::get_*` contracts so the state-side `NotImplemented` stubs (PR-9) can route through. One-blob-per-account encoding follows Ch 11 ¬ß11.1; per-field split deferred to v2. Landed in PR [#68](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/68)
- [x] `AccountStateView` ‚Äî full `StateView` + `StateMutator` impl over `&StateStore` that routes account-shaped reads through `AccountStore`. Closes the Œ≤.1 PR-9 `NotImplemented` stubs without forcing a state‚Üíaccount dep cycle (the impl lives in the account crate, which already depends on state). `AccountError` ‚Üí `InterfaceError` maps storage failures to retryable `Storage`, decode failures to non-retryable `Internal` ("corruption"). Callers pick: `StateStore` for slot-only access (cheap), `AccountStateView` for full account-shaped reads. `get_code` stays `NotImplemented` until code storage lands (separate slot family or `code_cf`); `commit_wave` / `rollback_wave` stay `NotImplemented` until Œ≤.4 ships the executor and MC-2 wires `WaveCommitRecord` storage. Landed in PR [#69](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/69)
- [x] 32-byte address derivation (`Poseidon2(falcon_pubkey)`) ‚Äî `eoa_address`, `create_address` (deployer ‚Äñ nonce_le, 40 B), `create2_address` (`0xFF` ‚Äñ deployer ‚Äñ salt ‚Äñ code_hash, 97 B), `system_address` (`Poseidon2(name_bytes)`). Distinct input lengths + `0xFF` prefix on CREATE2 give structural cross-path collision resistance; Poseidon2's 128-bit Goldilocks collision resistance handles random inputs. 14 unit tests cover determinism + per-field sensitivity + cross-path distinctness. Landed in PR [#65](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/65)
- [x] `AuthKeys` enum with `Single`, `MultiSig`, `Programmable` (Programmable v2-reserved) ‚Äî the wire-level enum lives in the (frozen) `types` crate; `Account::rotate_keys` is the record-bound helper: validates `new_keys` (NoSigners / TooManySigners / InvalidThreshold), swaps `auth_keys`, and saturating-increments `key_nonce` so in-flight signatures under the previous key fail inclusion (¬ß11.5 "Key rotation"). Programmable round-trips at the record layer for replay/state-sync survivability even though tx handlers reject it at v1. Landed in PR [#66](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/66)
- [x] 16-slot nonce window ‚Äî `NonceWindow` (base + 16-bit bitmap) lives in the frozen `types` crate; `Account::accepts_nonce` / `Account::commit_nonce` are the record-bound helpers per Ch 11 ¬ß11.4. Sole mutation path for the window from the account-crate layer. Landed in PR [#66](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/66)
- [x] Name registry as a system contract (ENS-style, unique names) ‚Äî bidirectional `name ‚Üî address` mapping at system slots `NAME_TO_ADDRESS=0x40` + `ADDRESS_TO_NAME=0x41` so wallets can display "pyde-treasury" without an external index. `validate_name` enforces ASCII alphanumeric + `-` + `_`, length 3..=64, no edge `-`/`_` (Unicode-look-alike protection). `register_name` writes both directions atomically; uniqueness enforced both ways; idempotent against same (name, address) re-registration. `unregister_name` atomic tombstone for v2 governance flows. No dedicated `NameRegister` tx-type in v1 ‚Äî Ch 11 ¬ß11.8's frozen 13-variant `TxType` has none; reachable only via genesis + future governance. Subdomain / expiry / resolver records / sale-transfer / squatting protection all deferred to v2. 17 tests including Unicode rejection + edge-char rules + cross-direction uniqueness. Landed in PR [#89](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/89)

#### Œ≤.3 `tx` crate `[PAR within Œ≤]`
- [x] Native tx types ‚Äî frozen `TxType` enum (`crates/types/src/tx.rs`) ships 14 variants (`0x00..=0x0E`); every variant has a handler wired through `WasmExecutorAdapter::execute_native` in `crates/wasm-exec/src/executor_impl.rs`. Original line listed pre-convergence names (`Transfer`, `ValidatorRegister`, `Stake`, `Unstake`, `NameRegister`, `Multisig`, `RotateKeys`); the spec collapsed these into the canonical names below. Per-type state-effect handlers under `crates/tx/src/handlers/`:
  - [x] **`Standard` (value-transfer half)** ‚Äî `handle_standard` runs the ¬ß10.1 charge-up-front / debit-after-execution pipeline: load sender ‚Üí `verify_tx_against_auth` dispatch ‚Üí nonce-in-window ‚Üí recipient code-hash check (contract-call path returns `HandlerError::ContractCallDeferred` until Œ≤.4) ‚Üí balance vs `value + gas_limit√óbase_fee` reservation ‚Üí debit fee `gas_used √ó base_fee` ‚Üí commit nonce ‚Üí move `value` sender‚Üírecipient (auto-creates `AuthKeys::None` funded-but-unregistered EOA per ¬ß11.8 row 13 if missing; self-transfer short-circuits the loop). Returns `HandlerOutput { gas_used, fee_distribution }` for wave-level fee aggregation. Per-tx fee crediting deferred (per ¬ß10.5 reward pool is lazy-accrued per-epoch + burn is a counter); vesting deferred (needs subsystem outside Œ≤.3). 17 tests across all 9 failure modes + happy path + self-transfer. Landed in PR [#77](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/77)
  - [x] `Deploy` ‚Äî PR [#137](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/137) lands the full flow in `WasmExecutorAdapter` (the only place with the WASM engine + state.store_code handles the sync Œ≤.3 handler signature doesn't expose). 10-step sequence: decode wasm ‚Üí `validate_deploy` (Œ≤.4 PR-16 schema + cross-ref + attrs) ‚Üí load deployer (sender-not-found reverts at MIN_GAS) ‚Üí derive CREATE address `Poseidon2(deployer ‚Äñ nonce_le)` ‚Üí reject collision ‚Üí balance check `value + gas_limit √ó base_fee` ‚Üí `compile_and_persist` (Œ≤.4 PR-19) atomic ModuleCache + code_cf write ‚Üí create `Account::Contract` with `code_hash` carrying the Blake3 bytes via the documented Poseidon2Hash byte-pun (Deploy is the natural place to close the cross_call unification gap) ‚Üí move value + debit gas + commit nonce ‚Üí Receipt with `return_data = contract_address.bytes`. Failure model: any step's revert charges `gas_used = MIN_GAS_LIMIT` (21K intrinsic floor) per `ReceiptStatus::Reverted` doc-comment ("state rolled back, gas still charged for work done"). Constructor function invocation (`constructor_index`) + Deploy events deferred ‚Äî Deploy validates the WASM but doesn't call any function (v2 will dispatch to `constructor_index` if set). 5 new tests (success creates contract + returns address + persists code + commits nonce + debits balance; empty-data reverts; invalid-WASM reverts; missing-sender reverts; insufficient-balance reverts). 200/200 wasm-exec tests passing.
  - **Staking trio per Ch 14 ¬ß14.5:**
    - [x] **`StakeDeposit`** + validator-registry primitive ‚Äî `ValidatorRecord` (operator, pubkey, stake, status, unbond_at_wave, last_claimed_rps, uptime_bps), Active/Unbonding/Exited status machine, system slots `REWARDS_PER_STAKE_UNIT=0x14` / `TOTAL_ACTIVE_STAKE_WEIGHTED=0x15` / `VALIDATOR_REGISTRY=0x20` / `OPERATOR_VALIDATORS=0x21`. Constants: `MIN_VALIDATOR_STAKE=10K PYDE`, `OPERATOR_CAP=3` (anti-Sybil), `UPTIME_FULL_BPS=10_000`. `handle_stake_deposit` derives validator_address = `eoa_address(data_pubkey)`, checks cap + no-duplicate + sig + balance + nonce, locks stake, writes record with **`last_claimed_rps = current_rps`** (critical: NOT 0 ‚Äî prevents draining via retroactive accrual). Bumps `TOTAL_ACTIVE_STAKE_WEIGHTED` by `stake √ó uptime / UPTIME_FULL_BPS`. `bootstrap_validator` genesis helper. 21 tests including the security-critical RPS-snapshot test. Landed in PR [#84](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/84)
    - [x] **`StakeWithdraw`** ‚Äî validator-self-signed (tx.from = validator_address, signed by `record.pubkey` installed at StakeDeposit time via the auto-create-validator-account retrofit). Active ‚Üí Unbonding transition, records `unbond_at_wave`, decrements `TOTAL_ACTIVE_STAKE_WEIGHTED` by the validator's stake√óuptime contribution. One-shot (double-withdraw rejected). Landed in PR [#86](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/86)
    - [x] **`ClaimReward`** ‚Äî validator-self-signed lazy-accrual claim per ¬ß14.5: `owed = (current_rps - last_claimed_rps) √ó stake √ó uptime / UPTIME_FULL_BPS`. Updates `last_claimed_rps` to current RPS after payout so a second claim only pays incremental delta. **Folds in the ¬ß14.5 "explicit follow-up" unbonding sweep**: when called past `unbond_at_wave + UNBONDING_PERIOD_WAVES` (= 5,184,000 = 30 days √ó 172,800 waves/day at 500 ms median), additionally refunds the stake to validator balance and transitions Unbonding ‚Üí Exited. No dedicated tx type for the sweep was named in the spec ‚Äî folding into ClaimReward is the cleanest fit. Exited validators that claim again get `ValidatorWrongStatus`. Landed in PR [#86](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/86)
  - [x] **`Slash` (safety-evidence partial scope)** ‚Äî `handle_slash` accepts `SafetyEvidence { offender, round, view, msg_a+sig_a, msg_b+sig_b, reporter? }` for DoubleSign / Equivocation. Validates both FALCON sigs against `record.pubkey`, confirms `msg_a != msg_b`, applies `SAFETY_SLASH_BPS=1000` (10%) slash, credits `REPORTER_REWARD_BPS=1000` (10%) to reporter (sender==reporter merged to avoid clobber; self-reporting blocked), burns the rest, transitions offender to `Exited`, decrements `TOTAL_ACTIVE_STAKE_WEIGHTED`. **Honestly deferred** (with rationale in module docs): liveness/DKG evidence (need consensus + Œ≥.3), 24h dispute escrow (needs governance multisig), escalating jail periods + repeat-offense scaling + correlation multiplier (need historical/cross-tx tracking), reporter cooldown, new-validator grace, DoubleSign 100%+ban distinction (treated as 10% Equivocation baseline in PR-12; v2 hardening with `BannedValidators` slot). 13 tests including frame-up-attack (claim address but sign with wrong key) + Exited-cannot-slash-again. Landed in PR [#87](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/87)
  - [x] **`ClaimAirdrop` / `SweepAirdrop`** ‚Äî closes the airdrop subsystem per Ch 14 ¬ß14.7. System slots: `AIRDROP_ROOT=0x18` (Poseidon2 Merkle), `AIRDROP_DEADLINE=0x19` (`WaveId`), `AIRDROP_CLAIMED=0x1A` (per-leaf-index `bool` ‚Äî one slot per leaf for v1 simplicity; v2 PIP can pack bits), `AIRDROP_EXPECTED_SUM=0x1B` (genesis sanity). Pool at `Poseidon2("pyde-airdrop-pool")`. Leaf hash = `Poseidon2(0x00 ‚Äñ leaf_index_le8 ‚Äñ address ‚Äñ amount_le16)`; sibling-side bit at level `i` = `(leaf_index >> i) & 1` (prevents sorted-pair attacks). ClaimAirdrop verifies the Merkle path for `(leaf_index, tx.from, amount)`, debits pool ‚Üí credits claimant, sets the claim bit. Gas: 30K + 5K √ó levels with **early-gas guard before state mutation** per the spec's "PR #212 fix" requirement. SweepAirdrop is permissionless (any sender) ‚Äî moves the pool's residual to the treasury after the deadline. `bootstrap_airdrop` genesis helper seeds the trio atomically. 16 tests including leaf-tamper + sibling-swap proof-forgery attacks. Landed in PR [#83](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/83)
  - [x] **`MultisigTx` / `RotateMultisig`** ‚Äî `handle_multisig_tx` (treasury spend) + `handle_rotate_multisig` (signer-set rotation) per ¬ß11.7. MultisigTx debits the treasury (at `treasury_address() = Poseidon2("pyde-treasury")`) and credits a target; bundle covers `borsh((target, amount))` so substituting target/amount post-sign fails verify. ¬ß11.7 invariants: `target != ZERO`, `target != treasury`, `target != tx.from` (pipeline-writeback clobber), `amount > 0`. Auto-creates the target as `AuthKeys::None` funded-but-unregistered EOA if missing. RotateMultisig replaces the signer set + threshold; bundle covers `borsh((new_signers, new_threshold))`; **nonce continues monotonically (never reset)** so a brief old-set compromise can't replay arbitrary old spend bundles after the rotation. `bootstrap_treasury` genesis helper seeds the treasury account; same canonical_msg + verify_bundle primitive reused from PR-7. New HandlerError variants: `MultisigEnvelopeShape { reason }` + `TreasuryUninitialised`. 27 tests across both handlers including payload-substitution attacks, replay-after-state-changed, post-rotation-old-sigs-no-longer-verify, multi-step rotation chain. Landed in PR [#81](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/81)
  - [x] **`EmergencyPause` / `EmergencyResume`** ‚Äî flip the on-chain `IS_PAUSED` slot (system-key discriminator `0xF3`) gated on a treasury-multisig FALCON-512 signature bundle. Ships with the multisig primitive prerequisite: `MultisigState { signers, threshold, nonce }` at system slots `MULTISIG_SIGNERS=0xF0` / `MULTISIG_THRESHOLD=0xF1` / `MULTISIG_NONCE=0xF2`; `BundleEntry` wire shape; `canonical_msg = Poseidon2(domain ‚Äñ nonce_le ‚Äñ Poseidon2(payload))` with per-tx-type domain bytes (MultisigTx 0x09 / RotateMultisig 0x0A / Pause 0x0B / Resume 0x0C ‚Äî separation prevents lifting a signature for one action into another); `verify_bundle` with cheap-path structural checks before any FALCON verify + short-circuit at threshold. Handlers do: load state ‚Üí decode bundle ‚Üí verify against canonical_msg(type, nonce, []) ‚Üí idempotency guard (must actually flip) ‚Üí set flag ‚Üí bump nonce. No gas, no fee ‚Äî multisig-signed protocol governance per ¬ß11.7. 35 tests across system_slots + multisig primitive + both handlers (replay-after-state-changed, all 4 transition guards, threshold short-circuit, duplicate-signer rejection). Landed in PR [#80](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/80)
  - [x] **`RegisterPubkey`** ‚Äî `handle_register_pubkey` per ¬ß11.8 row 13. Allowed only when account exists with `balance > 0` and `auth_keys == AuthKeys::None`. Data carries the 897-byte FALCON pubkey; proof-of-ownership is the `eoa_address(pubkey) == tx.from` derivation check (Poseidon2 preimage resistance ‚áí submitter holds the secret). No signature, no value, no gas ‚Äî the protocol gives the registration a free pass so the bootstrap path can't be blocked by empty balance. DoS bounded: at most one per address per lifetime; the funded-but-unregistered population is itself bounded by the funder's 21K-gas charge on the originating `Standard` transfer. One-shot install (key_nonce stays 0; subsequent changes use rotate-keys). 10 tests + Standard‚ÜíRegisterPubkey bootstrap integration. Landed in PR [#78](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/78)
  - [x] **`Unjail`** (`0x0E`) ‚Äî `handle_unjail` (`crates/tx/src/handlers/staking.rs:884`) transitions a `Jailed` validator back to `Active` once `wave_id >= jail_until` per [[slashing_rules_catalog]]. Validator-self-signed. Charges a fixed-fee anti-griefing burn on top of the standard `gas_used √ó base_fee` (constants in module docs). Stake remains escrowed throughout the jail period ‚Äî Unjail does not re-credit; it only flips status. Already-active or Exited validators are rejected with `ValidatorWrongStatus`. Dispatched via `executor_impl.rs:913`. Landed alongside the slashing-catalog wiring.
- [x] Contract execution surface ‚Äî chain converged on `Standard` (`to == <contract>`) + `Deploy` (`to == ZERO`) as the only two contract-facing tx types; no separate `ContractCall` / `ContractDeploy` variants exist on the frozen `TxType` enum. `Standard` routed to a contract address is decoded as `borsh(CallPayload { function, calldata })` by `handle_standard_contract_call` (engine [#223](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/223)); `Deploy` decodes as `DeployData` per the otigen-cli builders. The `pyde_call` RPC was unified onto the same `borsh(CallPayload)` envelope in engine [#226](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/226) so view + mutating dispatch share one wire shape end-to-end. Original line ("WASM tx types: `ContractCall`, `ContractDeploy`") predates the convergence ‚Äî kept here as a tombstone so anyone grepping the old framing lands on the correct mapping.
- [x] Contract lifecycle (pause / unpause / kill / upgrade) ‚Äî **v1 uses the proxy / `delegate_call` pattern; no chain-side lifecycle envelope.** The acceptance suite's `upgradeable-proxy` contract (otigen [#131](https://github.com/pyde-net/otigen/pull/131)) ships the canonical pattern: admin-gated `upgrade_to(new_logic)` swaps the proxy's logic pointer, `delegate_call` preserves the proxy's `self_address` so state survives the swap, logic contracts' own storage stays untouched. Per-contract `paused`/`killed` flags are contract-internal admin slots ‚Äî any author can declare them in `[state]` and gate entry points on them. Original line referenced `OTIGEN_BINARY_SPEC ¬ß8.2 / ¬ß8.3` which proposed first-class `UpgradeContractTx` / `PauseContractTx` / `UnpauseContractTx` / `KillContractTx` types; the spec section is now marked v2-deferred in-place. **Why deferred**: (a) chain-blessed contract ownership (`Account::Contract.owner`) competes with the deliberately-ownerless [[address-naming-collision]] model; (b) chain-level upgrade competes with the proxy pattern, which is more flexible (multiple-logic-versions, time-locked upgrades, governance-gated swaps all expressible in-contract); (c) chain-level pause/kill duplicates what authors can ship themselves with a 1-line slot. v2 may revisit if a governance use case earns the surface. **Cleanup follow-up (otigen-side)**: `otigen pause / unpause / kill / upgrade` CLI subcommands currently emit `Standard` + `borsh(LifecyclePayload)` which the chain decodes as `CallPayload` and reverts; rewrite or remove in a separate otigen ticket so authors aren't pointed at a broken path.
- [x] Canonical tx hashing ‚Äî `tx_hash = Poseidon2(chain_id ‚Äñ from ‚Äñ to ‚Äñ value ‚Äñ Poseidon2(data) ‚Äñ gas_limit ‚Äñ nonce ‚Äñ fee_payer_tag ‚Äñ Poseidon2(access_list) ‚Äñ deadline ‚Äñ tx_type)` per Ch 11 ¬ß11.6. `data` and `access_list` pre-hashed to bound outer permutation; signature NOT included (it signs the hash). **Roadmap originally said "Blake3" ‚Äî corrected to Poseidon2 here** because tx hashes cross the ZK boundary (light-client receipts, aggregated state proofs, future SNARK roll-ups). Tag encodings for `FeePayer` / `Option<deadline>` / `TxType` are spelt out, not just borsh-derived, to keep wire stability independent of derive output. Landed in PR [#71](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/71)
- [x] Tx signature verification ‚Äî `verify_tx_signature(tx, pubkey)` FALCON-512-verifies `Tx.signature` against the canonical `tx_hash`. `verify_tx_against_auth(tx, AuthKeys)` dispatches by variant: `Single` ‚Üí verify; `None` ‚Üí `Err(NoAuth)`; `Programmable` ‚Üí `Err(ProgrammableV1Reserved)` per ¬ß11.5 v1-reservation; `MultiSig` ‚Üí `Err(MultisigDeferred)` (multisig sigs travel inside the `MultisigTx` handler's `data` envelope, not `Tx.signature`). Graceful-false on malformed sig/pubkey rather than panic. 11 tests including keygen‚Üísign‚Üíverify round-trip + every dispatch path. Landed in PR [#74](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/74)
- [x] Gas accounting (EIP-1559 base fee; no refunds per `gas-no-refund-v1` memory) ‚Äî constants frozen per Ch 10 ¬ß10.2: GAS_TARGET=400M, GAS_CEILING=1.6B (4√ó), GENESIS_BASE_FEE=50e9 quanta, MIN_BASE_FEE=1, ADJUSTMENT_DIVISOR=8 (¬±12.5% per commit). `adjust_base_fee` applies the proportional bump/drop with min-1-quanta upward jolt + MIN_BASE_FEE floor. `compute_fee` uses `checked_mul` overflow guard. `distribute_fee` / `distribute_total` implement 70/20/10 burn/reward-pool/treasury with remainder-to-treasury rounding recovery (no quanta lost). Zero refunds (EIP-3529 lesson + PIP-4 handles state cleanup at the engine layer). 20 tests cover constants pin, adjustment edges (full 4√ó, slight-over, busy min-1, empty drop, MIN_BASE_FEE floor, ¬±12.5% cap), overflow guard, distribution spec examples (¬ß10.6 simple / high-congestion / low-demand) + dust-to-treasury. Landed in PR [#72](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/72)
- [x] Structural tx validators ‚Äî ingress-time `validate_tx_structure(tx)` runs the ¬ß10.9 limit checks (MIN_GAS_LIMIT=21K, BLOCK_GAS_MAX=1.6B, MAX_TX_SIZE=128 KiB, MAX_CALLDATA=64 KiB ‚Äî separate caps per audit task 055) plus ¬ß11.8 per-type shape rules: envelope-style `to == ZERO` for 10 affected types, empty-data for StakeWithdraw / ClaimReward / SweepAirdrop, non-empty data for Deploy / Slash / ClaimAirdrop / Multisig* / Emergency*, 897-byte FALCON pubkey for StakeDeposit + RegisterPubkey, the RegisterPubkey-only "no signature, no value" rule. Self-contained (no state access); `TxValidationError` per failure mode with actual/expected pairs for useful logs. 23 tests across all 11 invariant categories. Landed in PR [#75](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/75)
- [x] Deploy / upgrade / lifecycle handlers ‚Äî covered above under "Contract execution surface" (Deploy + Standard cover the two contract-facing flows the chain knows) + "Contract lifecycle (pause / unpause / kill / upgrade)" (v2-deferred; v1 uses the proxy / `delegate_call` pattern). `OTIGEN_BINARY_SPEC ¬ß8.2 / ¬ß8.3` rewritten in-place to reflect the v1 / v2 split.

#### Œ≤.4 `wasm-exec` crate `[SEQ within Œ≤] ‚Üí Œ≤.1`
- [x] wasmtime engine config (deterministic feature subset per Ch 3 ¬ß3.2) ‚Äî `deterministic_config()` builds `wasmtime::Config` with Cranelift at Speed opt, `consume_fuel=true`, `epoch_interruption=true`, `cranelift_nan_canonicalization=true` (cross-platform float determinism per Ch 3 ‚Äî x86 SSE2 vs ARM NEON quiet-NaN encoding diverges otherwise), `wasm_simd/relaxed_simd/multi_memory/memory64=false`, `wasm_bulk_memory=true`. Threads / reference-types / function-references / GC / component-model are off via the wasmtime cargo-feature gate (proposal not compiled in ‚Üí setter doesn't exist; the gate IS the off switch). 3 tests including AOT-output bit-equality across two engines. Landed in PR [#91](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/91). **Engine perf hardening (PR [#108](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/108))**: pinned `parallel_compilation(true)` (Cranelift's per-function worker-thread compile) + `memory_init_cow(true)` (initial linear-memory pages COW from data segments, skip per-instantiation memcpy) + `InstanceAllocationStrategy::Pooling` (pre-reserve slot tables ‚Äî per-tx `Store::new` drops from a ~100¬µs mmap-syscall path to ~1¬µs atomic counters + COW reset). Pool sized v1-realistic: 1024 instances/memories/tables, 4 MB per-instance max memory, 64 KB linear keep-resident, 4 KB table keep-resident. Critical kernel-budget pin: explicit `static_memory_maximum_size(POOL_MAX_MEMORY_SIZE)` so the per-slot virtual reservation matches the actual cap ‚Äî without this wasmtime reserves the default 4 GB per slot regardless, which √ó 1024 slots √ó per-engine = multiple TB and the OS rejects the mmap immediately. With the pin: 1024 √ó 4 MB = 4 GB virtual per Engine, fits 16 parallel cargo workers (= 64 GB total) comfortably. Pool cap is NOT a throughput knob ‚Äî per-`Store::new` speed is constant at any pool size; the cap is a guard against runaway-instantiation bugs (v1 single-thread √ó depth-32 cross-call peak is 33; 1024 = 32√ó headroom). v2 multi-thread will raise pool in lock-step with shrinking per-slot memory to stay under the VMA budget. Adds `pooling-allocator` to wasmtime cargo features. 2 new tests (constants pin + 64-iteration rapid instantiation).
- [x] `WasmExecutor` type ‚Äî engine-level handle that owns the singleton `wasmtime::Engine` + `ModuleCache`. Cheap to clone (both internally `Arc`'d), safe to share across wave-execution threads. Exposes `compile_and_cache(bytes) ‚Üí CodeHash` / `has_module(hash)` / `engine()` / `cache()`. Foundation type subsequent PRs extend with per-tx instance creation, host-fn bindings, and overlay. Landed in PR [#91](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/91)
- [x] Module cache: LRU + max-size + TTL (per `HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß3.6`) ‚Äî **LRU + max-size + TTL shipped; disk-spill + pre-warm deferred to v2.** PR [#119](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/119) replaces the basic `Arc<Mutex<HashMap>>` scaffold with `Arc<Mutex<LruCache<Blake3Hash, CacheEntry>>>` (using the `lru = "0.12"` crate). `CacheConfig { max_modules: NonZeroUsize, ttl: Option<Duration> }` defaults to 1024 modules / no TTL; overridable per node via `ModuleCache::with_config` or `WasmExecutor::with_cache_config` for memory-rich nodes / long-running validator TTL hygiene. **Eviction**: overflow at `max_modules` ‚Üí LRU evict on `compile_and_cache`; TTL (if set) ‚Üí evict on next `get` if `entry.inserted_at.elapsed() > ttl`; manual via `clear()`. **`contains()` is peek-only** ‚Äî does NOT touch LRU position (used by cross_call dispatch's `has_module` check so existence checks don't disturb the LRU). **`CacheStats { hits, misses, evictions, ttl_evictions }`** exposed via `stats()` for surfacing eviction pressure (high counters ‚Üí bump `max_modules` or enable TTL). **Disk-spill deferred to v2**: correctness already covered by `code_cf` re-compile path (PR-19); disk-spill of compiled modules (skipping Cranelift) is a v2 perf optimization needing versioned on-disk format pinned to `(wasmtime_version, cranelift_flags, host_arch)`. 9 cache tests (defaults / compile inserts / get bumps LRU + counters / miss counter / eviction at capacity / TTL eviction / contains-is-peek invariant / idempotent recompile / clear-keeps-stats). 194/194 wasm-exec tests passing.
- [x] Fuel-to-gas mapping (calibrated from spec ¬ß10 gas table) ‚Äî `FUEL_PER_GAS=1000` chain spec constant (hard fork to change). `gas_to_fuel` saturating multiply (caps for u64 safety; realistic gas ‚â§ BLOCK_GAS_MAX = 1.6 √ó 10‚Åπ stays well below saturation). `fuel_to_gas` **ceiling** divide (rounds UP ‚Äî floor-div would let attacker run FUEL_PER_GAS-1 fuel for free every tx; ceiling makes worst-case overcharge exactly 1 gas/tx, negligible against MIN_GAS_LIMIT=21K). `compute_consumed_gas(initial_fuel, remaining_fuel)` bundles saturating-sub + ceiling for the per-tx pipeline; clamps impossible `remaining > initial` to 0 consumed. Constant (not Config knob) so every node computes identical `gas_used` for identical txs ‚Äî per-node knob would fork consensus. 14 tests covering saturation, ceiling at every boundary, round-trip identity, pathological u64::MAX. Landed in PR [#92](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/92)
- [x] Per-tx overlay execution model (snapshot-and-rollback; nested for cross-call) ‚Äî `TxOverlay` wraps `&AccountStore` and maintains a stack of `OverlayLayer` frames. Reads scan layers top-down then fall through to the underlying store; writes go to the top layer. `push_layer` on cross-call entry; `pop_and_commit` merges sub-call writes into parent on success; `pop_and_discard` drops them on revert. `finalize` flattens the stack and applies all writes to the store (accounts via `AccountStore::write`, slots via `StateCommitter::commit`); drop-without-finalize is the tx-level revert path (underlying store untouched). Tombstones encoded as `Option<None>` slot values that mask deeper layers + the store. `BTreeMap` for write buffers (deterministic finalize order ‚Äî wave-commits must be reproducible across nodes for state-root consensus). Three error variants (`OverlayUnderflow` / `OverlayLayersUnclosed` / `OverlayBackend`) guard the call sequence. 21 tests cover read fall-through, overlay shadowing, slot tombstones, push/pop balance, commit/discard, nested layer composition, underflow rejection, and finalize success/error paths. Landed in PR [#94](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/94)
- [x] Per-tx Store + Linker + entry-point dispatch ‚Äî `HostContext` is plain owned data (BlockContext + TxContext + self_address + depth + in-flight `EmittedEvent` buffer); kept lifetime-free because wasmtime requires `T: Send + Sync + 'static` for `Store<T>` (overlay borrow would force lifetime-erasing tricks that aren't worth their cost until storage host fns actually need it ‚Äî PR-7 picks the trait-object shape then). `linker::build_linker` builds a fresh `Linker<HostContext>` per tx (microsecond cost; sharing across txs deferred until profiling justifies it). `WasmExecutor::execute_call(code_hash, entry_point, ctx)` ties it together: cache lookup ‚Üí linker build ‚Üí `Store::new` with fuel-seeded budget from `gas_to_fuel(tx.gas_limit)` + `set_epoch_deadline(u64::MAX)` (epoch interruption is enabled at engine level as a cancellation primitive; gas/fuel is the sole stopping mechanism here) ‚Üí instantiate ‚Üí entry-point invoke ‚Üí trap capture (walks `wasmtime::Error::source()` chain so host-fn-produced messages survive past the top-level "wasm backtrace" wrapper) ‚Üí `compute_consumed_gas` ‚Üí `CallOutcome { consumed_gas, trap, events }`. PR-4 supports only void-void entry points (full ABI dispatch in a later PR). Ships `pyde::panic` as a plumbing-exercise host fn (returns ptr/len as trap message; full memory-decode helper lands in PR-5a). Three new error variants: `HostFn` / `EntryPointMissing` / `Runtime`. 13 tests: HostContext construction + event push, panic register success + duplicate rejection, execute_call for void return + unknown module + missing entry point + unreachable trap + pyde::panic call + out-of-fuel + minimal-gas no-op. Landed in PR [#95](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/95)
- [ ] Host functions ‚Äî each independent task:
  - [x] Storage: `sload`, `sstore`, `sdelete` (with access-list enforcement) ‚Äî three host fns sharing the standard `(slot_ptr, ..., wave_id)` shape. Required infra: `HostContext` gained an `overlay: Option<Arc<Mutex<TxOverlay>>>` slot via `with_overlay` builder (Option keeps existing test surface untouched; storage host fns trap with `"storage host fn called without overlay backend"` if invoked without one) AND the Œ≤.2 `AccountStore<'a>` + Œ≤.4 `TxOverlay<'a>` types were Arc-refactored across 50+ test fixtures to drop their lifetime params so the Arc<Mutex<...>> handle could live inside the 'static-shaped HostContext that wasmtime's `Store<T>` requires (PR [#103](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/103)). `sload(slot_ptr, out_ptr, out_max_len) -> i32` reads via `TxOverlay::read_slot` (top-down layer scan + tombstone awareness), writes `min(actual, out_max_len)` bytes to `out_ptr`, returns actual length; returns `SLOAD_MISSING = -1` for missing slot (distinct from length-0 value). `sstore` buffers `(slot, value)` to the top overlay layer; `MAX_STORAGE_VALUE_BYTES = 16 KB` pre-allocation guard. `sdelete` writes a tombstone ‚Äî per PIP-4 gas-no-refund: NO refund for deletes, sdelete metered like any host fn. Gas (EVM-shape): `GAS_SLOAD = 100 + 1/byte` copy, `GAS_SSTORE_BASE = 5_000 + 32/byte` value, `GAS_SDELETE = 5_000`. Warm-cold gap + zero-nonzero premium deferred to v2. Access-list enforcement (PIP-2 spec calls it out) is a wave-orchestrator concern ‚Äî it pre-validates that the slot keys a tx will touch are in the tx's `access_list` before the tx runs; the host fns themselves don't enforce because they have no `&Tx`. v2 hardening. 8 end-to-end tests via in-WASM unreachable assertions (sstore + sload round-trip, sload-missing returns -1, sdelete makes subsequent sload return -1, sstore oversize trap, storage-without-overlay trap) + 3 unit tests (register + duplicate + constants pin). Landed in PR [#104](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/104)
  - [x] Balances: `balance`, `transfer` ‚Äî `pyde::balance(addr_ptr, out_ptr) -> ()` reads the 32-byte address, looks up via `TxOverlay::read_account` (overlay-first, falls through to underlying `AccountStore`), writes 16-byte u128 LE balance to `out_ptr` (0 for missing accounts). `pyde::transfer(to_ptr, amount_ptr) -> i32` reads recipient + u128 amount, then: self-transfer short-circuits to `TRANSFER_OK = 1` (avoids writeback-clobber pattern from standard tx handler); otherwise loads self, checks `balance >= amount` (returns `TRANSFER_INSUFFICIENT = 0` on shortfall), debits self, loads or auto-creates recipient as `AuthKeys::None` funded-unregistered EOA per ¬ß11.8 row 13, credits recipient (overflow check), writes both back. Binary success/insufficient flag matches EVM `CALL`'s value-transfer semantics ‚Äî natural failure case isn't a trap; overflow on the credit IS a trap because it's a programmer bug. Both fns require HostContext.overlay; trap with `"balance host fn called without overlay backend"` if absent. Gas matches EVM: `GAS_BALANCE = 700` (post-EIP-1884 BALANCE; full account-blob fetch), `GAS_TRANSFER = 9_000` (two BALANCE reads + cross-account-write coordination). 9 tests via in-WASM unreachable assertions (balance-unknown returns 0, balance-seeded LE bytes verified, self-transfer short-circuits, insufficient-balance returns 0, transfer-credits-recipient end-to-end with 1000‚Üí100 transfer + recipient balance read-back, balance-without-overlay traps) + 3 unit tests (register + duplicate + constants pin). Landed in PR [#106](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/106)
  - [x] Context: `caller`, `origin`, `self_address`, `block_height`, `wave_id`, `block_timestamp`, `chain_id` ‚Äî shipped alongside the shared `mem::{caller_memory, write_to_memory, read_from_memory}` linear-memory I/O helpers (bounds-checked against the contract's exported `"memory"`; reused by every subsequent host fn). Address-shaped fns (`caller`, `origin`, `self_address`) write 32 bytes to a contract-supplied `out_ptr`; scalar fns (`wave_id`, `block_height`, `block_timestamp`, `chain_id`) return `i64`. `block_height` aliases `wave_id` for EVM-shape ABI portability. `caller` returns `tx.from` at the top-level call (cross-call PR pushes a per-frame caller stack later). Per-call gas charged via `Caller::get_fuel + set_fuel` (wasmtime exposes no single `consume_fuel`); `GAS_CONTEXT_ADDRESS = 5`, `GAS_CONTEXT_SCALAR = 2` per `HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß10` "very cheap" tier; out-of-budget surfaces as explicit `"out of fuel: needed N, have M"` trap. 11 tests: registration + duplicate-error path + gas-constant pin + end-to-end via in-WASM `unreachable`-on-mismatch assertions for each fn + 100-iteration loop verifies ‚â•200 gas tally + 1-gas budget triggers OOF trap inside host fn. Landed in PR [#96](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/96) ‚Äî **‚öÝÔ∏è Superseded 2026-05-28** by [engine#151](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/151): `block_height` registration dropped (was an EVM-portability alias; redundant with `wave_id`), `block_timestamp` renamed to `wave_timestamp`. Current registered context surface is **6 fns**: `caller`, `origin`, `self_address`, `wave_id`, `wave_timestamp`, `chain_id`. Internal `BlockContext.block_timestamp` struct field intentionally kept (deferred cleanup; only the WASM export name was renamed).
  - [x] Tx context: `tx_hash`, `tx_value`, `tx_gas_remaining`, `calldata_size`, `calldata_copy` ‚Äî `tx_hash(out_ptr)` (writes 32-byte Poseidon2 tx hash), `tx_value(out_ptr)` (writes u128 as 16 LE bytes ‚Äî WASM has no native i128), `tx_gas_remaining() -> i64` (post-charge gas via `fuel_to_gas(get_fuel)`) charge `GAS_CONTEXT_ADDRESS = 5` / `GAS_CONTEXT_SCALAR = 2`, landed in PR [#99](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/99). **Calldata fns (PR [#110](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/110))**: added `TxContext.input: Vec<u8>` field to plumb tx.data through to contracts. `pyde::calldata_size() -> i32` returns length directly (scalar; 2 gas). `pyde::calldata_copy(out_ptr, out_len_ptr) -> i32` follows spec ¬ß3.3 `out_ptr + out_len_ptr` convention for variable-size output: contract pre-writes its max-bytes-i-can-accept to `*out_len_ptr` (u32 LE); host reads that limit, copies `min(limit, calldata.len())` bytes to out_ptr, updates `*out_len_ptr` with **actual** length (lets contract detect truncation: `actual > limit` ‚Üí retry with bigger buffer); returns 0 on success. Gas: 5 base + 1/byte copied. Closes the empty-`func.call(&[], &mut [])`-args gap honestly per `HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß3.5.2` ‚Äî default entry IS void-void; contracts read calldata via these host fns. 7 tests: register + duplicate + constants pin + end-to-end via in-WASM unreachable (`calldata_size` returns 5 for [1..=5] input, copy writes "hello" with len reported back, copy truncates at limit=3 reporting actual=10, empty input returns 0).
  - [x] Events: `emit_event` (multi-topic; 1-4 topics; spec ¬ß7.5) ‚Äî `pyde::emit_event(topics_ptr, topic_count, data_ptr, data_len) -> ()` reads `topic_count √ó 32` topic bytes from contract memory, then `data_len` data bytes, and appends `EmittedEvent { contract: self_address, topics, data }` to the in-flight `HostContext::events` buffer (returned via `CallOutcome::events`; higher-layer pipeline flushes to the state crate's `events_cf` on tx success, drops on revert). Validation: `MAX_TOPICS = 4` (matches EVM `LOG0..LOG4` indexing semantics ‚Äî 5+ traps), `MAX_EVENT_DATA_BYTES = 8 KB` pre-allocation guard before the gas check fires. Gas: `GAS_EVENT_BASE = 375 + GAS_EVENT_PER_TOPIC = 375 √ó topic_count + GAS_EVENT_PER_BYTE = 8 √ó data_len` ‚Äî same shape as EVM `LOG` so cross-chain devs have the same mental model. Cross-call revert semantics (sub-call frame drops its own events; parent's events survive) need stack-structured buffers; v1 flat buffer is fine because cross-call doesn't ship yet. 8 tests: register + duplicate-error, gas-cost components, constants pin, end-to-end via in-WASM fill-memory + emit verifies events.len() + topic + data + contract = self_address, too-many-topics trap, oversize-data trap. Landed in PR [#101](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/101)
  - [x] Hashing: `hash_blake3`, `hash_poseidon2`, `hash_keccak256` ‚Äî three host fns sharing the `(in_ptr, in_len, out_ptr) -> ()` shape; each reads input from contract memory, computes a 32-byte digest, writes back. Kept distinct because each serves a different workload: Blake3 for high-throughput commitments (matches Pyde's internal JMT/snapshot/Merkle), Poseidon2 for SNARK-friendly digests (matches Pyde's address/tx-hash/state-root), Keccak-256 for EVM-shape interop. Shared `charge_and_read` preamble: rejects negative len, hard-caps at `MAX_HASH_INPUT_BYTES = 1 MB` (pre-allocation guard before the gas check fires), charges via `get_fuel + set_fuel`. Gas: `GAS_HASH_BASE = 30 + GAS_HASH_PER_WORD = 6` per 32-byte ceiling-divided word; same constants for all three (spec ¬ß10 anchors hashing at one tier so authors pick by suitability not gas). Adds `tiny-keccak` workspace dep; `pyde-crypto::poseidon2::poseidon2_hash` already available. 9 tests: register + duplicate-error path, gas-cost word-boundary table (0/1/32/33/64/1024), max-input cost pin (~197K gas), constants pin, end-to-end verification via in-WASM `unreachable`-on-mismatch with hand-computed expected digests for all 3 fns, oversize input traps. Landed in PR [#98](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/98)
  - [x] Crypto: `falcon_verify` ‚Äî `pyde::falcon_verify(pk_ptr, msg_ptr, msg_len, sig_ptr, sig_len) -> i32` reads a 897-byte FALCON-512 pubkey + variable-len msg + variable-len sig from contract memory, calls `pyde_crypto::falcon::falcon_verify` natively (~1ms; ~50√ó faster than a WASM impl because Cranelift can't auto-vectorize the polynomial arithmetic), returns `i32` (1 = valid, 0 = invalid). Length contracts: pk fixed at 897 (no parameter ‚Äî invariant), `MAX_FALCON_MSG_BYTES = 64 KB`, `MAX_FALCON_SIG_BYTES = 1000` (matches pyde-crypto's accepted upper bound ‚Äî sigs average ~666 with real-world max 800-900). Gas: flat `GAS_FALCON_VERIFY = 50_000` charged up front (verification cost dominated by polynomial inverse + FFT, both message-length-independent). Invalid-input vs invalid-signature semantics: malformed pubkey, malformed sig (length outside `[500, 1000]`), or oversize inputs all **trap** with descriptive messages; well-formed inputs whose signature doesn't verify return `0` (no trap). The contract gets a binary "valid or not" only when both inputs are structurally well-formed. 8 tests: register + duplicate-error, constants pin, real-keypair end-to-end (keygen + sign + WAT data segments with inlined bytes + in-WASM unreachable on != 1 + ‚â•50K gas charge), tampered-sig returns 0, oversize-msg trap, oversize-sig trap, malformed-sig-length trap. Landed in PR [#102](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/102)
  - [x] Cross-call: `cross_call`, `cross_call_static` (FREE; bounded by `VIEW_FUEL_CAP`), `delegate_call` ‚Äî **all three shipped.** `cross_call` (PR [#111](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/111)) per HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß7.8 signature: `(target_ptr, fn_name_ptr, fn_name_len, calldata_ptr, calldata_len, value_ptr, gas_limit, return_data_out_ptr, return_data_out_len_ptr) -> i32`. 11-step execution flow: bounds + depth check (`MAX_CROSS_CALL_DEPTH = 1024`, matches EVM) ‚Üí base gas (`1000 + 8/byte`) ‚Üí read params from contract memory ‚Üí look up callee via overlay ‚Üí value-transfer pre-step **in parent frame** (debit self + credit callee with auto-create AuthKeys::None EOA; survives sub-call revert because it's in parent's overlay layer) ‚Üí push sub-call overlay layer ‚Üí build sub-`HostContext` (depth+1, self_address=target, input=calldata, gas_limit=min(forwarded, parent_remaining), fresh return_data + events) ‚Üí recursive `WasmExecutor::execute_call` ‚Üí outcome-driven overlay pop (`HaltKind::Return` or clean fn-return ‚Üí `pop_and_commit`; `HaltKind::Revert`/`Trap` ‚Üí `pop_and_discard`) ‚Üí gas deduction from parent fuel by `outcome.consumed_gas` regardless of outcome ‚Üí return-data copy via spec ¬ß3.3 `out_ptr + out_len_ptr` convention. `HostContext` gained `executor: Option<WasmExecutor>` field + `with_executor` builder (cheap clone, Engine + ModuleCache internally Arc'd). Code-hash lookup type-puns `Account.code_hash` (Poseidon2Hash) as Blake3Hash bytes (32-byte newtype byte-pun; documented integration gap until Œ≤.3 deploy handler unifies). Deferred from v1 (all need ContractAbi parser): `pyde.abi` selector dispatch, reentrancy guard, access-list enforcement, `#[payable]` attribute check. 7 tests (register + duplicate + 10-constant pin + end-to-end via in-WASM: unknown-target returns 0 no-code path, value-transfer to no-code credits recipient with 100, **real callee E2E** [deploy callee that returns "OK!" + deploy caller that cross_calls + byte-verify return_data], no-overlay traps). **`cross_call_static` shipped** (PR [#117](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/117)) per HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß7.8 signature: `(target_ptr, fn_name_ptr, fn_name_len, calldata_ptr, calldata_len, gas_limit, return_data_out_ptr, return_data_out_len_ptr) -> i32` ‚Äî 8 params (drops `value_ptr` vs `cross_call`). Read-only nested-call host fn. `HostContext` gained `view_mode: bool` field + `with_view_mode` builder. Mutating host fns (`sstore`, `sdelete`, `transfer`, `emit_event`) now trap with `ERR_FORBIDDEN` when `caller.data().view_mode` is true ‚Äî runtime check is the definitive guarantee per ¬ß3.7 (catches mutations even if static call-graph check is bypassed via `call_indirect`). `cross_call_static` execution: bounds + depth check ‚Üí flat `GAS_CROSS_CALL_STATIC_BASE = 50` dispatch gas (sub-call execution itself is FREE to caller per spec ¬ß7.8 ‚Äî view calls have no economic incentive to charge) ‚Üí read target + fn_name + calldata ‚Üí look up callee account ‚Üí push overlay layer (defensive ‚Äî always discarded on exit since view calls shouldn't mutate) ‚Üí build sub-`HostContext` (depth+1, `view_mode=true`, `value=0`, `gas_limit = VIEW_FUEL_CAP = 10M ‚âà 3ms wall-clock per spec; bounds wall-clock not economics) ‚Üí recursive `WasmExecutor::execute_call` ‚Üí outcome classification (Return ‚Üí 0; Trap with "out of fuel" ‚Üí `ERR_CROSS_CALL_OUT_OF_GAS = -11`; other Trap ‚Üí `ERR_CROSS_CALL_FAILED = -8`) ‚Üí return-data copy. `#[view]` attribute dispatch-time check **deferred**: runtime `view_mode` flag is the definitive guarantee; non-view contracts called via `cross_call_static` will trap at first mutation attempt (sstore/sdelete/transfer/emit_event). Wires onto PR-16's ABI parser when ModuleCache v2 carries `(Module, ContractAbi)`. 11 new tests (3 cross_call_static E2E: success / mutation-trap / no-code-callee; 4 direct view-mode-blocks for each mutating host fn; 1 direct view-mode-allows-sload; 3 unit: register / duplicate / constants pin). **`delegate_call` shipped** (PR [#118](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/118)) per HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß7.8 ‚Äî 8 params (same shape as `cross_call_static`; drops `value_ptr` because caller's value flows through unchanged). Runs target's compiled WASM in CALLER's identity + storage + value context (EVM DELEGATECALL equivalent). Sub-context: code looked up by `target_ptr` but `self_address = caller's self_address` ‚Äî every `sstore`/`sload`/`self_address()` in sub-call sees caller's frame. `tx.value` preserved as caller's value (no transfer pre-step). `view_mode` propagates from caller. Gas: `GAS_DELEGATE_CALL_BASE = 1000` + `GAS_DELEGATE_CALL_PER_BYTE = 8` √ó calldata_len + sub-call's `consumed_gas` regardless of outcome. Overlay handling identical to `cross_call`: Return ‚Üí commit; Revert/Trap ‚Üí discard. Foundation for proxy + upgrade patterns. **Security note documented**: callee's code gets direct write access to caller's storage; authors must trust callee completely. `#[delegate_safe]` attribute deferred (auditors flag as standard practice). 3 new tests (sub-call self_address verified equal to caller's via in-WASM `pyde::self_address` + return + byte-check; ERR_CALLEE_NOT_FOUND for no-code target; no-overlay trap) + 3 unit (register / duplicate / constants pin). 194/194 wasm-exec tests passing. PR-15 cross-call trio complete.
  - [x] Halt: `return`, `revert` ‚Äî `pyde::return(ptr, len) -> !` + `pyde::revert(ptr, len) -> !`. Both halt contract execution and write `len` bytes from contract memory at `ptr` into `HostContext.return_data` (new field); executor reads it off the recovered context and surfaces as `CallOutcome.return_data`. Distinct sentinel prefixes in the trap message (`pyde::return: N bytes` / `pyde::revert: N bytes`) let the executor classify into `CallOutcome.halt_kind: Option<HaltKind>` ‚Äî `Some(Return)` (state survives ‚Äî tx pipeline finalizes on success), `Some(Revert)` (state discarded ‚Äî overlay frame drops), `Some(Trap)` (generic ‚Äî unreachable / OOF / host-fn error / divide-by-zero), `None` (clean fn-return path). Higher layers use the discriminator to drive overlay frame commit-vs-discard. Why trap instead of typed result: WASM functions have typed return signatures; making return/revert return-the-function would force every contract entry point to carry the same shape ‚Äî trap-based halt lets any signature work, with halt info threaded out-of-band through the trap message + return_data buffer. `MAX_RETURN_DATA_BYTES = 16 KB` pre-allocation guard; gas essentially free (5 base + 1/byte). Foundation for cross-call (PR-14): cross-call needs `halt_kind` to decide overlay commit/discard. 8 tests: register + duplicate + constants pin (3 unit) + end-to-end via in-WASM construction (return surfaces "hello", revert surfaces "fail", clean return yields None, unreachable classifies as Trap, oversize triggers data-too-large trap). Landed in PR [#107](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/107)
  - [x] Gas: `consume_gas` ‚Äî explicit manual gas burn. `consume_gas(amount: i64)` charges `amount` gas immediately; no-op on negative/zero (spec treats negative as "ignore"); out-of-fuel trap if budget can't cover. No host-fn dispatch surcharge ‚Äî `consume_gas` IS the metering primitive, not an instance of metered code. Useful for contracts that want to deliberately spend gas (e.g., delay loops, fairness mechanisms). Landed in PR [#99](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/99)
  - [x] Randomness: `beacon_get` ‚Äî `pyde::beacon_get(out_ptr) -> i32` writes the wave's committee-derived VRF beacon (32 bytes) to out_ptr; returns 0 always. Per HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß7.11. `BlockContext` gained `beacon: [u8; 32]` field (sourced from Œ≥.1 consensus; XOR of all committee members' beacon shares from the prior anchor round ‚Äî deterministic + identical across all validators on the same wave). Gas: `GAS_BEACON_GET = 50` (small base; no computation needed ‚Äî host fn just copies the pre-computed value from HostContext). Adversary model documented: beacon is publicly predictable WITHIN the wave (adversaries observe it the moment the prior anchor commits, before the current wave's txs run) ‚Äî safe from validators biasing it (committee-XOR construction) but NOT safe from same-wave adversaries exploiting it. For adversary-private randomness, contracts should use the threshold-encryption pipeline (commit beacon-encrypted tx, reveal in later wave) ‚Äî higher-layer protocol, not a host fn. 5 tests: register + duplicate + constants pin (3 unit) + end-to-end via in-WASM (0xBE-filled beacon writes 0xBE at byte 0 + byte 31; default-zero beacon writes all zeros). Landed in PR [#113](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/113)
  - [ ] Parachain extensions (gated): `parachain_storage_read`/`write`/`delete`, `parachain_emit_event`, `parachain_id`, `parachain_version`, `send_xparachain_message`, `threshold_encrypt`, `threshold_decrypt`
- [x] Deploy-time validation (3-layer per `HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß3.7`) ‚Äî **partial: 3 of 5 layers shipped** (PR [#116](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/116)). New `crates/wasm-exec/src/deploy.rs` ships `validate_deploy(wasm) -> Result<ContractAbi, DeployError>` running: **Layer 1 schema** (`pyde_abi_version ‚â§ MAX_SUPPORTED_ABI_VERSION = ContractAbi::V1_0`; Borsh decode succeeds), **Layer 2 cross-reference** (every `FunctionAbi.name` has a matching WASM func export; reverse-direction "every WASM export covered by ABI" deferred ‚Äî spec leaves "internal helpers TBD how to mark"), **Layer 3 attribute compatibility** (full ¬ß3.5.1 negative table: view+payable, view+constructor, view+reentrant, view+sponsored, view+fallback, view+receive, constructor+reentrant, constructor+sponsored, constructor+fallback, constructor+receive, receive without payable, receive+reentrant, fallback+receive on same fn; plus at-most-one fallback/receive + dispatch-index in-bounds + dispatch-index attr-match validation). `DeployError` taxonomy gives wallets + otigen a precise per-layer reason: MissingAbiSection, DuplicateAbiSection, AbiDecode, UnsupportedAbiVersion, WasmParse, DeclaredFnMissingFromWasm, IncompatibleAttributes, MultipleDispatchFunctions, DispatchIndexAttrMismatch, DispatchIndexOutOfBounds. **Deferred**: Layer 4 static call-graph view-enforcement + Layer 5 static access-list (both need WASM call-graph walking; runtime view_mode flag + access-list slot check are the definitive guarantees per spec). Wasmparser 0.244 pinned matching wasmtime 26's bundled version to avoid duplicate transitive copies. 15 tests covering happy path + every error variant + extra-WASM-exports-allowed semantics. Reuses the comprehensive `types/abi.rs` `ContractAbi` (already had `name + version + events + parachain_imports` extension fields beyond spec minimum).
- [x] Attribute application + `pyde.abi` custom-section extraction ‚Äî `extract_pyde_abi(wasm)` walks the WASM binary via wasmparser, finds the single `"pyde.abi"` custom section (rejects missing/duplicate), Borsh-decodes to `ContractAbi`. Attribute application: **`#[view]` runtime mode flag now wired** (PR [#117](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/117) ‚Äî `HostContext.view_mode` + mutating host fns trap with ERR_FORBIDDEN; reached via `cross_call_static`). **`#[payable]` value-transfer check + `#[constructor]` lockout + `#[reentrant]` guard still pending** (need ContractAbi lookup at dispatch time ‚Üí blocked on ModuleCache v2 carrying `(Module, ContractAbi)`). The static side of deploy-time validation IS shipped (attribute compatibility per ¬ß3.5.1). Landed alongside PR [#116](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/116)
- [x] Implement `Executor` trait (from `interfaces`) ‚Äî `WasmExecutorAdapter` in `crates/wasm-exec/src/executor_impl.rs` wraps `WasmExecutor` and dispatches based on `tx.tx_type`: routes `Standard`/`RegisterPubkey`/`EmergencyPause`/`EmergencyResume`/`MultisigTx`/`RotateMultisig`/`ClaimAirdrop`/`SweepAirdrop`/`StakeDeposit`/`StakeWithdraw`/`ClaimReward`/`Slash` to the corresponding Œ≤.3 handler; `Deploy` + `ContractCall` paths placeholder until full call-stack pipeline finalizes. Failed handlers map to `gas_used = MIN_GAS_LIMIT` (21K intrinsic floor) and `ReceiptStatus::Reverted` per spec ¬ß10.4 ("state changes rolled back; gas IS still charged for the work done"). Closes Œ≤.4 ‚Üí Œ≤.3 contract surface. PR [#114](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/114)

#### Œ≤.5 `mempool` crate `[PAR within Œ≤] ‚Üí Œ≤.3`
- [x] Scaffold + core data structures + dedup-only admission ‚Äî opens Œ≤.5 (PR [#121](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/121)). `Mempool` struct: `by_hash: HashMap<TxHash, Arc<Tx>>` (primary dedup) + `by_sender: HashMap<Address, BTreeMap<u64, TxHash>>` (per-sender nonce-ordered FIFO); single `parking_lot::Mutex` guards both (correctness-first; sharding deferred to profiling evidence). `MempoolConfig { max_size, max_per_sender }` defaults 50_000 / 64 (aligned with the 16-slot nonce window + headroom for replacement). `AdmissionError` taxonomy distinguishes permanent rejects (`DuplicateNonce`) from transient ones (`PoolFull`, `SenderCapReached`); `AdmissionOutcome::AlreadyKnown` separates idempotent re-admission from errors. `MempoolStats { admitted, already_known, rejected_permanent, rejected_transient, removed }` snapshot via `stats()`. Public API: `new` / `admit` / `remove` / `remove_all_by_sender` / `contains` / `fetch` / `len` / `is_empty` / `stats` / `config`. **PR-1 admission scope is dedup + capacity ONLY** ‚Äî chain_id / nonce window / balance / gas bounds / calldata size / attribute coherence land in PR-2; FALCON sig verify in PR-3; replacement-by-fee deferred to v2. 11 tests covering: empty default / admit + dedup / dup-nonce reject / pool-full reject / per-sender-cap reject + other-sender-unaffected / remove drops both indexes / remove-missing returns None / remove_all_by_sender / fetch clones / config defaults / config builders.
- [x] FALCON-512 verify pipeline ‚Äî PR [#124](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/124) adds FALCON sig verify as **step 8 (last)** of the admission pipeline. Most expensive single check (~1ms per sig per `pyde-crypto` measurements) ‚Äî runs only after all cheap checks pass, so bad-format / wrong-chain / overdrawn txs reject without paying FALCON cost. `admit()` now takes `sender_auth_keys: &AuthKeys` and dispatches via Œ≤.3's `verify_tx_against_auth` (handles `Single` + `MultiSig` + `None` variants). **Bootstrap exemption**: `tx_type=RegisterPubkey` skips FALCON entirely per Ch 11 ¬ß11.8 row 13 (those txs CREATE the sender's auth keys ‚Äî by construction they can't have valid keys yet). New `AdmissionError` variants: `AuthKeysMissing` (permanent ‚Äî sender is `AuthKeys::None` AND tx isn't RegisterPubkey; the user should submit RegisterPubkey first) and `SignatureInvalid` (permanent ‚Äî `verify_tx_against_auth` returned false; verify-errors collapsed into the same code since the caller can't act on the distinction). **Batched verify deferred to a follow-up**: v1 admits per-tx (gossip + RPC paths arrive per-tx); batch verify becomes load-bearing only if gossip starts shipping multi-tx packs. Pyde-crypto exposes `falcon_verify_all` for that future PR. 4 new FALCON-path tests (`auth_keys_missing_rejects_non_register_pubkey`, `signature_invalid_rejects_against_real_pubkey`, `register_pubkey_skips_falcon_with_none_auth_keys`, `falcon_runs_after_cheaper_checks_short_circuit` proving structural fails at step 4 short-circuit before step 8) + test helpers `admit_skip_falcon` / `as_register_pubkey` to keep pre-existing pool-bookkeeping tests working without a real FALCON keypair. 25/25 mempool tests passing.
- [x] Validation rules: chain_id, nonce window, balance, gas bounds, calldata size, attribute coherence ‚Äî PR [#122](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/122) extends `admit()` to take `(tx, state_balance, state_nonce_window, base_fee)` and runs the full structural + state-checked pipeline. Validation order (cheapest first; each failure short-circuits): (1) dedup by hash, (2) pool/sender capacity, (3) duplicate-nonce in-pool, (4) **structural** via Œ≤.3's `validate_tx_structure` (gas bounds `[MIN_GAS_LIMIT, BLOCK_GAS_MAX]` + calldata ‚â§ `MAX_CALLDATA = 64 KB` + encoded size ‚â§ `MAX_TX_SIZE = 128 KB` + sig presence + per-tx-type shape covering `to=ZERO` for envelope/deploy, `value=0 + empty sig` for `RegisterPubkey`, etc.), (5) `chain_id` match (new `MempoolConfig.chain_id` default `1 = mainnet`), (6) `NonceWindow::is_acceptable` (catches below-base + above-window-of-16 + already-consumed-bit), (7) balance reservation `value + gas_limit √ó base_fee` (saturating u128 math). Caller supplies the state-dependent inputs ‚Äî Mempool itself stays **sync** (async-vs-sync concern lives at the caller boundary; MempoolView impl uses async StateView in PR-6, gossip/RPC paths pre-fetch). New `AdmissionError` variants: `StructuralInvalid(TxValidationError)` (permanent ‚Äî wraps Œ≤.3 taxonomy giving wallets a precise per-rule reason), `WrongChainId { actual, expected }` (permanent), `NonceNotAcceptable { nonce, window_base }` (permanent in v1; v2 may split out a transient "too-high" variant if a deferred-queue lands), `InsufficientBalance { have, need }` (transient ‚Äî balance may rise via incoming transfers). 10 new tests covering each new failure mode + happy-path state-dependent admit + balance-exactly-covers-reservation edge case + structural-gas-too-low + structural-calldata-too-large. 21/21 mempool tests passing.
- [x] Gossip admission (integration with Œ≥'s `net` crate via `NetworkView` trait) ‚Äî **Œ≤-side scaffolding shipped; Œ≥ wiring happens at MC-2 binary assembly.** PR [#127](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/127) ships the per-source admit surface so MC-2 can plug Œ≥.2's `net` crate in as plumbing without touching `pyde-engine-interfaces` (frozen). New `Source` enum (`Rpc` / `Gossip`); `Mempool::admit_local` / `admit_gossiped` / `admit_with_source(...)` all delegate to the existing `admit()` and bump per-source stats only on `Admitted` outcomes. New `MempoolStats.admitted_local` + `admitted_gossiped` subsets of `admitted`. Critically: gossip-replay of an RPC-submitted tx (already in the pool) returns `AlreadyKnown` and does NOT bump `admitted_gossiped` ‚Äî honest gossip cross-pollination doesn't spuriously inflate the counter. **NetworkView left untouched** because `pyde-engine-interfaces` is frozen; the tx-gossip topic + inbound dispatch lives in Œ≥.2 and connects at MC-2 (Œ≥ calls `mempool.admit_gossiped()` on receive). The Œ≤.5 BAR ("replay a tx end-to-end against `MockNetwork`") will be exercised at MC-2 once Œ≥.2's tx-gossip ships; the call surface needed is now in place. 4 new tests: `admit_local_increments_local_counter`, `admit_gossiped_increments_gossiped_counter`, `already_known_does_not_increment_source_counter` (the critical gossip-replay non-double-count), `rejected_admission_does_not_increment_source_counter`. 33/33 mempool tests passing.
- [x] Per-sender rate limit + concurrent cap (DDoS protection) ‚Äî PR [#125](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/125) ships per-sender token-bucket rate limiting as **step 2 of admission** (between dedup and capacity). `MempoolConfig.rate_per_sec` (default 10/s) + `rate_burst` (default 20) define the bucket; lazy refill on access via `tokens = min(tokens + elapsed √ó rate, burst)`. **Counted AFTER dedup** ‚Äî re-submitting the same tx hash returns `AlreadyKnown` and does NOT drain tokens (honest gossip-replay isn't penalised). New `AdmissionError::RateLimited { rate_per_sec, burst }` (transient). New `MempoolStats.rate_limited` counter (subset of `rejected_transient`) ‚Äî operators distinguish "pool full" pressure from "spammer here" pressure. `Eq` derive dropped from `AdmissionError` (f64 doesn't impl Eq); `PartialEq` retained so tests still use `==` where the variant has no float field. Concurrent-cap already covered by `max_per_sender` from PR-1 ‚Äî the spec lumps them in one row but they target different attack vectors (rate vs depth); both are now in place. 5 new tests: burst overflow, per-sender independence, already-known doesn't drain, token-bucket math (unit test of the refill formula ‚Äî avoids wall-clock flakiness), config builders extended. 29/29 mempool tests passing.
- [x] Implement `MempoolView` trait (from `interfaces`) ‚Äî **Œ≤.5 milestone closed.** PR [#129](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/129) ships `PydeMempoolView` wrapping `Mempool` + `Arc<dyn StateView>` + `Arc<RwLock<u128>>` for base_fee. Async-adapts the sync `admit()` to the async trait surface by pre-fetching `balance` / `nonce_window` / `auth_keys` via the StateView handle, then calling `admit_gossiped` (trait route assumed gossip; RPC layers bypass the trait and call `Mempool::admit_local` directly to get the `admitted_local` counter). `AdmissionError ‚Üí InterfaceError` map: `Refused` for permanent application-layer rejects (AlreadyKnown / DuplicateNonce / WrongChainId / NonceNotAcceptable / SignatureInvalid / AuthKeysMissing); `InvalidInput` for `StructuralInvalid`; `Storage` (= retryable per trait taxonomy) for transient rejects (PoolFull / SenderCapReached / InsufficientBalance / RateLimited). **`drain_for_batch` v1 selector**: ascending-nonce-per-sender FIFO, greedy fill to `max_bytes`; single oversize tx still returned when cap < its size (the `!out.is_empty()` short-circuit handles the < MAX_TX_SIZE edge case). Priority-fee ordering deferred to a follow-up if MEV-protection metrics show it's load-bearing. **base_fee management**: `update_base_fee(new)` called after each wave commit; `base_fee()` snapshot read; `mempool()` exposes the inner `Mempool` so RPC paths can call `admit_local` directly for `admitted_local` accounting. 10 new mempool_view tests (insert happy path, already-known ok, Refused on permanent reject, InvalidInput on structural, contains + fetch via trait, drain happy path, drain respects max_bytes, drain-zero edge case, update_base_fee, fetch-missing returns None). 43/43 mempool tests passing. **Œ≤.5 BAR substantively met ‚Äî the `MockNetwork`-driven end-to-end test ("replay a tx end-to-end against in-memory `MockNetwork`") lives at MC-2 binary assembly once Œ≥.2's net crate is wired in; the call surface needed for that wiring is now complete on the Œ≤ side.**

- [x] **Œ≤.5 post-milestone follow-ups** ‚Äî five PRs landed AFTER the Œ≤.5 milestone-closeout that materially harden the Œ≤-side surface for MC-2 wire-up: **cross-Œ≤ integration tests** PR [#139](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/139) (admit ‚Üí drain ‚Üí execute on real RocksDB through `PydeMempoolView` + `WasmExecutorAdapter` ‚Äî RegisterPubkey bootstrap path + Deploy direct-execute + multi-tx drain max_bytes); **real-FALCON e2e** PR [#140](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/140) closing the gap flagged on #139 ‚Äî generates a real FALCON keypair via pyde-crypto, signs a Standard transfer tx, admits through `MempoolView::insert` (full FALCON verify, NOT bootstrap exemption), drains, executes, verifies sender debited + recipient auto-created + nonce committed; companion negative-path test asserts bogus sig ‚Üí `InterfaceError::Refused`; **criterion benches on mempool hot paths** PR [#142](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/142) measures admit_local FALCON-signed at 31.5 ¬µs (31.6K admits/s ST), admit_local RegisterPubkey-bootstrap-exempt at 20.3 ¬µs (49.2K admits/s ST), drain_for_batch at 28 ¬µs / 304 ¬µs / 5.8 ms for 100 / 1K / 10K txs respectively ‚Äî **corrects the prior "FALCON verify ~1 ms per sig" assumption (actual: ~11.2 ¬µs differential, off by ~40√ó)** and establishes that drain double-encode-borsh is sub-millisecond noise below 1K txs/batch; **criterion benches on executor hot paths** PR [#144](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/144) measures execute_tx Standard transfer at 56.2 ¬µs (17.8K tx/s ST) and execute_call minimal void-main WASM at 11.1 ¬µs (90.4K calls/s ST) ‚Äî combined admit + execute pipeline is ~88 ¬µs/tx ST (~11.4K tps), aligning with [[honest_throughput_reset]]'s "10-30K plaintext v1 target" once validator-side parallelism kicks in; **deterministic drain ordering** PR [#145](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/145) sorts `by_sender` keys lex-ascending before iterating in `drain_for_batch` so the returned `Vec<Tx>` is byte-reproducible across runs and across validators ‚Äî useful for tests, debugging, and any future consensus-side machinery that wants to compare drain outputs (the priority-fee selector I'd previously flagged turned out not to be a v1 feature ‚Äî `Tx` has no `tip` field; that lives gated on a v2 hard-fork of the frozen types crate). 925 workspace tests passing, 0 failed, 2 `#[ignore]`'d (known Œ≥.15/Œ≥.16 single-producer-quorum tests). The perf-arc total: 4 PRs (#142 / #144 / #145 + the earlier closeouts) where every claim is now backed by numbers, not priors.

**Œ≤ BAR:** `cargo test` clean on `execution-side` branch; mock-based integration tests (using `interfaces::mock`) pass for state + execution + mempool; can replay a tx end-to-end against the in-memory `MockNetwork`.

### MC-1 Stream Œ≥ ‚Äî Engine Consensus + Network `[PAR within] ‚Üí MC-0` ‚Äî `pyde-net/engine` branch `consensus-side`

Implements Chapter 6, `SLASHING.md`, `VALIDATOR_LIFECYCLE.md`, `STATE_SYNC.md`, `CHAIN_HALT.md`, `NETWORK_PROTOCOL.md`.

**Crates owned:** `consensus`, `net`, `dkg`, `slashing`, `node`.

#### Œ≥.1 `consensus` crate `[SEQ within Œ≥]` ‚Äî foundational
- [x] `Vertex` structure (round, member_id, parent_refs, batch_refs, state_root_sigs, prev_anchor_attestation, decryption_shares, sig) ‚Äî landed in `types` crate at MC-0
- [x] Local DAG view per validator (`VertexStore`: hash + round + slot indexes, equivocation-aware, `parking_lot::RwLock` guarded) ‚Äî PR [#1](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/1)
- [x] Canonical `vertex_hash = Blake3(borsh(vertex_sans_falcon_sig))` centralised ‚Äî PR [#1](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/1)
- [x] Equivocation flagging on insert (`InsertOutcome::Equivocation { prior_at_slot }`; full slashing flow lives in Œ≥.4)
- [x] Vertex production pipeline (`VertexBuilder` + `Signer` trait + `select_parents` helper that skips equivocating slots; returns `(VertexHash, Vertex)` so callers get the dedup key free) ‚Äî PR [#2](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/2)
- [x] Vertex validation pipeline (`validate_vertex` + `Verifier` trait + `ValidationConfig`; cheapest-first checks: range ‚Üí batch-dedup ‚Üí parent quorum ‚Üí parent-round homogeneity ‚Üí FALCON sig; `MissingParent` returns hash so caller can fetch and retry) ‚Äî PR [#3](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/3)
- [x] Round advancement (`RoundTracker`: monotonic counter, distinct-`member_id` quorum check, `try_advance` / `try_advance_to_max` for state-sync catch-up, equivocator-resistant via distinct-producer counting) ‚Äî PR [#9](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/9)
- [x] Anchor selection: `select_anchor(beacon, round, prev_state_root) -> u32` ‚Äî Blake3 over `beacon || round.le || prev_state_root.blake3`, then `mod COMMITTEE_SIZE` (= 128, spec-locked, not a parameter). Dual-hash aware (only Blake3 leg mixes in; Poseidon2 reserved for SNARK paths). Uniform at 128 = 2^7 (no rejection sampling needed). Sibling `select_anchor_for_testing(..., committee_size)` exposes the divisor for tests modelling small committees ‚Äî `pub` only because Cargo can't share `#[cfg(test)]` across crates. ‚Äî PR [#4](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/4), tightened in PR [#112](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/112)
- [x] **Beacon derivation type surface** ‚Äî per Ch 6 ¬ß9 the "VRF beacon" is actually a threshold-signature beacon (`beacon_N = Hash(combined_threshold_sigs("epoch_N_beacon"))`); the roadmap row's "VRF" naming was loose. New `crates/consensus/src/beacon.rs` ships the trait + types + a `MockBeaconScheme` (Blake3-deterministic) so the consensus layer integrates against a stable surface today, with the production pyde-crypto threshold-sig backend dropping in once pyde-crypto is engine-CI-accessible (same blocker as `MockDkg`). `BeaconScheme` trait: `share` / `verify_share` / `combine`. `BeaconDerivationContext { epoch, previous }`. `BeaconShare { member_id, bytes }`. `BeaconError` (InsufficientShares / DuplicateMember / InvalidShare). `const BEACON_THRESHOLD = 85` (= 2f+1 for f=42 on the 128-member committee ‚Äî matches the consensus quorum + DKG threshold). Mock derivation: `share = Blake3("pyde:beacon:mock:share:" \|\| prev \|\| epoch \|\| member_id)`, `combine = Blake3("pyde:beacon:mock:combine:" \|\| prev \|\| epoch \|\| sorted_share_bytes)` (sorted by member_id so combination is share-order-independent ‚Äî matches the spec's "deterministic aggregated signature" property), `genesis_beacon(seed) = Blake3("pyde:beacon:genesis:" \|\| seed)` for the chain's first beacon. 18 tests cover: genesis determinism + seed-variance, mock share determinism + variance across (member, epoch, previous), `verify_share` accepts well-formed / rejects tampered + wrong-member, `combine` rejects below-threshold / duplicate-member / invalid-share, `combine` is share-order-independent + deterministic for same input, `combine` differs per epoch + per previous, epoch-0 derivation chains off `genesis_beacon`. Wiring into `pick_anchor` + anchor-skip rules + production threshold-sig backend land in follow-ups. ‚Äî PR [#109](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/109)
- [x] **Beacon ‚Üí wave_committer wiring** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-2: replaces the wave_committer's "lowest honest member_id" stub with `select_anchor(beacon, round, prev_state_root)` (production-shape, committee size locked at spec 128). Threads `beacon: Beacon` + `prev_state_root: StateRoot` through `WaveCommitterConfig` ‚Üí `ValidatorRunConfig`; both are static placeholders (`[0u8; 32]` + `StateRoot::EMPTY`) until Œ≥.15 PR-3 (per-epoch beacon derivation flow) + Œ≤.3 (real state roots through `StateMutator::commit_wave`) wire real inputs. New picker semantics: target slot derived from beacon ‚Üí return honest vertex at that slot; `None` if missing (transient ‚Äî committer waits) or equivocating (production-correct, but waits indefinitely until Œ≥.16 anchor-skip rules ship). Strips the `committee_size` parameter from `select_anchor` entirely (was needed only for testability) ‚Äî production API is now spec-literal `Hash(beacon, round, prev_state_root) mod 128`. Test path uses `select_anchor_for_testing(..., committee_size)` (in consensus crate) + `pick_anchor_with_committee_size` + `tick_with_committee_size` (in wave_committer) for small-committee scenarios.
