Pairs with the engine-side `lookback_state_root` ‚Üí `prev_state_root` rename + the matching pyde-book rename (commit fef9c30 on main, ticked here implicitly via this row). 2 integration tests (`run_commits_waves_at_tick_cadence`, `validator_with_producer_and_committer_commits_waves`) are `#[ignore]`'d because the 1/128 per-round anchor-hit rate under static all-zero beacon + member_id=0 only makes wave commit unreliable without Œ≥.16. Replaced with a sibling `validator_with_producer_and_committer_runs_both_tasks` asserting only on `vertices_produced`. ‚Äî PR [#112](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/112)
- [x] **Mysticeti anchor-skip rules + ‚â•85-vote support detection** ‚Äî Œ≥.16: replaces the wave-committer's "wait forever on missing anchor" semantic with the full 3-stage commit-or-skip decision per Ch 6 ¬ß7. New `resolve_anchor(dag, round, beacon, prev_state_root) -> AnchorResolution` returns `Commit(anchor) | Skip | Pending`: computes the target slot via `select_anchor` (Œ≥.15 PR-2), looks up the unique honest vertex there, then runs `check_anchor_support` against `QUORUM = 85` and maps the 3-stage outcome onto the resolution. Missing / equivocating slots apply the same R+1-fill rule ‚Äî Skip once R+1 reaches quorum, otherwise Pending (no future vertex can rescue a missing anchor with quorum already filled). Tick state machine: on `Commit`, assemble + persist + `sequencer.record_committed`; on `Skip`, advance `next_anchor_round` (NOT `next_wave_id`) + `sequencer.record_skipped` + bump `wave_anchors_skipped` metric; on `Pending`, break and wait. Tick loop now uses `highest_round - 2` as the upper bound (need R+2 to run the certify stage). `WaveCommitter` gains an internal `AnchorSequencer` (orchestrator-wiring of the Œ≥.4 `AnchorSequencer` type from PR [#37](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/37)), exposed via `sequencer()` for tests + a future PR that shares it with the RPC layer (`pyde_getAnchorOutcome`). New `wave_anchors_skipped: AtomicU64` metric (also in `MetricsSnapshot`). Test-only siblings `resolve_anchor_for_testing(..., committee_size, quorum)` + `WaveCommitter::tick_for_testing(state, committee_size, quorum)` let unit tests model small committees (e.g. quorum=3) without spawning 128 producers. 15 tests cover: full-3-stage commit + sequencer record, skip on R+1-full-unsupported / target-slot-empty / target-slot-equivocates, pending on R+1-below-quorum / target-slot-empty-below-quorum, production resolver at full 85-quorum DAG, tick advances through skipped rounds without bumping wave_id, single-anchor-no-R+1 is pending, empty-dag noop, run() exits on shutdown drop. The two `#[ignore]`'d validator integration tests from Œ≥.15 PR-2 stay ignored ‚Äî under a single producer at `member_id = 0` with the production `QUORUM = 85`, clearing 85 supporters at R+1 is mathematically impossible; they reinstate when multi-validator coordination ships. ‚Äî PR [#120](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/120)
- [x] **Beacon types + genesis bootstrap** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-3a: type surface + plumbing for the per-epoch beacon flow. No runtime rotation yet ‚Äî every wave commits under the same chain-globally-agreed genesis beacon, so PR-3b (gossip topic + share buffer) and PR-3c (epoch state machine + combine + publish) have a stable shape to wire against. New types in `crates/types/src/consensus.rs`: `pub type Epoch = u64` (sibling to `Round` / `WaveId`), `pub const BEACON_LEN: usize = 32` + `pub type Beacon = [u8; BEACON_LEN]` (migrated up from `pyde_engine_consensus::anchor`, which now `pub use`s them so the historic import path stays valid), `pub const GENESIS_BEACON_SEED: &[u8] = b"pyde:genesis:beacon:v1"` (chain-wide consensus parameter; v1 hardcodes it, governance ratification lands with the genesis-block surface). `WaveCommitRecord` gains two wire-format fields: `epoch: Epoch` (every wave carries its epoch) and `next_epoch_beacon: Option<Beacon>` (populated only on the last wave of each epoch per Ch 6 ¬ß9 step 4 ‚Äî `None` everywhere else). `WaveCommitInputs` mirrors both; every initializer across the workspace updated (12 files). `WaveCommitterConfig::default()` derives `beacon` from `genesis_beacon(GENESIS_BEACON_SEED)` instead of the previous `[0u8; BEACON_LEN]` placeholder ‚Äî every validator derives the same chain-derived value at bootstrap. ‚Äî PR [#123](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/123)
- [x] **Beacon-shares gossip topic + buffer** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-3b: receive-side plumbing. `BeaconShare` becomes wire-stable (`epoch: Epoch` field + `BorshSerialize`/`BorshDeserialize` derives); `MockBeaconScheme::verify_share` now rejects shares carrying a mismatched epoch. New `pyde/beacon-shares/1` gossip topic (`pyde_engine_net::topics::BEACON_SHARES`) added to `topics::ALL`. New `BeaconShareBuffer` (`crates/node/src/beacon_buffer.rs`) ‚Äî `Arc<RwLock<HashMap<Epoch, HashMap<u32, BeaconShare>>>>` with `insert` (returns `New | Duplicate`), `count(epoch)`, `quorum_reached(epoch, threshold)`, `shares_for_epoch(epoch)`, `prune_epoch`, `total`, `clear`. `ValidatorMainLoop` constructs an internal `Arc<BeaconShareBuffer>` exposed via `beacon_buffer()`; `dispatch` gains a `beacon_buffer: &BeaconShareBuffer` arg + a topic branch that borsh-decodes incoming shares and inserts them, with per-outcome metric bumps. Four new `MainLoopMetrics` counters (`beacon_shares_received`, `beacon_shares_buffered`, `beacon_share_duplicates`, `beacon_share_decode_failures`) surfaced through `MetricsSnapshot`. 18 new tests across consensus (epoch-mismatch verify rejection), net topics (BEACON_SHARES wire-pin), node beacon_buffer (10 tests covering insert / dedupe / count / quorum / prune / clear), and node mainloop dispatch (4 tests covering successful decode + buffer, duplicate accounting, malformed-bytes decode-failure path, and distinct-member parallel inserts). No signature verification yet ‚Äî PR-3c adds the FALCON-pubkey-vs-committee verify pass before buffering. No combine trigger or epoch-advancement logic ‚Äî also PR-3c. ‚Äî PR [#126](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/126)
- [x] **Epoch helpers + BeaconStore** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-3c.1: types-only slice of the original PR-3c (split mid-stream into 3c.1 + 3c.2 for review-ability ‚Äî the full thing was getting too big for one PR). New constants + helpers in `crates/types/src/consensus.rs`: `pub const EPOCH_LENGTH_WAVES: WaveId = 100` (chain-wide rotation cadence; v1 hardcoded, governance ratification with the genesis-block surface), `epoch_for_wave(wave_id, epoch_length) -> (Epoch, WaveId)` (pure partition helper ‚Äî panics on `epoch_length == 0`), and `is_last_wave_of_epoch(wave_id, epoch_length) -> bool` (detects the Ch 6 ¬ß9 step 4 publish boundary). New `BeaconStore` (`crates/node/src/beacon_store.rs`) ‚Äî `Arc<RwLock<HashMap<Epoch, Beacon>>>` cache of per-epoch derived beacons + a `genesis: Beacon` pre-computed via `genesis_beacon(GENESIS_BEACON_SEED)` at construction so every validator agrees on the epoch-0 fallback. API: `new`, `put(epoch, beacon)`, `get(epoch)`, `current(epoch)` (stored value ‚Üí genesis fallback for epoch 0 only ‚Üí `None` for an un-derived later epoch ‚Äî caller waits), `genesis()`, `len`/`is_empty`/`clear`. 12 new tests pin the constants + cover partition boundaries / panic paths / read-write roundtrip / genesis fallback rule / cross-instance determinism / overwrite semantics / clear-keeps-genesis. **No behaviour change** today ‚Äî the cache stays empty in production because nothing populates it yet. PR-3c.2 ships the dynamic flow: `NetworkView::publish_beacon_share` API, share-emit task at each wave commit, combine trigger when buffer reaches quorum, wave-committer swap-over to read from `BeaconStore`, and `WaveCommitRecord.next_epoch_beacon` populated at epoch boundaries. ‚Äî PR [#128](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/128)
- [x] **Beacon share-emit + NetworkView::publish_beacon_share** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-3c.2: consumer-side of the per-epoch beacon flow (PR-3c was further split into 3c.2 + 3c.3 mid-stream ‚Äî the combine trigger + wave-committer swap-over + `WaveCommitRecord.next_epoch_beacon` publish moved to 3c.3 so each PR stays reviewable). New trait method `NetworkView::publish_beacon_share(payload: Vec<u8>) -> Result<(), InterfaceError>` (`crates/interfaces/src/network.rs`); production impl on `NetworkHandle` routes through `topics::BEACON_SHARES`; `MockNetwork` captures payloads in an in-memory vec + `published_beacon_share_count` counter + `published_beacon_shares()` snapshot helper for tests. `WaveCommitter` gains four fields (`beacon_store: Arc<BeaconStore>`, `beacon_scheme: Arc<dyn BeaconScheme>`, `network: Arc<dyn NetworkView>`, and `my_member_id: u32` + `epoch_length: WaveId` on `WaveCommitterConfig`); `WaveCommitter::new` is now an 8-arg constructor with a `#[cfg(test)] WaveCommitter::for_test` helper that supplies safe defaults (fresh `BeaconStore`, `MockBeaconScheme`, `MockNetwork`) so the existing test surface stays tight. `CommitterState.last_emitted_epoch: Option<Epoch>` tracks per-epoch emission; the share-emit flow fires once per epoch transition (after each successful commit: derive `committed_epoch` via `epoch_for_wave`, build `BeaconDerivationContext { epoch: committed_epoch + 1, previous: beacon_store.current(committed_epoch) ?? config.beacon }`, call `beacon_scheme.share(ctx, my_member_id)`, borsh-encode, fire-and-forget publish via `tokio::runtime::Handle::try_current()` so sync unit tests don't panic). Two new `MainLoopMetrics` counters (`beacon_shares_emitted`, `beacon_share_publish_failures`) + matching `MetricsSnapshot` fields. Validator runtime wires `Arc<BeaconStore>` + `Arc<MockBeaconScheme>` + `Arc<dyn NetworkView>` into the committer. Vertex-producer test impls (`RecordingNetwork`, `FailingNetwork`) extended to satisfy the updated trait. Two new wave_committer tests cover the emit path: `tick_commits_when_resolver_returns_commit_and_records_sequencer` now also asserts `beacon_shares_emitted == 1` + `last_emitted_epoch == Some(1)`; new `share_emit_is_idempotent_within_an_epoch` verifies that multiple commits in the same epoch produce exactly ONE share. ‚Äî PR [#131](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/131)
- [x] **Beacon combine + swap-over + WaveCommitRecord publish ‚Äî loop closed** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-3c.3: the per-epoch beacon rotation is now end-to-end. Three discrete edits in `wave_committer.rs`: (1) **Combine trigger** ‚Äî new `maybe_combine_next_epoch_beacon(state, threshold)` helper fires after the share-emit hook on every commit; checks `BeaconShareBuffer.quorum_reached(next_epoch, QUORUM)`, pulls shares via `shares_for_epoch`, calls `BeaconScheme::combine` with `BeaconDerivationContext { epoch: next_epoch, previous: beacon_store.current(committed_epoch) }`, stores result in `BeaconStore`, prunes buffer. Idempotent ‚Äî store-presence check short-circuits subsequent triggers for the same epoch. (2) **Anchor-selection swap-over** ‚Äî `tick_with_resolver` derives `live_beacon = beacon_store.current(epoch_for_wave(state.next_wave_id))` per tick instead of `&self.config.beacon`. For epoch 0 the store returns the genesis fallback; for later epochs with no combine yet ‚Üí `None` ‚Üí committer breaks out of tick (waits for share gossip + combine to populate). (3) **Publish hook** ‚Äî `commit_one_wave_with_anchor` populates `WaveCommitInputs.epoch` from `epoch_for_wave` (no longer hardcoded `0`) and `WaveCommitInputs.next_epoch_beacon = beacon_store.get(committed_epoch + 1)` on the last wave of each epoch (gated by `is_last_wave_of_epoch`), so the wire shape from PR-3a becomes live. `WaveCommitter` gains a 4th beacon-flow field (`beacon_buffer: Arc<BeaconShareBuffer>`); `WaveCommitter::new` is now 9-arg; validator runtime threads the mainloop's `beacon_buffer()` into the committer so writer (gossip path) + reader (combine trigger) share one Arc. Two new metrics (`beacons_combined`, `beacon_combine_failures`) + `MetricsSnapshot` fields. 5 new wave_committer tests cover: combine-quorum-gating (3 mock shares < QUORUM=85 ‚Üí combine does NOT fire ‚Äî proves the threshold gate is real), `next_epoch_beacon` populated only on epoch boundary, swap-over reads from store not config (config points to slot-7-picker, store has slot-0-picker, committer uses store), swap-over waits when store lacks current epoch's beacon. Two existing tests fixed (previously passing only because the genesis beacon happened to pick the right slot). New `#[cfg(test)] beacon_store_handle()` + `beacon_buffer_handle()` accessors let tests pre-load both. 21 wave_committer + 239 node lib + full workspace green. FALCON-pubkey verify on incoming shares deferred (needs `CommitteeRegistry` wiring; mock scheme's `verify_share` is hash-deterministic, sufficient for v1). ‚Äî PR [#136](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/136)
- [x] **FalconBeaconScheme ‚Äî real PQ FALCON-512 sigs** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-4 (closes the original PR-4 row): production-shape `BeaconScheme` impl backed by per-member FALCON-512 sigs via `pyde-crypto`. Wire-compatible with `MockBeaconScheme` through the shared `BeaconScheme` trait + `BeaconShare` format; the two schemes use distinct domain tags (`pyde:beacon:falcon:share:` / `:combine:` vs `pyde:beacon:mock:share:` / `:combine:`) so shares can never be cross-decoded. **Design rationale:** the spec (Ch 6 ¬ß9) describes the beacon as `Hash(aggregated_threshold_sig)`. `pyde-crypto` doesn't ship threshold sigs yet ‚Äî post-quantum threshold sigs are research-level per memory `feasibility_honest_assessment`. This PR approximates "aggregated threshold sig" as `Blake3(prev_beacon \|\| epoch \|\| sorted_by_member_id(falcon_sigs).concat())`. Security holds because adversary with `<85` shares cannot pre-image the hash of 85 unpredictable PQ sigs without producing all 85; when `pyde-crypto` ships true threshold sigs proper, the upgrade is a one-trait-impl swap. **share()**: `falcon_sign(local_secret, FALCON_SHARE_DOMAIN \|\| ctx.previous \|\| ctx.epoch.to_le_bytes() \|\| member_id.to_le_bytes())`. Panics if `member_id != local_member_id` ‚Äî production callers always pass `my_member_id`; the panic guards against API misuse (only the local validator has the secret). **verify_share()**: bounds-check `share.member_id < committee.len()`, then `falcon_verify(committee[member_id], same_preimage, share.bytes)`. Rejects epoch mismatch, out-of-committee `member_id`, tampered sig, malformed-bytes (falls through `FalconSignature::from_bytes` ‚Üí `None`). **combine()**: threshold (`BEACON_THRESHOLD = 85`) + dedup (sorted-by-`member_id`, reject windows with same id) + `verify_share` each + Blake3 over sorted bytes ‚Üí 32-byte beacon. Same domain-separation discipline as `MockBeaconScheme`. **Validator wiring:** opt-in via `--falcon-beacon` CLI flag (default off ‚Äî `MockBeaconScheme` stays the production-validator default until multi-validator committee distribution is wired). Enabled: generates an ephemeral FALCON keypair at startup, constructs `committee = [self_pk]` (solo mode), threads `Arc<FalconBeaconScheme>` into the wave-committer in place of the mock. Restart loses the keypair ‚Üí beacons from prior runs won't combine; persistence + genesis-committee loading are follow-ups. `ValidatorRunConfig::falcon_beacon: bool` + `Command::Validator { falcon_beacon, .. }` propagated through `dispatch` ‚Üí `run_validator_cli`. **12 new beacon-crate tests** (4.5s on M-class): share/verify roundtrip, tamper rejection, epoch mismatch, out-of-committee `member_id`, share differs per epoch / prev, panic-on-non-local-member-id, imposter-sig-from-other-member (member 0 signs message for member 1, verify uses committee[1]'s pubkey ‚Üí fails ‚Äî proves sig-to-member-id binding), combine-below/at-threshold, dup member, invalid share, combine differs per epoch / prev, `committee_size` accessor. **1 new validator-integration test**: `validator_with_falcon_beacon_boots_and_produces_vertices` boots solo validator with `falcon_beacon=true` + producer/committer on; asserts ‚â•3 vertices flow under the real PQ-sig beacon path. **1 new CLI test**: `parses_validator_with_falcon_beacon_flag`. 1620 workspace tests passing (was 1603; +14 new ‚Äî 12 beacon + 1 validator + 1 cli; -1 net delta after deduplication checks). All 4 CI gates green. **Out of scope (next slices):** (1) persistent FALCON beacon keypair ‚Äî currently ephemeral; the existing `FalconKeypair` infrastructure in `crates/node/src/falcon_keypair.rs` is mock-backed, so a follow-up unifies the real-FALCON migration across the validator (consensus keypair + beacon keypair via a single file format, or separate-key hygiene); (2) multi-validator committee distribution ‚Äî `committee: Vec<FalconPublicKey>` hardcoded to `[self_pk]` in solo mode; the genesis-committee surface (config-file or chain-genesis-derived) lands separately; (3) true threshold-sig combine ‚Äî single aggregated sig instead of `n` concatenated sigs; blocked on `pyde-crypto` shipping threshold sigs proper. ‚Äî PR [#155](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/155)
- [x] **Persistent BeaconKeypair** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-4 follow-up #1 (closes the "next slice" #1 callout on #155): disk-backed FALCON-512 keypair for `FalconBeaconScheme` so the validator's beacon identity survives restarts. Without this, every restart regenerates the keypair ‚Üí peer `verify_share` rejects the post-restart shares ‚Üí no beacon combine fires ‚Üí wave-committer stalls on missing beacons. **Module:** new `crates/node/src/beacon_keypair.rs` with `BeaconKeypair { secret: FalconSecretKey, pubkey: FalconPublicKey }` carrying real PQ keys via `pyde_crypto::falcon::*`. API: `generate()`, `save_to(path)`, `load_from(path)`, `load_or_generate(path)` ‚Äî same atomic tmp‚Üírename pattern as the libp2p + main consensus keypairs. Versioned on-disk format (`BEACON_KEYPAIR_FILE_VERSION_FALCON = 1`) so a future algorithm swap surfaces as `MismatchedVersion` instead of silently breaking. `Debug` impl never leaks secret bytes (pubkey-fingerprint only ‚Äî same hygiene as the existing `FalconKeypair`). **Deliberately separate** from the main consensus `FalconKeypair` (still mock-backed): the validator's vertex-signing key and beacon-signing key live in distinct files, so a leaked beacon key only affects beacon-share predictability for that committee member, not vertex sigs (and vice versa). The trade-off is two files to manage; for v1 the simplicity wins. **CLI:** `--beacon-keypair <PATH>`, only consulted when `--falcon-beacon` is set. Omit for ephemeral mode (existing behavior). **Validator wiring:** `ValidatorRunConfig.beacon_keypair_path: Option<PathBuf>`. `Some(path)` ‚Üí `BeaconKeypair::load_or_generate(path)`. `None` ‚Üí `BeaconKeypair::generate()`. Both feed the same `FalconBeaconScheme::new(validator_id, kp.secret(), vec![kp.pubkey()])` constructor; load_or_generate failure falls back to `MockBeaconScheme` with a `tracing::error!` (keeps the validator running even if the keypair file is unreadable). **10 new tests:** 8 unit tests in `beacon_keypair::tests` (generate produces valid keypair, save+load roundtrip, load_or_generate creates file when missing, load_or_generate idempotent across 3 calls, rejects malformed bytes, rejects unknown version, rejects corrupt key lengths, `Debug` doesn't leak secret bytes); 1 CLI parse test (`parses_validator_with_beacon_keypair_path`); 1 validator-integration test (`validator_with_persistent_beacon_keypair_reuses_file_across_restarts` ‚Äî boots the validator twice with the same `--beacon-keypair` path, asserts the on-disk pubkey bytes are byte-identical across runs; gated on `committer_tick_ms: Some(_)` because the FalconBeaconScheme is only constructed when the wave-committer spawns). **Pyde-crypto note:** `BeaconKeypair::load_from` doesn't apply the pubkey-derives-from-secret cross-check that `FalconKeypair` uses for the mock-secret path ‚Äî `pyde-crypto` doesn't expose secret‚Üípubkey derivation as a standalone primitive (`falcon_keygen` produces both at once); we trust the persisted pair instead. 1630 workspace tests passing (was 1620; +10 new). All 4 CI gates green. **Out of scope (next slices):** (1) multi-validator committee distribution ‚Äî `FalconBeaconScheme` still constructs `committee = [self_pk]` in solo mode; persistence alone doesn't unblock the two `#[ignore]`'d integration tests, but it's the prereq for sharing a stable committee table across restarts; (2) unifying the file format with `FalconKeypair` once the main consensus keypair migrates to real FALCON. ‚Äî PR [#156](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/156)
- [x] **Genesis-committee distribution** ‚Äî Œ≥.15 PR-4 follow-up #2 (closes the "next slice" #2 callout on #156): `--genesis-committee <PATH>` loads a plain-text file mapping `member_id ‚Üí FALCON beacon pubkey`, and `FalconBeaconScheme` constructs with the full committee table from disk instead of solo `[self_pk]`. Without this, each peer's `verify_share` rejects the others' shares as out-of-committee (only `self_pk` is in the table), so the ‚â•85 combine threshold can never be reached. This PR ships the static-file form first; the validator-registry-derived form lands when slashing + validator lifecycle wire up. **File format:** plain-text, one `<member_id> <hex_pubkey>` per line, `#` for comments, `0x` prefix optional, hex case-insensitive, pubkey exactly 897 bytes (FALCON-512). Mirrors the bootnodes file pattern from Œ≥.2.bootnodes (engine #109) ‚Äî single-purpose, hand-editable for devnet operators, no TOML dep pulled into the binary's link surface. **Validation:** `member_id`s must be dense `0..N` (no gaps), no duplicates; extra columns silently accepted (`/etc/hosts` style) for future per-member fields (`peer_id`, `stake`, ...) without breaking back-compat readers. Errors carry both line numbers for duplicates and `(expected, actual)` for gaps so the operator sees exactly which line to fix. **Module:** new `crates/node/src/genesis_committee.rs` with `read_genesis_committee(path)` + `parse_genesis_committee(content, path)` + `GenesisCommitteeError` (Io / Parse / DuplicateMember / NonDenseMemberIds / Empty). **Validator wiring:** `ValidatorRunConfig.genesis_committee_path: Option<PathBuf>`. When set alongside `--beacon-keypair`, the validator checks `committee[validator_id]` matches the loaded keypair's pubkey. Mismatch (wrong keypair file or stale committee table) ‚Üí `tracing::error!` + fall back to `MockBeaconScheme`; the validator keeps running rather than halting on misconfig. Out-of-range `validator_id` for the loaded table ‚Üí same fallback path. **18 new tests:** 15 unit tests in `genesis_committee::tests` covering parse happy paths (solo, dense in-order, dense out-of-order, `0x` prefix optional, uppercase hex, comments + blanks) + error paths (empty file, duplicate `member_id` with both line numbers, non-dense gap, bad hex, wrong pubkey length, missing pubkey column) + forward compat (extra columns silently accepted) + disk IO (roundtrip + missing-file Io error); 1 CLI parse test (`parses_validator_with_genesis_committee_path`); 2 validator-integration tests (`validator_with_genesis_committee_boots_when_pubkey_matches` ‚Äî boots with matching keypair + committee ‚Üí emits vertices via the loaded committee table; `validator_with_genesis_committee_mismatch_falls_back_to_mock` ‚Äî boots with mismatched keypair pubkey ‚Üí validator stays up under mock fallback, doesn't halt). 1648 workspace tests passing (was 1630; +18 net new). All 4 CI gates green. **Out of scope (next slices):** (1) reinstating the two `#[ignore]`'d integration tests from Œ≥.15 PR-2 + Œ≥.16 (`run_commits_waves_at_tick_cadence` / `validator_with_producer_and_committer_commits_waves`) ‚Äî the test harness needs to spin up ‚â•2 validator instances + a shared committee file + cross the gossip path; infrastructure is now in place but the harness change is its own slice; (2) genesis-committee derivation from chain config (the validator registry + epoch transitions form, not static file) ‚Äî lands when slashing + validator lifecycle wire up; (3) true threshold-sig combine ‚Äî still blocked on `pyde-crypto` shipping threshold sigs proper. ‚Äî PR [#157](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/157)
- [x] **Canonical-subset rule for combine (lowest-member-id 85)** ‚Äî Œ≥.15.PR-4.canonical-subset: closes the HIGH-priority subset-disagreement bug surfaced during a design conversation about the v1 FALCON-aggregate beacon. Without this fix, two validators with different superset views of the buffered share pool would produce different beacons ‚Üí consensus fork on the first multi-validator run. The conversation also produced the matching Ch 6 ¬ß9 + ¬ß10 spec correction in pyde-book #197. **The rule:** `BeaconScheme::combine` MUST use exactly the lowest-`member_id` `BEACON_THRESHOLD` (85) shares ‚Äî sort by `member_id` ascending, reject duplicates (before subset cut so duplicate low-id shares can't smuggle different sig bytes), truncate to 85, verify the selected 85, hash exactly those. Extras above the threshold are silently dropped. This makes the output deterministic for any caller whose buffer contains the same lowest-85 set, regardless of how many extras either validator has buffered. **Trait doc updated** with the rule + Ch 6 ¬ß9 v1 caveat cross-link; both `MockBeaconScheme::combine` and `FalconBeaconScheme::combine` follow the same discipline. **4 new tests pin the contract:** (1) mock: extras above lowest-85 don't change beacon (proves invariance); (2) mock: removing a low-id share + adding a high-id MUST shift the beacon (proves the rule actually uses lowest-85, not "any 85"); (3) mock: reverse-order + high-id padding still produces baseline beacon (proves sort+truncate logic is order-independent); (4) FALCON-aggregate: extras above lowest-85 don't change beacon ‚Äî the real PQ-sig path, the property that actually matters for multi-validator safety. 1676 workspace tests passing (was 1672; +4). All 4 CI gates green. **What this does NOT fix (next slice):** the wave-committer's combine trigger (`maybe_combine_next_epoch_beacon`) currently fires as soon as the local buffer has ‚â•85, which can race the gossip diameter ‚Äî if validator A has shares `{0..84}` while validator B has `{1..85}` (B missing member 0), they STILL fork because their "lowest 85" disagrees. Follow-up: add a wait-window at the wave-committer layer (e.g., "wait for all 128 OR a 30s timeout past first threshold-met") so all validators converge on the same lowest-85 before combining. This PR fixes the combine API; the wait-window fixes the WHEN-to-combine policy. ‚Äî PR [#162](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/162)
- [x] **Wait-window policy for beacon combine** ‚Äî Œ≥.15.PR-4.wait-window (pairs with #162's canonical-subset rule to close the residual fork risk flagged on #162): the canonical-subset rule guarantees safety IF AND ONLY IF all validators have the same lowest-85 shares in their buffer at combine time ‚Äî if A has `{0..84}` while B has `{1..85}` (B missing member 0), their lowest-85 disagrees ‚Üí they STILL fork. This PR adds the WHEN-to-combine policy at the wave-committer layer. **The policy:** after the local buffer first reaches `beacon_combine_threshold`, wait for either (a) `beacon_combine_target_count` shares to arrive (e.g., all 128 in) ‚Üí combine fires immediately, OR (b) `beacon_combine_wait_window` to elapse since the first-met moment ‚Üí combine fires with whatever's buffered (still ‚â•threshold). The wait gives gossip diameter time to propagate so the lowest-85 set converges across all validators before anyone combines. **Config:** `WaveCommitterConfig` gains `beacon_combine_threshold` (production = `QUORUM = 85`), `beacon_combine_target_count` (production = `COMMITTEE_SIZE = 128`), `beacon_combine_wait_window` (production = ~30 sec per spec gossip-diameter estimate; tests use `ZERO` to preserve pre-wait-window semantics). The previously-hardcoded `QUORUM` in `tick_with_resolver`'s call to `maybe_combine_next_epoch_beacon` swapped for `self.config.beacon_combine_threshold` so tests can exercise the path with small committees. **State:** `CommitterState.combine_first_threshold_met: HashMap<Epoch, Instant>` tracks per-epoch first-met timestamps; pruned on successful combine + on no-threshold reset (defensive ‚Äî if a buffer drops below threshold mid-wait, restart the timer). NOT persisted ‚Äî on restart the wait resets, which is safe because gossip has already settled by the time the validator finishes restarting. **Metric:** new `beacon_combines_deferred_by_wait: AtomicU64` surfaces "wait policy is firing" vs "stuck on a bug". **4 new tests pin the contract:** (1) `combine_defers_when_threshold_met_below_target_and_wait_not_elapsed` ‚Äî deferral path; metric increments on each call while the wait is open; (2) `combine_fires_immediately_when_target_count_hit` ‚Äî early-exit (steady-state) path; (3) `combine_fires_after_wait_elapses_with_threshold_below_target` ‚Äî timeout-fallback path (ZERO wait, target unreachable, combine fires anyway); (4) `combine_clears_first_met_after_success_and_reset` ‚Äî cleanup on both success + no-threshold-met paths. Tests pre-load `BEACON_THRESHOLD = 85` shares so the underlying `BeaconScheme::combine` threshold gate is satisfied. 1680 workspace tests passing (was 1676; +4). All 4 CI gates green. **Status of the beacon-fork-risk track:** with #162 (canonical-subset API rule) + #163 (this PR, wait-window policy), the HIGH-priority fork risk flagged in `beacon_v1_weaknesses` memory is now closed at both layers. Residual risk: ~1 bit/epoch last-signer grinding bias (waits on `pyde-crypto` true threshold sigs). ‚Äî PR [#163](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/163)
- [x] **2-validator boot harness (multi-validator integration)** ‚Äî Œ≥.5.multi-validator-harness: spawns two `pyde validator` instances over loopback with a shared `FalconBeaconScheme` committee table, verifies both boot cleanly under the multi-validator config (`--falcon-beacon` + `--beacon-keypair` + `--genesis-committee` all wired) and emit vertices via the real PQ FALCON beacon path. **Harness payoff** for the prior 4 PRs (#155 FalconBeaconScheme, #156 persistent BeaconKeypair, #157 genesis-committee distribution, #158 typed `NewListenAddr`). **What this proves:** (1) two persistent `BeaconKeypair`s + a shared `genesis-committee` file wire `FalconBeaconScheme` cleanly across both validators (no `MockBeaconScheme` fallback fires on either side); (2) validator A binds its listen socket, B's dial multiaddr (with `/p2p/<peer-id>` suffix from a pre-generated libp2p keypair) reaches it; (3) both validators stay healthy + emit at least genesis + a couple of solo-cascade follow-on vertices through the full FalconBeaconScheme path. **Helpers:** `pick_free_tcp_port()` (binds `127.0.0.1:0`, reads the OS-assigned port, drops the listener ‚Äî TOCTOU window is tiny on loopback, acceptable for in-process tests). `libp2p` added to `crates/node/Cargo.toml` dev-deps (version + minimal features in sync with `crates/net/Cargo.toml`) ‚Äî needed to base58-encode a `PeerId` into the `/p2p/<peer-id>` multiaddr suffix; `pyde_engine_net::PeerId` carries multihash bytes but doesn't expose a textual encoder. **What this does NOT prove (deferred):** (1) cross-validator vertex exchange via gossipsub ‚Äî libp2p gossipsub's mesh formation in a 2-peer cluster is fragile (default `mesh_n_low = 4` means a 2-peer mesh never reaches the well-connected threshold; messages may drop). Verifying end-to-end vertex exchange needs either a small-mesh gossipsub config override (test-only) or a ‚â•4-peer test cluster; (2) beacon-share combine ‚Äî `BEACON_THRESHOLD = 85` is hardcoded; 2 validators can't reach it (the combine path stays covered by single-process tests in `pyde_engine_consensus::beacon`); (3) wave commit under multi-validator ‚Äî anchor-selection is still `1/128` for `member_id 0..1` under `COMMITTEE_SIZE = 128`. 1651 workspace tests passing (was 1650; +1 new harness test). - [x] **Finality-cert assembly + persistence + ConsensusStore CF** ‚Äî Œ≥.mc2 task #143 sub-PR 2/2 (closes #143): closes the emit half of the finality-cert pipeline. End-to-end now lives: `pyde/state-root-sigs/1` gossip ‚Üí `StateRootSigBuffer` (from 1/2) ‚Üí wave-committer commit hook ‚Üí `try_assemble_finality_cert` ‚Üí `HardFinalityCert` persisted in `finality_certs_cf`. - [x] **Restart resumption for committer + beacon store** ‚Äî Œ≥.mc2 task #147 (closes #147): a restarted validator now picks up at `highest_wave_id + 1` instead of replaying from genesis. New `CommitterState::resume(&store)` reads the most-recent `WaveCommitRecord` and derives: `next_wave_id = highest_wave_id + 1`, `next_anchor_round = record.anchor_round + 1`, `last_anchor_round = Some(record.anchor_round)`, `last_emitted_epoch = Some(record.epoch + 1)` (the share-emit hook fires once per epoch when the first wave of that epoch commits, so the rehydrate is set to `epoch + 1` to prevent redundant share-emits in the same epoch post-restart). New `BeaconStore::resume_from_store(&store)` walks `waves_cf` ascending + replays every `next_epoch_beacon` entry from last-wave-of-epoch records (per PR-3c.3); genesis fallback for epoch 0 unchanged. New `ConsensusStore::collect_next_epoch_beacons()` underlies the BeaconStore resume ‚Äî returns `Vec<(Epoch, Beacon)>` ascending by `WaveId` (which is ascending `Epoch` under monotonic commit order). `WaveCommitter::run` calls `CommitterState::resume` instead of `CommitterState::new`; validator runtime constructs the committer's `BeaconStore` via `resume_from_store` instead of `new`. Both fall back to fresh state on read failure with a `warn` log ‚Äî better to lose the resume than to crash the node. **Intentional gaps:** (1) `AnchorSequencer` skipped-round history NOT rehydrated ‚Äî existing v1 doc comment defers this (only impact is `pyde_getAnchorOutcome(round)` returns "unknown" for skipped rounds before the restart); (2) `committed: HashSet<VertexHash>` left empty ‚Äî the `VertexStore` is in-memory and starts empty after restart, so any historical-ancestor walk by `walk_subdag` is naturally bounded by what's in-memory (reconstruction waits on vertex persistence / state-sync). 6 new wave_committer tests: empty store ‚Üí genesis-shaped state; 3-waves resume ‚Üí next slot is `highest+1` + next round = `last anchor+1`; `last_emitted_epoch` gates redundant share-emit after restart; `BeaconStore::resume_from_store` empty ‚Üí empty with genesis fallback; `BeaconStore::resume_from_store` replays multiple `next_epoch_beacon` entries; `collect_next_epoch_beacons` yields ascending order regardless of insertion order. 33 wave_committer + 924 workspace tests green; all 4 CI gates clean. ‚Äî PR [#146](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/146)
- [x] **Equivocation evidence ‚Üí slashing consumer** ‚Äî Œ≥.mc2 task #145 (closes #145): closes the consensus‚Üíslashing wire that `EquivocationDetector` had set up but nothing was driving. The `VertexStore`'s existing `EquivocationDetected` sink now has a consumer task that drains it + feeds each event through the slashing pipeline. New `crates/node/src/equivocation_consumer.rs` defines `EquivocationConsumer` ‚Äî owns the detector + channel receiver + metrics + shutdown signal + v1 stubs. `run()` is a long-running `tokio::select!` that drains events until shutdown flips or all senders drop; `dispatch()` is public for tests, routes one event to `EquivocationDetector::handle_equivocation` + bumps `equivocation_consumer_processed` (slash applied + escrow entry pending) or `equivocation_consumer_rejected` (missing prior, pipeline rejected). Validator runtime spawns the consumer alongside mainloop / producer / committer: attaches an unbounded channel via `vertex_store.set_equivocation_sink(tx)`, builds the detector against the same vertex store / slasher / escrow, joins the task on shutdown. Mainloop's `InsertOutcome::Equivocation` log line tightened from "deferred to follow-up PR" ‚Üí "routed to slashing consumer via sink". **v1 stubs called out explicitly** (each annotated for a clean follow-up swap): (1) **Verifier** ‚Äî production needs `member_id ‚Üí FALCON pubkey` lookup driven by the committee registry; not yet running, so the consumer uses `AcceptingVerifier` (always returns `true`). The store's slot-collision detection is the meaningful gate at v1. (2) **DKG** ‚Äî `verify_evidence` requires a DKG ref even for Equivocation payloads (where it's never touched); the consumer instantiates a fresh `MockDkg(Threshold(3))`. (3) **Epoch** ‚Äî hardcoded `DEFAULT_EPOCH = 0` until per-epoch tracking is wired. (4) **Stake** ‚Äî hardcoded `DEFAULT_STAKE = 10_000` (single-tier minimum from the staking spec). Two new `MainLoopMetrics` counters + matching `MetricsSnapshot` fields. 6 new consumer tests pin the contract: happy-path ‚Üí slash + jail + escrow entry + processed-metric bump; empty `prior_at_slot` ‚Üí rejected (defensive against store contract violation); unknown prior hash ‚Üí `PriorNotFound` rejection; `run()` drains channel then exits on sender drop; `run()` exits on shutdown flip; `AcceptingVerifier` returns `true` for any input. 930 workspace tests green; all 4 CI gates clean. ‚Äî PR [#147](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/147)
- [x] **StateMutator::commit_wave trait reshape for Œ≥‚ÜîŒ≤ handshake** ‚Äî Œ≥.mc2 task #144 sub-PR 1/2 (interfaces-only): proposes the right `StateMutator::commit_wave` trait surface so Œ≤ can implement the production orchestrator behind a frozen contract. **Trait change:** old `commit_wave(wave_id, txs: Vec<Tx>) -> WaveCommitRecord` ‚Üí new `commit_wave(walked_vertices: Vec<Arc<Vertex>>) -> WaveCommitInputs`. The new shape is the right contract: Œ≥ produces the BFS sub-DAG ordering via `walk_subdag(anchor)`, Œ≤ resolves each vertex's `batch_refs` to txs using Œ≤'s own batch cache, Œ≤ executes per-tx accumulating `gas_used: u128` + events + receipts, Œ≤ calls `StateCommitter::commit_with_events` to produce a single atomic state_root + events_root + events_bloom, returns the 7 execution-side `WaveCommitInputs` fields. Œ≥ then folds into a `WaveCommitRecord` via `assemble_wave_commit_record(anchor, inputs)`. **Crate moves:** `WaveCommitInputs` moves from `pyde_engine_consensus::wave_commit` ‚Üí `pyde_engine_types::consensus` so the `interfaces` crate can name it in `StateMutator::commit_wave`'s return type without taking a dep on `consensus` ‚Äî keeps layer order honest: `types` ‚Üí `interfaces` ‚Üí (`consensus` + Œ≤); Œ≤ doesn't depend on `consensus`. `pyde_engine_consensus` re-exports for backwards compat. **Mock + spike updates:** `MockState::commit_wave` matches new shape, returns empty-execution inputs (the mock doesn't crack open `batch_refs`; production Œ≤ resolves batches + executes per-tx). `DevnetState` (the spike): per-tx execution logic moves to a new public inherent `commit_wave_with_resolved_txs(wave_id, txs) -> WaveCommitInputs`; the trait method returns `NotImplemented` so it's unambiguous that real Œ≤ implements the resolution + execution end-to-end. Devnet composer pre-resolves batches (it owns the spike's batch cache) + calls the inherent helper directly + patches in the composer-owned `prior_anchor_round` on top of the returned `WaveCommitInputs`. **Œ≤ audit conclusion** informs this PR: Œ≤ has the primitives (`StateCommitter.commit_with_events`, full Deploy handler, per-tx Receipt flow with events + return_data) but lacks (1) the orchestrator + (2) the right trait shape + (3) `rollback_wave` persistence; ~4-7 days Œ≤-side effort to ship the production impl behind this surface. This is **sub-PR 1/2** for #144 ‚Äî the 2/2 wires the running wave-committer to call `state.commit_wave(walked_vertices)` once Œ≤ lands its impl. 930 workspace tests green; all 4 CI gates clean. ‚Äî PR [#148](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/148)
- [x] **Vertex producer: event-driven on parent quorum** ‚Äî Œ≥.mc2 task #142 (closes #142): replaces the wall-clock-ticking producer (Œ≥.5 solo-bring-up spike) with the architecturally-correct Mysticeti Ch 6 ¬ß4 design ‚Äî a validator emits round R+1 only when ‚â•`quorum` parents from round R are in the local DAG. The wall-clock pacing was wrong because: (1) in multi-validator runs, 128 validators all emitted round N+1 in lockstep regardless of whether they'd seen each other's round N ‚Äî round numbers raced ahead while parent sets stayed sparse; (2) the "2271 vertices in 5s at 250ms tick" observation that prompted the task was a separate runaway bug that the design fix supersedes entirely. **Architecture:** new `VertexStore::insertion_notify() -> Arc<tokio::sync::Notify>` fires once on every successful insert (`New` or `Equivocation`; not `Duplicate`). Uses `notify_one` to stash a permit when no waiter is parked ‚Äî avoids the missed-wake problem where an insert that lands while the producer is busy emitting would otherwise leave the producer parked forever waiting for the next insert. `VertexProducer::run()` refactored: replaces `tokio::time::interval` with a `select!` over (shutdown, notify, min-tick-floor). On every wake ‚Üí `parent_quorum_reached()` which checks `select_parents(dag, next_round, usize::MAX).len() >= quorum`. Round 0 has no parent gate (genesis always fires). On condition met ‚Üí emit + insert + publish + `tokio::task::yield_now()` (cascades through the runtime so shutdown/network/mainloop tasks can run between produces). Sync shutdown check at the top of every loop iteration covers the cascade path where `continue` bypasses the `select!` ‚Äî without it, lockstep-solo (quorum=1 + zero floor) would never observe a shutdown flip. **Config:** `VertexProducerConfig::quorum: usize` (production = `QUORUM = 85`; tests override to small values for sub-committee scenarios). `tick_interval` repurposed as a min-tick floor against lockstep-solo cascade runaway (default 50ms; was 250ms wall-clock pace). `ValidatorRunConfig::producer_quorum: Option<usize>` + `--producer-quorum` CLI flag ‚Äî solo/devnet runs pass `Some(1)`, 2-validator devnet uses `Some(2)`, production mainnet uses `None` (= QUORUM = 85). Existing validator tests set `producer_quorum: Some(1)` so solo cascades still advance past genesis. **3 new producer tests pin the contract:** (1) `solo_quorum_one_advances_after_each_insert` ‚Äî quorum=1 cascade fires ‚â•5 rounds in 50ms (proves the notify‚Üítick‚Üínotify cascade works); (2) `high_quorum_blocks_until_peers_insert_parents` ‚Äî quorum=3 stalls at genesis until 2 peer round-0 vertices land, then producer wakes via notify + fires round 1 (proves the notify-driven trigger works for multi-validator); (3) `high_quorum_no_peers_produces_only_genesis` ‚Äî quorum=85 + no peers ever arrive ‚Üí exactly 1 vertex (genesis) produced (proves the quorum gate is real). 12 producer + 933 workspace tests green; all 4 CI gates clean. ‚Äî PR [#149](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/149)

- [x] **wasm-exec: drop `pyde::panic` ‚Äî last legacy alias before otigen's canonical 28-fn surface** ‚Äî final cleanup of the otigen-engine host fn alignment kicked off by #151. `pyde::panic` was a Œ≤.4 PR-4-era plumbing scaffold registered before `pyde::revert` shipped in `host_fns/halt.rs`. The two had identical shape (`(reason_ptr: i32, reason_len: i32) -> !`) and identical semantics (halt + surface a reason string as a trap); the panic-fn body was always a placeholder that returned `Err(wasmtime::Error::msg("contract panic at ptr=X len=Y"))` and never even read the reason bytes from linear memory (real reason-decode landed in `revert`). otigen's canonical `CORE_HOST_FNS` allowlist has `revert` but NOT `panic` ‚Üí engine drifted at 29 fns instead of the spec's 28. Same class of fix as the `block_height` drop in #151. **Benign drift** (otigen-built contracts wouldn't import `pyde::panic` because otigen's deploy validator would reject it as out-of-allowlist), but worth cleaning up so the engine linker matches the spec exactly. **Changes:** (1) deleted `crates/wasm-exec/src/host_fns/panic.rs` (86 lines + 2 internal `register_panic_*` tests); (2) removed `host_fns::register_panic(&mut linker)?;` from `crates/wasm-exec/src/linker.rs::build_linker`; (3) removed `pub mod panic;` + `pub use panic::register_panic;` from `crates/wasm-exec/src/host_fns/mod.rs`; (4) deleted test `execute_call_surfaces_pyde_panic_host_fn_call_as_trap` in `crates/wasm-exec/src/executor.rs` (the PR-4-era plumbing test that imported `(import "pyde" "panic" ...)` from a WAT contract ‚Äî semantically replaced by the `revert`-based traps in halt.rs's tests); (5) updated doc comments in `error.rs` (`pyde::panic` ‚Üí `pyde::revert`), `executor.rs` (two sites: trap-source comment + execute_call's contract-trap list), `host_fns/mod.rs` (replaced "PR-4 ships only panic..." paragraph with "current registered surface: 28 canonical core host fns per HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß7"), `linker.rs` (build_linker docstring now references the canonical 28-fn surface), and `lib.rs` (retired-PR-4-scaffold note explaining the history). **Verification:** `grep -B 0 -A 2 '"pyde"' crates/wasm-exec/src/host_fns/*.rs | grep -oE '"[a-z_]+"' | sort -u | wc -l` ‚Üí 28 (was 29). Final 28-fn list matches otigen's `CORE_HOST_FNS` 1:1 ‚Äî storage 3 (sload/sstore/sdelete) + account 2 (balance/transfer) + context 6 (caller/origin/self_address/wave_id/wave_timestamp/chain_id) + tx 5 (tx_hash/tx_value/tx_gas_remaining/calldata_size/calldata_copy) + events 1 (emit_event) + hashing 3 (hash_blake3/hash_poseidon2/hash_keccak256) + PQ crypto 1 (falcon_verify) + cross-call 3 (cross_call/cross_call_static/delegate_call) + halt 2 (return/revert) + gas 1 (consume_gas) + beacon 1 (beacon_get). - [x] **Wave-committer ‚Üî DevnetState wiring: production validator executes committed waves end-to-end** ‚Äî Œ≥.mc2 task #144 sub-PR 2/2 (closes #144 entirely). Closes the Œ≥‚ÜîŒ≤ trait handshake started in #144 sub-PR 1/2 (engine #148, landed via the integration merge #150). The production `pyde validator` binary's wave-committer now invokes a real state executor on every commit ‚Äî resolving walked vertices ‚Üí txs end-to-end via the shared `BatchCache` + `ConsensusStore.txs_cf` ‚Äî instead of constructing empty placeholder `WaveCommitInputs`. This is the **v1-spike-level integration**: `DevnetState` (Œ≤'s MC-2.1 work, inherited via the integration merge) runs the actual transfer/fee/nonce logic. When Œ≤'s wasm-exec orchestrator (`StateStore` production impl) ships post-MC-2, the wiring swap is a one-line change in `ValidatorRuntime` (replace the `Arc<DevnetState>` construction with the real `Arc<StateStore>` once it implements `commit_walked_subdag` or the production-shaped equivalent). **Per persistent memory `wasm_exec_atomic_relaxed_assumes_single_threaded`**: this is safe because the wave-committer's tick remains single-threaded per Mysticeti spec (one wave at a time); a Œ≥-side integrator who parallelizes per-tx execution within a wave MUST add an outer mutex around state access. **Changes:** `crates/node/src/devnet/state.rs` ‚Äî `DevnetState` gains two optional fields (`batch_cache: Option<Arc<BatchCache>>` + `consensus_store: Option<Arc<ConsensusStore>>`) plus paired constructor `new_with_caches(fee_config, batch_cache, consensus_store)`; existing `new(fee_config)` keeps Option as `None` (preserves devnet composer + existing-test behavior). New inherent method `commit_walked_subdag(wave_id, walked_vertices: &[Arc<Vertex>]) -> Result<WaveCommitInputs, InterfaceError>`: returns `NotImplemented` if caches aren't wired (composer path stays as-is ‚Äî pre-resolves via `commit_wave_with_resolved_txs`); otherwise for each vertex iterates `batch_refs` ‚Üí looks up bytes in `BatchCache` ‚Üí borsh-decodes the `Batch` ‚Üí walks `batch.tx_hashes` ‚Üí looks up each `Tx` in `consensus_store.txs_cf` ‚Üí delegates the resolved `Vec<Tx>` to the existing `commit_wave_with_resolved_txs`. Missing batches (gossip race), missing txs (txs_cf miss), and borsh decode failures are skipped silently + logged at `warn` ‚Äî the wave commits what's resolvable, matching the network's eventual-consistency model. `crates/node/src/runtime.rs` ‚Äî `ValidatorRuntime` gains `state: Arc<DevnetState>` constructed via `new_with_caches` with the runtime's shared `BatchCache` + `ConsensusStore`. `crates/node/src/wave_committer.rs` ‚Äî `WaveCommitter` gains `state: Arc<DevnetState>` (12-arg ctor; existing arg order preserved). `for_test` default state constructs via `DevnetState::new` (no caches ‚Üí NotImplemented fallback exercised by existing tests, preserving pre-#144 behavior). `commit_one_wave_with_anchor` swaps the placeholder `WaveCommitInputs` construction for `state.commit_walked_subdag(wave_id, &walked)`: on `Ok(inputs)` use the state's execution-derived fields (state_root, events_root, events_bloom, events_count, gas_used, included_txs), then patch composer-owned consensus-side fields on top (prior_anchor_round, epoch, next_epoch_beacon); on `Err(NotImplemented)` fall back to empty inputs (legacy path); on `Err(Storage|Internal)` log + fall back to empty inputs (the wave still commits ‚Äî lossy but doesn't halt the chain). `crates/node/src/validator.rs` ‚Äî production validator threads `runtime.state.clone()` into the wave-committer ctor. **4 new resolution tests in `devnet/state.rs` pin the contract:** (1) `commit_walked_subdag_returns_not_implemented_when_caches_missing` ‚Äî unwired state ‚Üí NotImplemented (proves composer path stays valid); (2) `commit_walked_subdag_resolves_batches_and_executes_txs_end_to_end` ‚Äî pre-loaded batch (in BatchCache) + tx (in txs_cf) ‚Üí resolved + executed ‚Üí non-EMPTY state_root, gas_used == 21000, included_txs == [tx_hash] (proves the full resolution chain works); (3) `commit_walked_subdag_skips_missing_batch_in_cache` ‚Äî vertex refs unknown batch hash ‚Üí skipped silently, wave commits empty (proves graceful degradation under gossip races); (4) `commit_walked_subdag_skips_tx_missing_from_consensus_store` ‚Äî batch resolves but tx hash absent from txs_cf ‚Üí skipped silently (proves txs_cf miss handling). 1600 workspace tests passing (was 1596; +4 new). All 4 CI gates green. **Out of scope (next slice):** the production producer doesn't yet fill vertex `batch_refs` (mempool drain ‚Üí Batch construction ‚Üí BatchCache put ‚Üí vertex batch_refs). Until that lands, live `pyde validator` runs still produce empty waves on the wire ‚Äî but the spine is now wired + testable, and the moment producer-side ships, real state changes flow end-to-end without further wave-committer changes. ‚Äî PR [#153](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/153)
- [x] **Producer ‚Üî mempool ‚Üî batch wiring: live waves now carry real txs** ‚Äî Œ≥.5.producer-wiring. Closes the "next slice" callout from #153 (engine roadmap line 332): the production `VertexProducer` now drains the live `PydeMempoolView` into a `Batch` on every tick, persists each tx to `consensus_store.txs_cf` keyed by canonical `pyde_engine_tx::tx_hash` (the spec-correct Poseidon2-based hash per Ch 11 ¬ß11.6), borsh-encodes the `Batch` and caches it under `batch_hash = blake3(borsh(tx_hashes) ++ borsh(encryption_metadata))` in the shared `BatchCache`, and embeds `[batch_hash]` in the vertex's `batch_refs`. Empty mempool ‚Üí empty `batch_refs` (round still advances). The resolution chain wired in #153 (`DevnetState::commit_walked_subdag` ‚Üí `BatchCache.get` ‚Üí `borsh::from_slice<Batch>` ‚Üí `batch.tx_hashes` ‚Üí `consensus_store.get_tx`) now sees real batches end-to-end. **Mainloop side**: gossiped txs (already persisted to `txs_cf` per Œ≥.5.mempool-persistence) now ALSO admit into `PydeMempoolView::insert` via a fire-and-forget `tokio::spawn`, mirroring the state-root-sig + beacon-share emit pattern from #138. This runs the full validation pipeline (FALCON sig + balance + nonce window + chain_id + structural per PR [#129](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/129)) before the tx becomes drainable. `ValidatorRuntime` constructs the mempool over the same `Arc<DevnetState>` used as `StateView` so balance/nonce/auth-keys lookups stay coherent. **`BatchPipeline` design**: optional wiring attached via `VertexProducer::with_batch_pipeline(...)` so the producer remains usable in tests / solo bring-up without dragging in mempool + RocksDB. The `mempool` field is typed `Arc<dyn MempoolView>` so unit tests use the no-validation `MockMempool` while production wires the same concrete `PydeMempoolView` the mainloop admits txs into. Per-tick budget on serialized-tx bytes defaults to `BATCH_MAX_BYTES = 4 MB` per Mysticeti Ch 6 ¬ß2. Tx-persist failures (txs_cf put error) degrade gracefully ‚Äî log + drop the affected tx; the wave-committer's existing `consensus_store.get_tx(...) ‚Üí None` branch handles the resulting batch_ref ‚Üí tx miss without aborting the wave. **3 new producer tests**: (1) `assemble_batch_refs_empty_mempool_returns_empty` ‚Äî empty drain ‚Üí empty refs (proves the no-tx path stays clean); (2) `assemble_batch_refs_persists_txs_caches_batch_and_returns_hash` ‚Äî admit-drain-persist-cache cycle yields a `Batch` decodable from `BatchCache` with `tx_hashes = [h]` + `encryption_metadata = None`, and the tx is recoverable from `consensus_store.get_tx(&h)` (proves the full resolution chain); (3) `run_with_pipeline_emits_vertex_with_batch_refs` ‚Äî live run with one admitted tx publishes a first vertex with one `batch_ref` then empty-`batch_refs` vertices after (proves the producer emits real waves on the wire). **3 new metrics**: `producer_batches_assembled` (non-empty batches emitted), `producer_txs_packed` (cumulative txs across batches), `producer_tx_persist_failures` (drained txs that failed `put_tx`; degrades gracefully). 1603 workspace tests passing (was 1600; +3 new). All 4 CI gates green. **Out of scope (next slice)**: priority-fee tx ordering (HARD-excluded per memory `hard_excluded_v1_features`); the per-batch encryption envelope (`encryption_metadata`) ‚Äî v1 ships plaintext-only, threshold-decryption ceremony comes with the DKG production rollout (Œ≥.15 PR-4). ‚Äî PR [#154](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/154)
- [x] **wasm-exec: align `caller` / `origin` / `self_address` to HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß7.3 `-> i32`** ‚Äî surfaced by otigen Phase 1 integration brief A1. The three address-shaped context fns were registered as `(i32) -> ()`; per HOST_FN_ABI_SPEC ¬ß7.3 (frozen at v1 mainnet per memory `host-fn-abi-spec-locked.md`) each returns `i32` (always `0` for success). The mismatch caused every otigen-built contract to fail at instantiate-time with `incompatible import type for pyde::self_address`. Each closure now returns `Ok(0)` after the existing memory write; module-level doc + four inline WAT test fixtures pick up `(result i32)` + a trailing `drop`. Unblocks `engine_runner::tests::counter_rust_increments_via_real_engine_wasm_exec` which was `#[ignore]`'d pending this alignment. Surfaced via the otigen-test integration that consumes engine's `build_linker` directly ‚Äî Phase 1's whole point being "consume engine wasm-exec so spec drift surfaces at integration, not at mainnet". ‚Äî PR [#167](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/167)
- [x] **wasm-exec: bump wasmtime 26 ‚Üí 36 (+ matching wasmparser 0.236)** ‚Äî surfaced by otigen Phase 1 integration brief A2: otigen had to downgrade to wasmtime 26 to consume engine's `build_linker` directly. Engine workspace now on `wasmtime = "36"` + `wasmparser = "0.236"`. Production binary now carries one wasmparser (was two during the bump window). Migration: `Config::static_memory_maximum_size` renamed to `Config::memory_reservation` (wasmtime 36 unified static/dynamic memory configuration; same per-slot virtual-reservation cap semantic ‚Äî still caps the pool's per-instance max at `POOL_MAX_MEMORY_SIZE` so the kernel doesn't reject the mmap). Pool allocator API (`total_core_instances`, `total_memories`, `total_tables`, `max_memory_size`, `linear_memory_keep_resident`, `table_keep_resident`) unchanged. Determinism config ‚Äî NaN canonicalization, fuel metering, parallel compilation, COW memory init, pooling allocator ‚Äî all preserved. otigen reverts the downgrade in step. ‚Äî PR [#168](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/168)
- [x] **wasm-exec: `pyde.abi` selector dispatch + attribute pre-checks** ‚Äî implements HOST_FN_ABI ¬ß3.5.2 per-call dispatch flow end-to-end. Engine moves from "void-void single entry-point" demo shape to canonical spec contract dispatch. New `WasmExecutor::execute_contract_call` is the canonical Standard tx entry point: looks up the cached `ContractAbi`, resolves the entry point via `dispatch.rs::resolve` (selector ‚Üí fallback ‚Üí receive ‚Üí `ERR_INVALID_FUNCTION_NAME`), applies attribute pre-checks before invoking the WASM body ‚Äî `CONSTRUCTOR` post-deploy lockout ‚Üí `ERR_CONSTRUCTOR_LOCKOUT`; `PAYABLE` missing on non-zero `tx.value` ‚Üí `ERR_VALUE_TRANSFER_NOT_PAYABLE`; `VIEW` ‚Üí flips `HostContext::view_mode = true` so mutating host fns (`sstore`, `sdelete`, `transfer`, `emit_event`) trap with `ERR_FORBIDDEN` per ¬ß3.7 Layer 3 enforcement. New `dispatch.rs` module hosts the pure resolution logic (10 unit tests covering every branch). `ModuleCache` extended per ¬ß3.6 to store the parsed `ContractAbi` alongside the compiled module ‚Äî `compile_and_cache` attempts `extract_pyde_abi` after validation; success stores `Some(Arc<ContractAbi>)`, failure stores `None` (graceful for raw-WASM legacy fixtures). New `ModuleCache::get_with_abi` returns `(Module, Arc<ContractAbi>)` for the dispatch path; new `ExecutorError::AbiMissing` is the graceful-signal variant for raw-WASM fixtures that should keep using the un-dispatched `execute_call` path. 22 new tests (10 dispatch resolution unit + 11 executor-level dispatch integration + 1 end-to-end view-mode runtime enforcement where a `VIEW` fn calling `sstore` traps with the forbidden error). All 201 pre-existing wasm-exec tests remain green via the un-dispatched `execute_call` path. Unblocks otigen Phase 3 multi-entry contracts dispatched by selector + attribute-enforced at runtime. Surfaced by otigen Phase 1 integration brief A5. ‚Äî PR [#171](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/171)
- [x] Mysticeti 3-stage support check (`check_anchor_support`: supporters at R+1 + certifiers at R+2; Committed / Pending / Skipped ‚Äî Skipped prevents stall on bad proposer) ‚Äî PR [#5](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/5)
- [x] BFS subdag walk + canonical sort (`walk_subdag`: BFS over parent_vertex_refs, skips already-committed, canonical (round, member_id, hash) order ‚Äî wire-load-bearing) ‚Äî PR [#7](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/7)

- [x] Equivocation detection + evidence collection ‚Üí Œ≥.4 Slashing ‚Äî `VertexStore::insert` already detected equivocations and returned `InsertOutcome::Equivocation { prior_at_slot }`; this PR adds the event-channel side. New `EquivocationDetected` struct (member_id, round, new_hash, full new_vertex cloned in, prior_at_slot insertion-order list) emitted via an optional `tokio::sync::mpsc::UnboundedSender` attached through `set_equivocation_sink` / `clear_equivocation_sink`. Default = no sink (existing callers unaffected). Receiver-drop is silently swallowed ‚Äî equivocation is *stored* regardless; only the notification is lost. Completes the consensus-side half of the loop opened by Œ≥.5.equivocation (the node-side `EquivocationDetector::handle_equivocation` is already wired); a follow-up PR adds the main-loop drain task once a verifier + DKG + epoch + stake oracle is available. ‚Äî PR [#85](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/85)

- [x] Layered peer discovery ‚Äî **mDNS LAN layer shipped (dev-only)**: libp2p `mdns` feature + `mdns::tokio::Behaviour` composed into `PydeBehaviour.mdns: Toggle<_>` (Toggle keeps the behaviour opt-in without forking the swarm builder). `enable_mdns: bool` threaded through `Network::new` ‚Üí `NetworkRunner::from_keypair` ‚Üí `ValidatorRuntimeConfig` ‚Üí `ValidatorRunConfig` ‚Üí CLI; surfaced as `pyde validator --enable-mdns` (default off ‚Äî mDNS broadcasts validator presence to the LAN and is unsafe on a public node). - [x] **Typed `NewListenAddr` event (closes test-flake)** ‚Äî Œ≥.net.NewListenAddr: replace the string-parser in `two_networks_exchange_gossipsub_message` with a typed `NetworkEvent::NewListenAddr { addr: Multiaddr }` variant. The prior test regex-matched `SwarmEvent::NewListenAddr`'s `Debug` repr, so it broke whenever libp2p added or renamed inner fields (`listener_id`, `address`, ...); the typed variant is structural ‚Äî no parsing. **Side benefit:** the typed event is the exact surface a future multi-validator integration harness needs for port discovery (bind `/tcp/0`, drain events until `NewListenAddr` fires, hand the resolved `Multiaddr` to the peer's `--dial` config ‚Äî same pattern the soak-test + chaos-test infrastructure will lean on per memory `performance_harness`). **Changes:** new `NetworkEvent::NewListenAddr` variant; `Network::handle_event` intercepts `SwarmEvent::NewListenAddr` explicitly instead of falling through to the `Debug`-formatted `Other` variant; mainloop dispatch funnels the new variant into the existing `passthrough_events` metric (validators never need to handle their own listen addrs at the consensus layer); `two_networks_exchange_gossipsub_message` rewritten to use the typed variant + **`#[ignore]` removed** (it was only ignored because the parser was flaky, not because it was slow) ‚Äî now runs in CI; new `new_listen_addr_event_carries_resolved_address` test pins the typed surface (`/ip4/127.0.0.1/tcp/<NON-ZERO>`). 1650 workspace tests passing (was 1648; +2: the un-ignored test runs now + the new pin). All 4 CI gates green. ‚Äî PR [#158](https://github.com/pyde-net/engine/pull/158)
